#1 Electric eels (電鳗) #060001 原文
中文翻譯

1807年，19世紀探險家亞歷山大·馮·洪堡在亞馬遜河的一次實地考察中，目睹了一群馬被牽過一個滿是電鰻的泥濘水池，他描述電鰻戲劇性地躍出水面攻擊入侵者。但科學家們對這個故事持懷疑態度。

一幅描繪亞歷山大·馮·洪堡所述馬與電鰻之戰的插圖。

「第一次讀到馮·洪堡的故事時，我覺得完全匪夷所思，」卡塔尼亞說。「電鰻為什麼要攻擊馬，而不是游走逃開？」但後來他在實驗室裡用金屬邊框網將電鰻從一個水槽轉移到另一個水槽時，意外觀察到了相同的行為。較大的電鰻非但沒有游走，反而躍出水面攻擊網子。

卡塔尼亞將電壓計連接到鋁板上，或將導電金屬條接到「掠食者」模型物體（例如鱷魚頭部複製品）上，藉此追蹤電鰻放電的強度。

潛伏水中的電鰻透過水傳導的電擊，到達目標時相對較弱。但當電鰻用其會發電的下巴直接接觸目標時，電流會直接傳入目標體內，必須穿過目標的身體才能回到水中，卡塔尼亞在《美國國家科學院院刊》中報告了這一發現。

「這使得電鰻能夠對侵入其領地、半身露出水面的陸地動物施以最大功率的電擊，」卡塔尼亞解釋道。「這也讓牠們能夠電擊入侵者更大範圍的身體部位。」

卡塔尼亞發現，當水族箱中的水位較低時，電鰻更頻繁地選擇躍起攻擊，而非退縮。他認為，這種攻擊行為讓電鰻在亞馬遜旱季能更好地保護自己——旱季時牠們被困在狹小的水池中，極易成為獵物。

英文原文

On a field trip to the Amazon in 1807, 19th-century explorer Alexander von Humboldt witnessed a group of horses lead through a muddy pool filled with electric eels , which he described as dramatically leaping up to attack the intruders. But scientists have doubted the story . An illustration of Alexander von Humboldt's story of the battle between the horses and electric eels. "The first time I read von Humboldt's tale, I thought it was completely bizarre," Catania says. "Why would the eels attack the horses instead of swimming away?" But then he observed the same behavior by accident as he transferred the eels in his lab from one tank to another using a metal-rimmed net. Instead of swimming away, larger eels attacked the net by leaping out of the water. Catania tracked the strength of the eels’ electric shock by attaching a voltmeter to an aluminum plate, or conductive metal strips to "predator" objects such as a crocodile head replica. The zap a submerged eel distributes through the water is relatively weak when it reaches the target. But when an eel touches it with its electricity-generating chin, the current travels directly to the target and has to travel through its body before it gets back to the water , Catania reported in Proceedings of the National Academy of Sciences. "This allows the eels to deliver shocks with a maximum amount of power to partially submerged land animals that invade their territory," Catania explains. "It also allows them to electrify a much larger portion of the invader's body." Catania found the eels leapt to attack, rather than receded , more often when the water in the aquarium was lower. He argues the attack lets electric eels better defend themselves during the Amazonian dry season, when they’re cornered in small pools and make easy prey.

#2 Double blind (雙盲測試法) #060002 原文
中文翻譯

「雙盲」的特點在於患者與醫師都不知道誰接受了實驗性治療，這幾乎被一致推崇為臨床試驗的一大優點。因此，未能成功維持雙盲狀態的試驗，被視為所提供的證據支持較為薄弱。這一觀點的理據無可厚非：雙盲設計排除了患者與醫師信念可能造成的混淆影響。

然而，將雙盲試驗視為必然優越的做法是有問題的。首先，這會導致一個悖論：非常有效的實驗性治療反而無法獲得最佳證據的支持。若某種新藥能在數秒內消除普通感冒最嚴重的症狀，大多數參與者和研究人員都能正確辨識出它是最新的神奇藥物，而非對照組（即安慰劑）的治療效果。

因此，任何測試這種神奇藥物效果的試驗都將無法維持雙盲狀態。對於運動和大多數外科手術技術等治療方式，也會出現類似的問題，因為其本質使其難以在雙盲條件下進行測試。

一套關於證據的理論，竟先驗地斷定某些主張永遠無法獲得「最佳證據」的支持，這似乎相當奇怪。若爭議中的主張屬於偽科學——即無法被檢驗的——那又另當別論。但就具有顯著效果的治療而言，其有效性的主張是高度可檢驗的，直覺上，它們從證據中所獲得的支持，理應強於那些效果僅屬中等的治療主張。

英文原文

The feature of being "double blind", where neither patients nor physicians are aware of who receives the experimental treatment, is almost universally trumpeted as being a virtue of clinical trials . Hence, trials that fail to remain successfully double blind are regarded as providing inferior evidential support. The rationale for this view is unobjectionable: double blinding rules out the potential confounding influences of patient and physician beliefs . Nonetheless, viewing double blind trial as necessarily superior is problematic . For one, it leads to the paradox that very effective experimental treatments will not be supportable by best evidence . If a new drug were to make even the most severe symptoms of the common cold disappear within seconds, most participants and investigators would correctly identify it as the latest wonder drug and not the control (i·e· placebo) treatment. Any trial testing the effectiveness of this wonder drug will therefore fail to remain double blind. Similar problems arise for treatments , such as exercise and most surgical techniques, whose nature makes them resistant to being tested in double blind conditions. It seems strange that an account of evidence should make priori judgments that certain claims can never be supported by ‘best evidence’. It would be different if the claims at issue were pseudoscientific – untestable. But so far as treatments with large effects go, the claim that they are effective is highly testable and intuitively they should receive greater support from the evidence than do claims about treatments with moderate effects.

#3 Australian Education (澳洲教育) #060003 原文
中文翻譯

當澳洲人就教育品質或教育公平展開辯論時，他們似乎常常預設一個國家無法同時兼顧兩者。
原本旨在提升教育公平的課程改革，往往事與願違，因為這些改革以增加課程廣度或差異化選項的方式，反而擴大了品質上的落差。更進一步，這些品質差異往往反映了學生社會背景的差異，因為「新增」的課程選項通常由相對弱勢的學生選修，而這些學生並未因此獲得良好的服務。以下將以新南威爾斯州的實證資料來說明這一點。

提升教育品質的必要性，在經合組織成員國及其他國家中已獲廣泛認同，因為各國都致力於強化人力資本，以支撐其現代知識經濟。提升教育公平對於同一目標同樣至關重要，因為對高階技能的需求十分普遍，而低技能者的機會則日益萎縮。

提升教育公平對於社會凝聚力同樣不可或缺。在某些國家，教育體系似乎主要在於複製既有的社會結構——讓原本就享有特權者繼續享有特權，讓原本就被剝奪者繼續被剝奪。即便在情況不那麼極端的國家，學校教育建構社會凝聚力的能力，也往往因為學校將個人與群體加以區隔的方式而受到削弱。

英文原文

When Australians engage in debate about educational quality or equity, they often seem to accept that a country cannot achieve both at the same time . Curriculum reforms intended to improve equity often fail to do so because they increase breadth or differentiation in offerings in a way that increases differences in quality. Further, these differences in quality often reflect differences in students’ social backgrounds because the ‘new’ offerings are typically taken up by relatively disadvantaged students who are not served well them. Evidence from New South Wales will be used to illustrate this point. The need to improve the quality of education is well accepted across OECD and other countries as they seek to strengthen their human capital to underpin their modern, knowledge economies. Improved equity is also important for this purpose, since the demand for high level skills is widespread and the opportunities for the low skilled are diminishing. Improved equity in education is also important for social cohesion . There are countries in which the education system seems primarily to reproduce existing social arrangements, conferring privilege where it already exists and denying it where it does not. Even in countries where the diagnosis might be less extreme, the capacity of schooling to build social cohesion is often diminished by the way in which schools separate individuals and groups.

#4 Travel (旅遊業) #060004 原文
中文翻譯

旅遊業所創造的就業機會遍及整體經濟，涵蓋零售、建築、製造與電信等各個領域，以及旅遊業相關企業的直接雇用。這些工作崗位吸納了大量女性、少數族裔與年輕人；以中小型企業為主要雇主；並提供良好的職業培訓與流動性。旅遊業也是推動區域經濟發展的最有效引擎之一。這些特點在已開發國家與新興經濟體中同樣適用。

旅遊業作為環境保護與改善、維護在地多元性與文化的催化劑，已有許多成功的實例。旅遊業創造就業機會與財富，在推動已開發國家及新興國家實現經濟、環境與社會可持續發展方面具有巨大潛力。與許多其他產業形式相比，旅遊業的啟動成本與運營成本相對較低，因而具備比較優勢。

在許多地區，旅遊業也往往是少數切實可行的發展選項之一。因此，旅遊業在全球範圍內於短期至中期內持續增長的可能性極高。

英文原文

Jobs generated by Travel & Tourism are spread across the economy in retail, construction, manufacturing and telecommunications, as well as directly in Travel & Tourism companies. These jobs employ a large proportion of women, minorities and young people; are predominantly in small and medium sized companies; and offer good training and transferability. Tourism can also be one of the most effective drivers for the development of regional economies . These patterns apply to both developed and emerging economies. There are numerous good examples of where Travel & Tourism is acting as a catalyst for conservation and improvement of the environment and maintenance of local diversity and culture . Travel & Tourism creates jobs and wealth and has tremendous potential to contribute to economically, environmentally and socially sustainable development in both developed countries and emerging nations. It has a comparative advantage in that its start up and running costs can be low compared to many other forms of industry development. It is also often one of the few realistic options for development in many areas. Therefore, there is a strong likelihood that the Travel & Tourism industry will continue to grow globally over the short to medium term .

#5 Twins (雙胞胎) #060005 原文
中文翻譯

UCLA 神經學教授 Paul Thompson 與其同事掃描了 23 對同卵雙胞胎
與 23 對異卵雙胞胎的大腦。由於同卵雙胞胎擁有相同的基因，而異卵雙胞胎
僅共享約一半的基因，研究人員因此能夠比較兩組數據，證明髓鞘的完整性
在大腦中許多與智力密切相關的區域是由基因決定的。這些區域包括頂葉——負責空間推理、視覺處理與邏輯思維——以及胼胝體，負責整合來自身體兩側的信息。

研究人員使用了一種名為 HARDI（高角度解析度擴散成像）的掃描儀的更快版本——可以把它想像成加強版的 MRI 機器——能以遠高於標準 MRI 的解析度掃描大腦。標準 MRI 掃描透過測量水分含量來顯示大腦中不同組織的體積，而 HARDI 則追蹤水分在大腦
白質中的擴散方式——藉此衡量髓鞘的品質。

「HARDI 測量的是水分的擴散情況，」Thompson 說道，他同時也是 UCLA 神經影像實驗室的成員。「如果水分沿特定方向迅速擴散，就說明大腦具有非常
快速的連結。若擴散範圍較廣，則表示信號傳遞較慢，智力也相對較低。」

英文原文

UCLA neurology professor Paul Thompson and his colleagues scanned the brains of 23 sets of identical twins and 23 sets of fraternal twins . Since identical twins share the same genes while fraternal twins share about half their genes, the researchers were able to compare each group to show that myelin integrity was determined genetically in many parts of the brain that are key for intelligence . These include the parietal lobes, which are responsible for spatial reasoning, visual processing and logic, and the corpus callosum, which pulls together information from both sides of the body. The researchers used a faster version of a type of scanner called a HARDI (high-angular resolution diffusion imaging) — think of an MRI machine on steroids — that takes scans of the brain at a much higher resolution than a standard MRI. While an MRI scan shows the volume of different tissues in the brain by measuring the amount of water present, HARDI tracks how water diffuses through the brain's white matter — a way to measure the quality of its myelin . "HARDI measures water diffusion," said Thompson, who is also a member of the UCLA Laboratory of Neuro-Imaging. "If the water diffuses rapidly in a specific direction, it tells us that the brain has very fast connections. If it diffuses more broadly, that's an indication of slower signaling, and lower intelligence."

#原文

Since identical twins share the same genes while fraternal twins share about half their genes, the researchers were able to compare each group to show that myelin integrity was determined genetically in many parts of the brain that are key for intelligence . These
2The researchers used a faster version of a type of scanner called a HARDI (high-angular resolution
3brain by measuring the amount of water present, HARDI tracks how water diffuses through the brain's white matter — a way to measure the quality of its myelin . #6 Technology course (科技課程) #060006 大意

每門課程都有特定的課綱，明確列出所需的特定技術。
有些教師懂得如何融入科技，有些則不然。
將會有講師協助職前教師學習如何將科技與課堂經驗相結合，並鼓勵職前教師思考科技融入的方式，使他們得以隨時隨地在線上學習。

#7 Mammal (哺乳動物) #060007 原文
中文翻譯

哺乳動物可能是棲地喪失中受創最嚴重的族群之一，目前已有大量研究致力於尋找保護哺乳動物多樣性的最佳方法。
許多研究聚焦於大規模的土地利用變遷，以及這些變遷對整體哺乳動物多樣性所帶來的影響。然而，許多重要的土地利用決策卻是在更地方性的層級上制定的，例如個別土地所有者的層級。
如今，一項由帝國理工學院倫敦分校主導、針對婆羅洲不同小規模地景中哺乳動物多樣性所進行的詳細研究，讓研究人員發現了一個過去被忽視的哺乳動物避難所來源——曾經遭受伐木的森林。
這些「選擇性伐木」森林僅移除特定樹種，通常被視為已退化的土地，且經常被清除以騰出空間供種植園使用。這項發表於《生態應用》期刊的新研究結果顯示，這些森林應獲得更好的保護。
研究團隊採用誘捕放回技術與動態感應相機，歷時三年記錄哺乳動物，在三種土地利用類型中建立了前所未有的兩萬筆物種紀錄，涵蓋原始森林、伐木森林與油棕種植園。這是迄今為止針對雨林哺乳動物多樣性所進行的最密集研究之一。
令研究人員感到意外的是，他們發現雲豹、靈貓等大型哺乳動物的多樣性，在原始森林與伐木森林中相近。至於松鼠、囓齒類等小型哺乳動物，其多樣性在伐木森林中實際上更高。

英文原文

Mammals can be one of the hardest-hit groups by habitat loss , and a lot of research has been carried out to find the best ways to conserve mammal diversity. Much of this research has focused on very large-scale changes in land use and the impacts this will have on overall mammal diversity. However, many important decisions about land use are made at much more local scales, for example at the level of individual landowners. Now, in a detailed study led by Imperial College London that looked at mammal diversity across different small-scale landscapes in Borneo, researchers have identified previously logged forests as an overlooked source of refuge for mammals . These ‘selectively logged’ forests, where only certain tree species are removed, are often considered to be degraded and are frequently cleared to make way for plantations. The new results, published in the journal Ecological Applications, suggest they should be better protected . The team recorded mammals using trap-and-release techniques and motion-sensing cameras over three years, creating an unprecedented 20,000 records of species in three land-use types: old-growth forest, logged forest and oil palm plantation. This is one of the most intensive studies of rainforest mammal diversity ever undertaken . To their surprise, they found that mammal diversity for large mammals , like the clouded leopard and civets, was similar for both old-growth forests and logged forests. For small mammals , such as squirrels and rodents, the diversity was actually higher in logged forests .

2Now, in a detailed study led by Imperial College London that looked at mammal diversity across different small-scale landscapes in Borneo, researchers have identified previously logged forests as an overlooked source of refuge for mammals .
3the journal Ecological Applications, suggest they should be better protected .
4forest, logged forest and oil palm plantation. This is one of the most intensive studies of rainforest mammal diversity ever undertaken . To their surprise, they found that mammal diversity for large mammals , like the clouded leopard and civets, was similar for both old-growth forests and logged forests. For small mammals , such as squirrels and rodents, the diversity was actually higher in logged forests .

#9 Plug-in vehicle (電動汽車) #060009 原文
中文翻譯

這裡有一個你將會越來越常聽到的詞：插電式車輛，縮寫為 PEV。這就是
你和許多其他人在未來十年及以後上班時所駕駛的交通工具。
到那個時候，在你早上出門前，你首先要拔掉車子的充電插頭——你的插電式車輛。它的
大容量車載電池將已在夜間完全充滿電，儲有足夠的電力讓你在市區交通中行駛
50 至 100 公里。

當你抵達公司，你會再次為車子插上電，這次插入的插座能讓電力從你車子的電池流向電網。你在購車時所做的事情之一，就是與你屬意的電力供應商簽訂合約，允許他們在有需要時從你的車輛電池中抽取有限的電量——例如發生停電，或批發即時電價極高的情況。電力分銷商向你購買車輛電力所支付的價格，不僅對你而言極具吸引力，對他們來說也是一筆划算的交易，因為他們的替代方案是向調峰電廠購買極為昂貴的電力。

如果你在返家途中或因其他原因，電池電量看起來即將耗盡，一具相對小型、但安靜且高效的引擎便會自動啟動——它可以使用汽油、柴油、壓縮天然氣甚至生質燃料——驅動發電機為電池供電，讓你得以完成行程。

對「石油峰值」的憂慮、溫室氣體排放量的持續上升，以及本世紀中葉全球登記在冊的機動車輛數量可能達到現在五倍的可能性，
意味著全球對以石油為基礎的交通燃料幾近完全的依賴，在每一個
層面上都是不可持續的。

英文原文

Here's a term you're going to hear much more often: plug-in vehicle, and the acronym PEV . It's what you and many other people will drive to work in ten years and more from now . At that time, before you drive off in the morning you will first unplug your car - your plug-in vehicle. Its big on board batteries will have been fully charged overnight, with enough power for you to drive 50-100 kilometers through city traffic . When you arrive at work you'll plug in your car once again, this time into a socket that allows power to flow from your car's batteries to the electricity grid. One of the things you did when you bought your car was to sign a contract with your favorite electricity supplier, allowing them to draw a limited amount of power from your car's batteries should they need to, perhaps because of a blackout, or very high wholesale spot power prices. The price you get for the power the distributor buys from your car would not only be most attractive to you, it would be a good deal for them too, their alternative being very expensive power form peaking stations. If, driving home or for some other reason your batteries looked like running flat, a relatively small, but quiet and efficient engine running on petrol, diesel or compressed natural gas, even bio-fuel, would automatically cut in, driving a generator that supplied the batteries so you could complete your journey. Concerns over 'peak oil', increasing greenhouse gas emissions , and the likelihood that by the middle of this century there could be five times as many motor vehicles registered world-wide as there are now, mean that the world's almost total dependence on petroleum-based fuels for transport is, in every sense of the word, unsustainable .

#10 Dogs and humans (狗與人類) #060010 原文
中文翻譯

透過與人類的密切接觸，狗已發展出特定技能，使牠們能夠有效地與人互動
並進行溝通。
近期研究顯示，犬類大腦能夠捕捉人聲、體味與姿態中所蘊含的情緒線索，並解讀人類的臉部表情。在這項研究中，作者觀察了當他們將同兩位成人（一男一女）的臉部照片呈現給26隻正在進食的狗時所發生的情況。這些影像被刻意擺放在動物視線的兩側，照片中的人臉分別表現出六種基本人類情緒之一：憤怒、恐懼、快樂、悲傷、驚訝、厭惡，或保持中立表情。

當看到表達高度喚起情緒狀態（如憤怒、恐懼和快樂）的照片時，狗表現出更強烈的反應與心臟活動。牠們在看到這些影像後，也需要更長時間才會恢復進食。狗的心率加快表明，在這些情況下牠們經歷了較高程度的壓力。此外，當狗看到表達憤怒、恐懼或快樂的人臉時，會將頭轉向左側。而當人臉表現出驚訝時，情況則相反，這可能是因為狗將驚訝視為一種無威脅性的放鬆表情。因此，這些發現支持了犬類大腦在處理基本人類情緒時存在不對稱情緒調節機制的論點。

英文原文

By living in close contact with humans, dogs have developed specific skills that enable them to interact and communicate effectively with people . Recent studies have shown that the canine brain can pick up on emotional cues contained in a person's voice, body odor and posture, and read their faces . In this study, the authors observed what happened when they presented photographs of the same two adults' faces, a man and a woman, to 26 feeding dogs. The images were placed strategically to the sides of the animals' line of sight and the photos showed a human face expressing one of the six basic human emotions: anger, fear, happiness, sadness, surprise, disgust or being neutral. The dogs showed greater response and cardiac activity when shown photographs that expressed arousing emotional states such as anger, fear and happiness . They also took longer to resume feeding after seeing these images. The dogs' increased heart rate indicated that in these cases they experienced higher levels of stress. In addition, dogs turned their heads to the left when they saw human faces expressing anger, fear or happiness. The reverse happened when the faces looked surprised, possibly because dogs view it as a non-threatening, relaxed expression. These findings, therefore, support the existence of an asymmetrical emotional modulation of dogs' brains to process basic human emotions .

2The dogs showed greater response and cardiac activity when shown photographs that expressed arousing emotional states such as anger, fear and happiness . They also took longer to resume feeding
3surprised, possibly because dogs view it as a non-threatening, relaxed expression. These findings, therefore, support the existence of an asymmetrical emotional modulation of dogs' brains to process basic human emotions .
#11 Orbit debris (軌道碎片) #060011 原文
中文翻譯

數十年來，太空專家們一直擔心，某天一塊高速飛行的軌道碎片可能撞碎一艘大型太空船，將其化為數百個碎片，並引發連鎖反應——一場緩慢蔓延的碰撞瀑布，歷經數百年不斷擴展，在太空中散播混亂。

在過去約十年間，隨著科學家們逐漸達成共識，認為軌道上的物體數量已超過臨界質量——用他們的術語來說，即臨界空間密度，也就是連鎖反應變得不可避免的那個臨界點——他們的憂慮與日俱增。

今年初，經過半個世紀的增長，聯邦政府可偵測物體清單（四英寸寬或以上）已達10,000筆，其中包括失效衛星、廢棄火箭殘骸、一台相機、一件手工具，以及因偶發性爆炸和破壞性測試所遺留下來、不斷旋轉的碎片墳場。因此，我們價值數十億美元的衛星正面臨風險。

英文原文

For decades, space experts have worried that a speeding bit of orbital debris might one day smash a large spacecraft into hundreds of pieces and start a chain reaction , a slow cascade of collisions that would expand for centuries, spreading chaos through the heavens. In the last decade or so, as scientists came to agree that the number of objects in orbit had surpassed a critical mass — or, in their terms, the critical spatial density, the point at which a chain reaction becomes inevitable — they grew more anxious. Early this year, after a half-century of growth, the federal list of detectable objects (four inches wide or larger) reached 10,000, including dead satellites, spent rocket stages, a camera, a hand tool and junkyards of whirling debris left over from chance explosions and destructive tests. So our billion dollar of satellites are at risk .

2In the last decade or so, as scientists came to agree that the number of objects in orbit had surpassed a critical mass — or, in their terms, the critical spatial density, the point at which a chain reaction becomes inevitable — they grew more anxious.
3junkyards of whirling debris left over from chance explosions and destructive tests. So our billion dollar of satellites are at risk .
#12 Brundtland Report (布朗特蘭報告) #060012 原文
中文翻譯

布朗特蘭報告《我們共同的未來》（1987）將永續發展定義為：既能滿足當代人的需求，又不損害後代人滿足
其自身需求能力的發展。這個定義隱含了一個概念：過去的發展模式已無法
持續維持。

果真如此嗎？過去的發展是由成長與創新所驅動的。它催生了新技術，並大幅提升了生活水準。假設我們能預知未來世代的處境或需求，這種想法是錯誤的，且不可避免地會帶來一種令人沮喪的感覺——彷彿我們正在透支未來。

唯有假設社會將維持靜止不變，我們才能理解未來的需求。今日我們的生活方式，在二十年前是無法預測的。永續性典範未能
認識到這一點。它是一種靜態的觀點，因而限制了人類的創造力與智慧。

同樣地，大量錯誤的假設主導著環境思維：問題的規模被誇大，資源的數量被低估，且在諸如綠色政策與利潤、貧窮與環境惡化等領域之間建立了虛假的關聯。我們這些期盼更美好未來的人，需要對這些假設提出質疑。

英文原文

The Brundtland Report , Our Common Future (1987), defines sustainable development as development which meets the needs of the present without compromising the ability of future generations to meet their own needs . Implicit in this definition is the idea that the old pattern of development could not be sustained. Is this true? Development in the past was driven by growth and innovation . It led to new technologies and huge improvements in living standards. To assume that we know what the circumstances or needs of future generations will be is mistaken and inevitably leads to the debilitating sense that we are living on borrowed time. Only if we assume that society will remain static can we understand the needs of the future. The way we live today could not have been predicted twenty years ago. The sustainability paradigm fails to recognize this . It is a static view and thus places limits on human ingenuity . Similarly, a whole host of false assumptions dominate environmental thought; the scale of problems is exaggerated, the amount of resources is underestimated and spurious links are made between areas such as green policies and profit, poverty and environmental degradation. Those of us who want a better future need to question these assumptions .

Implicit in this definition is the idea that the old pattern of development could not be

#13 Diasporas (背井離鄉的人) #060013 原文
中文翻譯

離散族群（Diasporas）——那些生活在故鄉之外、卻仍與故鄉保持聯繫的群體——正變得規模更大、連結更緊密、力量更強盛。 他們是全球化的人性面孔。離散族群意識正在崛起：離散族群對自身起源愈來愈感興趣，也更有組織地凝聚自身力量；故鄉各地隨著移民汙名的消退，也在重新審視對離散族群的看法，並加大與他們互動的力度；與此同時，移入國正目睹愈來愈強勢的離散族群在本國社群中發聲，對「第五縱隊」與外國遊說力量深感憂慮，並飽受「離散族群恐懼症」的困擾。

這一趨勢源自五個因素，而這五個因素均與全球化密切相關：國際移民人口的增長；交通與通訊技術的革命，正加速離散族群與故鄉之間的互動頻率；對全球文化均質化的反彈， 促使人們重新思考自身認同；冷戰的終結，提升了族裔與民族主義的重要性，並為離散族群 開闢了新的行動空間；以及各國政府在雙重國籍與多元文化主義等議題上的政策調整，使人們得以過上跨國生活。 依附於中國、印度、俄羅斯與墨西哥的離散族群規模已相當龐大，但仍將持續擴張； 滋養這些族群的移民潮，未來很可能會更廣泛、更迅猛地湧現。

英文原文

Diasporas – communities which live outside, but maintain links with, their homelands – are getting larger, thicker and stronger . They are the human face of globalization. Diaspora consciousness is on the rise: diasporas are becoming more interested in their origins, and organizing themselves more effectively; homelands are revising their opinions of their diasporas as the stigma attached to emigration declines, and stepping up their engagement efforts; meanwhile, host countries are witnessing more assertive diasporic groups within their own national communities, worrying about fifth columns and foreign lobbies, and suffering outbreaks of ‘diaspora phobia’. This trend is the result of five factors, all of them connected with globalization : the growth in international migration; the revolution in transport and communications technology, which is quickening the pace of diasporas’ interactions with their homelands; a reaction against global homogenized culture , which is leading people to rethink their identities; the end of the Cold War , which increased the salience of ethnicity and nationalism and created new space in which diasporas can operate; and policy changes by national governments on issues such as dual citizenship and multiculturalism, which are enabling people to lead transnational lives. Diasporas such as those attaching to China, India, Russia and Mexico are already big, but they will continue to grow; the migration flow which feed them are likely to widen and quicken in the future .

3quickening the pace of diasporas’ interactions with their homelands; a reaction against global homogenized culture , which is leading people to rethink their identities; the end of the Cold War ,
4can operate; and policy changes by national governments on issues such as dual citizenship and
5attaching to China, India, Russia and Mexico are already big, but they will continue to grow; the migration flow which feed them are likely to widen and quicken in the future .
#14 Human brain activity (人類大腦活動) #060014 原文
中文翻譯

在《公共科學圖書館·綜合》期刊的最新一期研究中，德國一支科學家團隊讓專家與新手辨識簡單的幾何圖形和簡單的西洋棋棋局，並要求受試者加以識別。
研究人員測量了反應時間，並使用功能性核磁共振掃描監測大腦活動。在識別幾何圖形方面，受試者的表現相同，顯示西洋棋專家並不具備特殊的視覺化能力。當受試者被展示西洋棋棋局時，專家的識別速度更快。
專注於早期一項針對西洋棋專家進行的圖案與物體識別研究的某個環節，研究人員原本預期，當受試者執行西洋棋任務時，專家大腦左半球——與物體識別有關——的某些區域會比新手反應得更快。但反應時間卻相同。
真正使專家脫穎而出的，是他們右腦半球的部分區域——更多參與圖案識別——同樣出現了活躍的反應。專家同時在兩個腦區處理資訊。
研究人員還發現，當受試者被展示西洋棋棋盤圖時，新手會直接注視棋子以辨認它們，而專家則將目光落在棋盤中央，以周邊視覺將整體局面一覽無遺。

英文原文

In a study in the current issue of the journal PLoS One, a team of scientists in Germany showed experts and novices simple geometric objects and simple chess positions and asked the subjects to identify them . Reaction times were measured and brain activity was monitored using functional M·R·I· scans. On the identification of the geometric objects, the subjects performed the same , showing that the chess experts had no special visualization skills. When the subjects were shown the chess positions, the experts identified them faster . Focusing on an element of an earlier study on pattern and object recognition by chess experts, the researchers had expected to see parts of the left hemispheres of the experts’ brains — which are involved in object recognition — react more quickly than those of the novices when they performed the chess tasks. But the reaction times were the same . What set the experts apart was that parts of their right brain hemispheres — which are more involved in pattern recognition — also lit up with activity. The experts were processing the information in two places at once. The researchers also found that when the subjects were shown the chess diagrams, the novices looked directly at the pieces to recognize them, while the experts looked on the middle of the boards and took everything in with their peripheral vision .

#原文

Reaction times were measured and brain activity was monitored using functional M·R·I· scans. On the identification of the geometric objects, the subjects performed the same , showing that the chess experts had no special visualization skills. When the subjects were shown the chess positions, the experts identified them faster .
2the chess tasks. But the reaction times were the same .

#15 Microplastics (微塑料) #060015 原文
中文翻譯

新研究已證實，流入世界各大洋的塑料顆粒正在殺死魚類，並阻礙牠們長至成熟。
研究發現，部分幼魚竟偏好吞食微小塑料顆粒，而非天然食物來源，導致牠們在能夠繁殖之前便已實際上餓死。微塑料的問題日益嚴峻——這些來自現代工業的微小聚合物類材料顆粒——數年來一直被認為是魚類的一大威脅，而週四發表的這項研究，首次在實驗中證實了這種危害。
微塑料在自然環境中幾乎無法被分解。它們透過垃圾污染進入海洋——當塑料袋、包裝材料及其他便利性材料被隨意丟棄時，便開始這段旅程。大量此類垃圾因廢棄物處理系統不完善及污水排放，最終流入大海。
另一個日益增長的來源是微珠，這些堅硬塑料的微小顆粒被用於化妝品中，例如作為現代潔膚產品的磨砂成分。這些顆粒在使用時隨水沖走、流入下水道後便無人追蹤，卻能在海洋中存留數十年。
儘管這些材料的危害愈發令人憂慮，其影響卻一直難以量化。在海鳥、魚類和鯨魚體內已發現微小塑料顆粒，這些動物雖然吞下了這些材料，卻無法消化，導致其在消化道中不斷積累。
科學家首次證實，在發育期間暴露於此類材料的魚類，會出現生長遲緩和死亡率升高的現象，同時伴隨行為改變，而這些行為改變可能進一步危及牠們的生存。

英文原文

Fish are being killed, and prevented from reaching maturity , by the litter of plastic particles finding their way into the world’s oceans, new research has proved . Some young fish have been found to prefer tiny particles of plastic to their natural food sources , effectively starving them before they can reproduce. The growing problem of microplastics – tiny particles of polymer-type materials from modern industry – has been thought for several years to be a peril for fish, but the study published on Thursday is the first to prove the damage in trials. Micro-plastics are near-indestructible in natural environments. They enter the oceans through litter, when waste such as plastic bags, packaging and other convenience materials are discarded. Vast amounts of these end up in the sea, through inadequate waste disposal systems and sewage outfall. Another growing source is micro-beads , tiny particles of hard plastics that are used in cosmetics, for instance as an abrasive in modern skin cleaners. These easily enter waterways as they are washed off as they are used, flushed down drains and forgotten, but can last for decades in our oceans. The impact of these materials has been hard to measure , despite being a growing source of concern. Small particles of plastics have been found in seabirds, fish and whales, which swallow the materials but cannot digest them, leading to a build up in their digestive tracts. For the first time, scientists have demonstrated that fish exposed to such materials during their development show stunted growth and increased mortality rates, as well as changed behavior that could endanger their survival .

#原文
1Fish are being killed, and prevented from reaching maturity , by the litter of plastic particles finding their way into the world’s oceans, new research has proved . Some young fish have been found to prefer tiny particles of plastic to their natural food sources , effectively starving them before they can reproduce. The growing problem of microplastics – tiny
2Another growing source is micro-beads , tiny particles of hard plastics that are used in cosmetics, for
3The impact of these materials has been hard to measure , despite being a growing source of concern.
4For the first time, scientists have demonstrated that fish exposed to such materials during their development show stunted growth and increased mortality rates, as well as changed behavior that could endanger their survival .
#16 Rosetta stone (羅塞塔石頭) #060016 原文
中文翻譯

1999年，當這件著名文物成為大英博物館「破解密碼」展覽的核心展品時，一個對羅塞塔石碑進行調查與清潔的機會隨之而來。當清除所有非原始古代物質的工作展開時，石碑呈現黑底白字的外觀。隨著處理工作的推進，所發現的各種物質逐一被分析。人手觸摸留下的油脂、十九世紀初塗抹的巴西棕櫚蠟，以及1799年的印刷油墨，均以棉球沾取肥皂液、白酒精、丙酮及純水清除乾淨。最後，1981年塗於文字上的白色塗料——此前一直作為保護層保留——以棉棒沾純水將其去除。石碑正面左下角留有一小塊方形區域未作處理，以展示原本已變深的蠟層與白色填充物。

石碑呈深灰帶粉紅的色調，並有一道粉紅色紋路貫穿其中。如今在文字中可見帶紅褐色的痕跡。經分析，此物質為一種透明礦物，稱為羥基磷灰石；其色澤可能源於鐵的微量成分。該礦物或許是經人刻意塗抹，但目前尚無證據支持此說。此物質在專家認知中既非作為顏料使用，亦非作為繪畫底料（底層塗料）使用於古埃及。

英文原文

An opportunity for investigation and cleaning the Rosetta Stone arose when this famous object was made the centerpiece of the Cracking Codes exhibition at The British Museum in 1999 . When work commenced to remove all but the original, ancient material the stone was black with white lettering. As treatment progressed, the different substances uncovered were analyzed . Grease from human handling, a coating of carnauba wax from the early 1800s and printer's ink from 1799 were cleaned away using cotton wool swabs and liniment of soap, white spirit, acetone and purified water. Finally, white paint in the text, applied in 1981, which had been left in place until now as a protective coating, was removed with cotton swabs and purified water. A small square at the bottom left corner of the face of the Stone was left untouched to show the darkened wax and the white infill . The Stone has a dark grey-pinkish tone with a pink streak running through it . Today you see traces of a reddish brown in the text. This material was analyzed and found to be a clear mineral known as hydroxyapatite ; the color may be due to iron traces. The mineral may have been applied deliberately, but there is no proof of this. This substance is not known by experts to have been used as a pigment , nor to have been used as a base for painting (a ground) in ancient Egypt .

紅字句（原文）
#原文
1An opportunity for investigation and cleaning the Rosetta Stone arose when this famous object was made the centerpiece of the Cracking Codes exhibition at The British Museum in 1999 . #17 Aging Population (人口老齡化) #060017 原文
中文翻譯

2005年，日本的中位年齡在全球所有國家中最高，而澳洲的人口老齡化程度僅屬中等。約50年前，人口結構狀況大相徑庭，當時澳洲人口的中位年齡比日本高出七歲。

人口老齡化是澳洲政策制定者面臨的重大議題，尤其是在長期影響方面——包括經濟成長放緩，以及對老年退休金、醫療和長期照護服務需求日益增加的問題。隨著人口老齡化，勞動年齡人口的增長將趨緩，而退休年齡人口的比例則將持續上升。

持續性的人口老齡化也會導致人口增長放緩甚至出現負增長。雖然已開發國家人口增長下滑的現象受到部分環保人士和社會科學家的歡迎，（注釋3）但經濟學家普遍認為，人口減少將帶來黯淡的經濟前景。除了勞動力供給減少之外，商品與服務市場的萎縮也可能從需求端衝擊整體經濟。

這一過程發生的速度快慢，取決於生育率、死亡率與海外移民的動態變化。適度的人口結構變化速度，可讓經濟與政策得以逐步調適，以因應人口結構的改變；而劇烈的變化則更難以應對。因此，政府與整體社會可能需要採取行動來解決這些問題。

英文原文

In 2005 Japan had the highest median age of all countries in the world, while Australia's population was only moderately aged. Some 50 years ago the demographic situation was quite different, with the median age of Australia's population being seven years older than Japan's. The ageing of the population is a major issue for Australian policy makers , particularly in regard to the long-term implications for reduced economic growth and the increasing demand for Age Pensions, and health and aged care services. As the population ages, growth in the number of people of working age will slow, while the proportion of people of retirement age will increase. Sustained population ageing also leads to slowing or negative population growth . While declining population growth in developed countries is welcomed by some environmentalist and social scientists, (EndNote 3) economists tend to agree that population decline brings gloomy economic prospects. In addition to the decrease in the labor supply, the demand side of the economy may be affected through shrinking markets for goods and services. How quickly this occurs depends on the dynamics of fertility, mortality and overseas migration . While a moderate pace of demographic change allows for gradual adjustment of the economy and policies to the changing population demographics, rapid changes are more difficult to manage. As a result, governments and society as a whole may need to take actions to address these issues .

#19 IPCC vs Gore (IPCC vs 戈爾) #060019 原文
中文翻譯

今年的諾貝爾和平獎實至名歸，頒給了聯合國氣候變遷委員會（IPCC）的數千位科學家。這些科學家從事著卓越而嚴謹的工作，精確地揭示了世界應對氣候變遷的預期結果。
另一位得獎者，美國前副總統艾爾·戈爾，則花了更多時間告訴我們應該恐懼什麼。IPCC 的估算與結論建立在嚴謹的研究之上，戈爾卻似乎不受同樣的約束。
戈爾在其榮獲奧斯卡的電影中（近來被一位英國法官評為「片面」且含有「科學錯誤」）告訴全世界，本世紀海平面將上升二十英尺。他忽略了同為諾貝爾獎得主的 IPCC 的研究結論——IPCC 認為本世紀海平面僅會上升半英尺至兩英尺，最可能的預估約為一英尺。這與過去一百五十年間世界所經歷的海平面變化幅度相近。
同樣地，戈爾對格陵蘭冰層加速融化及其對地球的影響憂心忡忡，卻對 IPCC 的結論視而不見——IPCC 指出，若目前的融化速度持續下去，到本世紀末僅會為海平面上升增加三英寸。戈爾也無視於研究顯示格陵蘭在一九四一年的氣溫實際上高於今日的事實。
這位從政客轉型為電影製作人的人士，對預測中與高溫相關的死亡人數上升寢食難安。然而故事還有另一面，只是說來不那麼方便：氣溫上升將減少寒流侵襲的次數，而寒冷造成的死亡遠多於高溫。最具代表性的研究顯示，到二〇五〇年，高溫將多奪走四十萬條人命，但因寒冷而死亡的人數將減少一百八十萬。事實上，根據首份針對氣候變遷對全球經濟影響所做的完整調查，全球暖化實際上將有助於挽救生命。

英文原文

This year’s Nobel Peace Prize justly rewards the thousands of scientists of the United Nations Climate Change Panel (the IPCC). These scientists are engaged in excellent, painstaking work that establishes exactly what the world should expect from climate change. The other award winner, former US Vice President Al Gore, has spent much more time telling us what to fear. While the IPCC’s estimates and conclusions are grounded in careful study, Gore doesn’t seem to be similarly restrained . Gore told the world in his Academy Award winning movie (recently labelled "one sided" and containing "scientific errors" by a British judge) to expect 20-foot sea level rises over this century. He ignores the findings of his Nobel co-winners, the IPCC, who conclude that sea levels will rise between only a half foot and two feet over this century, with their best expectation being about one foot. That’s similar to what the world experienced over the past 150 years. Likewise, Gore agonizes over the accelerated melting of ice in Greenland and what it means for the planet, but overlooks the IPCC’s conclusion that, if sustained, the current rate of melting would add just three inches to the sea level rise by the end of the century. Gore also takes no notice of research showing that Greenland’s temperatures were higher in 1941 than they are today. The politician turned movie maker loses sleep over a predicted rise in heat related deaths . There’s another side of the story that’s inconvenient to mention: rising temperatures will reduce the number of cold spells, which are a much bigger killer than heat. The best study shows that by 2050, heat will claim 400,000 more lives, but 1·8 million fewer will die because of cold. Indeed, according to the first complete survey of the economic effects of climate change for the world, global warming will actually save lives.

#20 Nutritional science (營養科學) #060020 原文
中文翻譯

大多數時候，當我著手進行這類調查時，很快就會發現事情比我原本預想的要複雜且模糊得多——灰色地帶遠不止一兩層。
但這次不同。我愈深入鑽研這片混亂而令人困惑的營養科學叢林，梳理那場曠日持久的脂肪與碳水化合物之戰、膳食纖維的小規模交鋒，以及激烈爭論不休的膳食
補充劑論戰，眼前的圖景反而愈來愈清晰。我發現，事實上科學對營養的了解遠比你預期的少——事實上，說得客氣一點，營養科學是一門非常年輕的學科。
它仍在努力弄清楚，當你啜飲一口汽水時，你的身體裡究竟發生了什麼；或者一根胡蘿蔔深處到底藏著什麼，讓它對你如此有益；又或者，你的胃裡為何會有那麼多神經元——腦細胞！——偏偏就在那個地方。這是個令人著迷的領域，也許有朝一日這個學科能對我們關心的營養問題給出明確答案，但——正如營養學家自己所坦承的——他們還沒到那一步。甚至還差得遠。
營養科學畢竟不過是在兩百年前才剛剛起步，如今的發展程度，大約相當於1650年的外科醫學——前景非常看好，看著它進步也非常有趣，但你準備好讓他們替你動刀了嗎？我想我還是再等一等。

英文原文

Most of the time when I embark on such an investigation, it quickly becomes clear that matters are much more complicated and ambiguous — several shades grayer — than I thought going in. Not this time. The deeper I delved into the confused and confusing thicket of nutritional science, sorting through the long-running fats versus carb wars, the fiber skirmishes and the raging dietary supplement debates, the simpler the picture gradually became. I learned that in fact science knows a lot less about nutrition than you would expect – that in fact nutrition science is, to put it charitably, a very young science. It’s still trying to figure out exactly what happens in your body when you sip a soda, or what is going on deep in the soul of a carrot to make it so good for you, or why in the world you have so many neurons – brain cells! – in your stomach, of all places. It’s a fascinating subject, and someday the field may produce definitive answers to the nutritional questions that concern us, but — as nutritionists themselves will tell you — they’re not there yet. Not even close. Nutrition science , which after all only got started less than two hundred years ago, is today approximately where surgery was in the year 1650 – very promising, and very interesting to watch , but are you ready to let them operate on you? I think I’ll wait awhile .

紅字句（原文）
#原文
1supplement debates, the simpler the picture gradually became. It’s still trying to figure out exactly what happens in your body when you sip a soda, or what is going on deep in the soul of a carrot to make it so good for you, or why in the world you have so many neurons – brain cells! – in your stomach, of all places. It’s a fascinating subject, and someday the field may produce definitive answers to the nutritional questions that concern us, but — as nutritionists themselves will tell you — they’re not there yet. Not even close. Nutrition science , which after all only got started less than two hundred years ago, is today approximately where surgery was in the year 1650 – very promising, and very interesting to watch , but are you ready to let them operate on you? I think I’ll wait awhile .
#21 Water resources (水資源) #060021 原文
中文翻譯

水是可持續發展的核心。水資源及其所提供的各類服務，是減貧、經濟成長與環境永續的基石。從糧食
與能源安全，到人類與環境健康，水促進了社會
福祉的提升與包容性成長，影響著數十億人的生計。
在不久的將來可實現的永續世界中，水及相關資源的管理，應能支撐人類福祉，並在穩健的經濟體系中維護生態系統的完整性。
充足且安全的水能滿足每個人的基本需求，透過可靠且負擔得起的供水與衛生服務，使健康的生活方式與行為得以輕鬆維持，並藉由公平延伸、高效管理的基礎設施加以支撐。水資源管理、基礎設施與服務提供均以永續方式獲得資金支持。
水在其所有形式中均受到應有的重視，廢水被視為可回收能源、養分與淡水的資源。人類聚落的發展與自然水循環及其支撐的生態系統和諧共存，並設有相應措施以降低脆弱性、提升應對
水相關災害的韌性。以整合方式推進水資源開發、管理與利用，
以及落實人權，已成為常態。
水的治理採取參與式方式，充分發揮女性與男性作為專業人士與公民的潛能，在公正透明的制度框架下，由多個具能力且知識豐富的組織加以引導。

英文原文

Water is at the core of sustainable development . Water resources, and the range of services they provide, underpin poverty reduction, economic growth and environmental sustainability. From food and energy security to human and environmental health, water contributes to improvements in social well- being and inclusive growth , affecting the livelihoods of billions. In a sustainable world that is achievable in the near future, water and related resources are managed in support of human well-being and ecosystem integrity in a robust economy . Sufficient and safe water is made available to meet every person’s basic needs , with healthy lifestyles and behaviors easily upheld through reliable and affordable water supply and sanitation services, in turn supported by equitably extended and efficiently managed infrastructure. Water resources management, infrastructure and service delivery are sustainably financed. Water is duly valued in all its forms, with wastewater treated as a resource that avails energy, nutrients and freshwater for reuse. Human settlements develop in harmony with the natural water cycle and the ecosystems that support it, with measures in place that reduce vulnerability and improve resilience to water-related disasters. Integrated approaches to water resources development, management and use, and to human rights, are the norm . Water is governed in a participatory way that draws on the full potential of women and men as professionals and citizens, guided by a number of able and knowledgeable organizations, within a just and transparent institutional framework.

#22 Presidential election (總統選舉) #060022 原文
中文翻譯

根據美國憲法，總統選舉每四年舉行一次。選出總統和副總統的程序在選舉日之前很久便已開始。來自主要及次要政黨的候選人，以及獨立候選人，至少在全國總統大選前一年便開始籌募資金並展開競選活動。為了正式代表某一政黨，候選人必須獲得該黨提名。這一初選提名過程是一場競爭，往往在政黨內部引發派系紛爭。這些分裂影響了爭取提名的候選人在政策立場和議程上的取向，因為他們需要竭力爭取黨內領袖和活躍人士的支持。提名程序正式始於各州的第一輪初選和黨團會議，通常在選舉年的二月舉行。正是在這些地方性活動中，選民獲得了首次參與選出下一任總統的機會。

影響誰最終成為政黨候選人的因素有很多。公眾對候選人的觀感受到諸多因素影響，例如媒體報導、民意調查、候選人偏好調查及廣告宣傳。這些因素將有助於確定候選人在黨團會議和初選前數月內的perceived優勢與劣勢。

英文原文

According to the United States Constitution, a presidential election is to be held once every fourth year . The process of electing a President and Vice-President begins long before Election Day . Candidates from both major and minor political parties and independent candidates begin to raise money and campaign at least one year in advance of the general presidential election. In order to officially represent a political party, a candidate must be nominated by that party . This primary nomination process is a contest that often produces factions within political parties. These divisions impact the policy stances and agendas of the candidates running for nomination as they attempt to garner the support of party leaders and activists. The nominating process officially begins with the first state primaries and caucuses, which usually occur in the month of February of the election year. It is at these local events that voters are given their first chance to participate in electing the nation’s next President. There are many factors that influence who will ultimately become the candidate for a party . The public’s perception of the candidates is influenced by such things as media reports, public opinion polls, candidate preference surveys, and advertising. These factors will help determine the perceived strengths and weaknesses of the candidates in the months leading up to the caucuses and primaries .

#23 Strategic alliance (美澳聯盟) #060023 原文
中文翻譯

有些「時刻」事後回想起來，似乎比當時更為重要。以大衛·戴伊（David Day）為例，他研究了約翰·科廷（John Curtin）在1941年12月發表的著名聲明「澳大利亞寄望於美國」——這一時刻被視為澳大利亞戰略聯盟從英國轉向美國的根本性轉變。正如戴伊所指出的，美國成為澳大利亞主要盟友的轉變，是一個歷經半個多世紀的漫長過程。科廷的聲明具有標誌性意義——它代表並象徵著這一轉變——但就其本身而言，幾乎未帶來任何實質改變。羅素·麥格雷戈（Russell McGregor）就1967年全民公投提出了類似論點，這次公投在人們記憶中被錯誤地稱頌為原住民權利的重大進步。

我們的撰稿人還考察了許多其他重要事件——拯救富蘭克林河的運動；加里波利的登陸；1851年的黃金發現；以及為應對大蕭條而制定的災難性「首相計劃」，僅舉幾例。

綜合而言，我們的撰稿人表明，對澳大利亞歷史的敘事性解讀並不像想像中那麼簡單。當然，這涉及一個問題：哪些內容應該被納入，哪些不應該——究竟什麼樣的時刻或事件才足夠重要，值得被納入官方敘事？同樣重要的是，被納入敘事歷史的時刻和事件，都可以有多種詮釋方式。

我們希望這部文集能為那些希望為學童推行統一歷史課程的人提供重要警示，也確實為所有希望了解本國歷史的澳大利亞人帶來啟示；歷史從來都不是簡單或直白的，它永遠抵拒使其如此的企圖。

英文原文

Some "moments" seem more important in hindsight than they were at the time. David Day, for example, looks at John Curtin's famous "Australia looks to America" statement of December 1941, a moment remembered as embodying a fundamental shift in Australia's strategic alliance away from Britain towards the US . As Day points out, the shift to the US as our primary ally was a long, drawn-out process which occurred over half a century. Curtin's statement is iconic - it represents and symbolizes the shift - but in and of itself it made almost no difference. Russell McGregor makes similar arguments with regard to the 1967 referendum, falsely hailed in our memories as a huge advance in Aboriginal rights. There are many other important events which our contributors examine - the campaign to save the Franklin River; the landings at Gallipoli, the discovery of gold in 1851, the disastrous Premiers' Plan designed to cope with the Great Depression, to name just a few. Taken together, our contributors show that narrative approaches to Australian history are not as simple as might be imagined . There is of course the issue of what should be included and what should not be - what, after all, makes a moment or an event sufficiently important to be included in an official narrative? Just as importantly, the moments and events that are included in narrative histories are open to multiple interpretations . We hope this collection will provide an important reminder to those wanting to impose a universal history curriculum for our schoolchildren, and indeed a lesson to all Australians wishing to understand their nation's past; History is never simple or straightforward, and it always resists attempts to make it so .

#24 Aging (人口老齡化) #060024 原文
中文翻譯

我們生活在一個日益老齡化的世界。這一現象在已開發國家已被認識許久，但直到近年來才得到全面的正視。全球通訊正在「縮小」世界，而全球老齡化正在使世界「走向成熟」。老年人口在世界上日益增多，使各個年齡層的人們更加意識到，我們生活在一個多元、多世代共存的社會中。無論人們以正面或負面的眼光看待老齡化，都已無法再對其視而不見。

人口學家指出，若老齡化的當前趨勢如預測般持續發展，一場人口革命將在短短三個世代內到來——年輕人口與老年人口的比例將經歷歷史性的交叉逆轉。這幅世界人口變遷的圖景，其規模可與工業革命相媲美——工業革命向來被視為自新石器時代以來人類歷史上最重大的社會與經濟突破。它開啟了邁向現代經濟增長的持續運動，正如今日的全球化正標誌著一場邁向「全球文化」的前所未有的持續運動。可以預見，這場人口革命的影響力將至少同樣深遠。

儘管未來的影響尚不明朗，一個可能的情景是：挑戰與機遇將同時從一個注滿探索與研究、對話與辯論的容器中湧現。挑戰來自社會與經濟結構試圖適應這一並行現象——年輕世代縮減，同時老年群體壯大；而機遇則體現在龐大的老年人口數量，以及社會從其貢獻中所能獲取的豐厚資源。

英文原文

We live in an ageing world . While this has been recognized for some time in developed countries, it is only recently that this phenomenon has been fully acknowledged . Global communication is "shrinking" the world, and global ageing is "maturing" it. The increasing presence of older persons in the world is making people of all ages more aware that we live in a diverse and multigenerational society. It is no longer possible to ignore ageing, regardless of whether one views it positively or negatively. Demographers note that if current trends in ageing continue as predicted, a demographic revolution, wherein the proportions of the young and the old will undergo a historic crossover, will be felt in just three generations . This portrait of change in the world's population parallels the magnitude of the industrial revolution traditionally considered the most significant social and economic breakthrough in the history of humankind since the Neolithic period. It marked the beginning of a sustained movement towards modern economic growth in much the same way that globalization is today marking an unprecedented and sustained movement toward a "global culture". The demographic revolution, it is envisaged, will be at least as powerful. While the future effects are not known, a likely scenario is one where both the challenges as well as the opportunities will emerge from a vessel into which exploration and research, dialogue and debate are poured. Challenges arise as social and economic structures try to adjust to the simultaneous phenomenon of diminishing young cohorts with rising older ones, and opportunities present themselves in the sheer number of older individuals and the vast resources societies stand to gain from their contribution.

3poured. Challenges arise as social and economic structures try to adjust to the simultaneous phenomenon of diminishing young cohorts with rising older ones, and opportunities present themselves in the sheer number of older individuals and the vast resources societies stand to gain
#25 City Livability (宜居城市) #060025 原文
中文翻譯

如果我們無法就是什麼讓城市偉大達成共識，又怎能從零開始設計出偉大的城市？那些人們最嚮往居住的城市——如倫敦、紐約、巴黎和香港——在詢問最宜居城市的調查中，幾乎從未名列前茅。

以最新一期《經濟學人》智庫的宜居城市排名為例，前三名分別是 墨爾本、溫哥華和維也納。它們都令人心曠神怡，但稱得上偉大嗎？首先要釐清的問題，是宜居與偉大之間的差異。或許我們無法奢望打造出一座偉大的城市，但若我們致力於打造一座宜居的城市，它日後是否有可能成為偉大的城市？

有幾項基本要素是不可或缺的。第一是公共空間。無論是維也納的環城大道與普拉特公園，還是墨爾本和溫哥華的海灘，這些場所讓 城市得以喘息，讓市民不分階級、不論貧富，都能相聚交流、自在呼吸。優秀的城市 也似乎與自然緊密相連，這三座城市都能輕鬆抵達多樣而壯麗的自然景觀與地形地貌。

倫敦政治經濟學院城市研究教授瑞奇·伯德特表示，第二個關鍵因素 是完善的交通系統。「平價的公共交通，是所有成功城市共同具備的一項特質，」 他說。

英文原文

How can we design great cities from scratch if we cannot agree on what makes them great? None of the cities where people most want to live — such as London, New York, Paris and Hong Kong — comes near to being at the top of surveys asking which are best to live in. The top three in the most recent Economist Intelligence Unit’s livability ranking, for example, were Melbourne, Vancouver and Vienna. They are all perfectly pleasant, but great? The first question to tackle is the difference between livability and greatness . Perhaps we cannot aspire to make a great city, but if we attempt to make a livable one , can it in time become great? There are some fundamental elements that you need . The first is public space . Whether it is Vienna’s Ringstrasse and Prater park, or the beaches of Melbourne and Vancouver, these are places that allow the city to pause and the citizens to mingle and to breathe, regardless of class or wealth. Good cities also seem to be close to nature, and all three have easy access to varied, wonderful landscapes and topographies . A second crucial factor , says Ricky Burdett, a professor of urban studies at the London School of Economics, is a good transport system. " Affordable public transport is the one thing which cuts across all successful cities ," he says.

#26 Honey (蜂蜜的好處) #060026 大意
中文翻譯

為了獲得競爭優勢，運動員常常使用能大幅提升運動表現的藥物。
美國全國蜂蜜委員會近期發現，蜂蜜具有相同的功效，但負面影響更小。這項臨床試驗是一系列以運動員使用蜂蜜為主題的研究中第三個。第一項研究（共71名受試者）發現，蜂蜜對血糖的影響比其他常見碳水化合物凝膠形式更為溫和。
該系列的第二項研究（共39名重量訓練受試者）探討了蜂蜜與蛋白質補充劑的組合，結果顯示蜂蜜能加速運動後的肌肉恢復。

英文原文

- In order to have a competitive edge, athletes often use drugs with high athletic performance . - The National Honey Board recently found that honey has the same functions but less negative impact. This clinical trial is the third in a series of studies focusing on the use of honey by athletes. The first study (involving 71 subjects) determined that honey has a milder effect on blood sugar than other popular forms of carbohydrate gel . - The second study in the series (with 39 weight trained subjects) investigated the combination of honey with a protein supplement and suggested that honey speeds muscle recovery after a workout .

#27 Silent movies (無聲電影) #060027 原文
中文翻譯

1920年代的電影觀眾體驗主要由無聲電影主導，但也見證了同步聲音技術的引入。在1920年代，電影明星真的是閃耀的巨星——他們領取豐厚的薪酬，好萊塢大咖的時尚品味與生活動態在全球引發迴響；當瑪莉·碧克馥與道格拉斯·費爾班克斯赴歐巡迴時，全球各大城市——包括倫敦、莫斯科等風格迥異的都會——各有10萬人蜂擁而至，爭相迎接這對巨星。早期無聲電影通常伴隨著現場鋼琴或管風琴演奏，為那些被銀幕上活動影像所震撼的觀眾帶來了極大的娛樂享受。

儘管此前已有人嘗試引入聲音技術，但直到1923年，同步音軌才首次以攝影方式錄製並印製於電影膠片的邊緣，並隨之出現在商業發行的電影中。然而此後又過了漫長的七年，有聲電影才全面取得主導地位，最終終結了無聲電影時代。

最早的電影院被稱為「鎳幣影院」，與其後富麗堂皇的豪華影宮相比十分簡陋，但圍繞其間的那股興奮、歡笑、歡樂與淚水交織的氛圍，卻是何等動人！在電影配樂技術引入之前，電影通常由鋼琴依照腳本演奏的音樂加以伴奏。

英文原文

The 1920's movie goers experience was largely dominated by silent movies but saw the introduction of synchronized sound. In the 1920's movie stars were really stars - with huge salaries, the fashions and activities of the Hollywood greats echoed around the world and 100,000 people would gather in cities all over the world, including such diverse cities as London and Moscow, to greet Mary Pickford and Douglas Fairbanks when they toured of Europe. Early silent movies were often accompanied by live piano or organ music and provided enormous entertainment value to audiences captivated by the experience of watching moving pictures on the silver screen. Although there had been previous attempts to introduce sound, it wasn’t until 1923 that a synchronized soundtrack was photographically recorded and printed on to the side of the strip of motion picture film and made it on to a commercially distributed movie. It would still be seven long years before talking pictures gained total supremacy and finally replaced the silent film era . The first movie theatres were called Nickelodeons , and were very basic compared with the luxurious picture palaces that followed but what an aura of excitement, of laughter, fun and tears surrounded them! Before the introduction of movie soundtracks, movies were often accompanied by scripted music from a piano.

#28 Greenhouse gases (溫室氣體) #060028 原文
中文翻譯

當個人開車、為房屋供暖或使用噴霧式髮膠時，溫室氣體便會產生。從經濟學角度來看，這造成了典型的負外部性。大部分成本（在此指源於全球暖化的成本），由並非在做「要開多少英里的車」或「要用多少髮膠」此類決策的其他個體來承擔。

由於駕駛者（或噴霧使用者）享有活動帶來的全部好處，卻只承擔部分成本，該個體從事的活動量便超過了經濟效率所要求的水準。就此而言，溫室氣體問題與某人在密閉空間內吸菸、或在鄉間隨意丟棄速食包裝袋的問題如出一轍。若要讓個體將溫室氣體排放量降低至有效率的水準，我們必須設法誘使他們表現得如同自己承擔了所有行動成本一般。目前最廣為接受的兩種方式是政府管制與課稅，兩者皆已被提出用以應對溫室氣體問題。

英文原文

When an individual drives a car, heats a house, or uses an aerosol hair spray, greenhouse gases are produced. In economic terms, this creates a classic negative externality . Most of the cost (in this case, those arising from global warming) are borne by individuals other than the one making the decision about how many miles to drive or how much hair spray to use. Because the driver (or sprayer) enjoys all the benefits of the activities but suffers only part of the cost, that individual engages in more than the economically efficient amount of the activity . In this sense, the problem of greenhouse gases parallels the problem that occurs when someone smokes a cigarette in an enclosed space or litters the countryside with fast-food wrappers. If we are to get individuals to reduce production of greenhouse gases to the efficient rate, we must somehow induce them to act as though they bear all the costs of their actions . The two most widely accepted means of doing this are government regulation and taxation, both of which have been proposed to deal with greenhouse gases .

紅字句（原文）
#原文
1produced. In economic terms, this creates a classic negative externality . Most of the cost (in this case, those arising from global warming) are borne by individuals other than the one making the decision about how many miles to drive or how much hair spray to use.
2that individual engages in more than the economically efficient amount of the activity . In this sense,
3reduce production of greenhouse gases to the efficient rate, we must somehow induce them to act as though they bear all the costs of their actions . The two most widely accepted means of doing this are government regulation and taxation, both of which have been proposed to deal with greenhouse gases .
#29 Disabled people (殘疾人) #060029 原文
中文翻譯

殘疾人是個人電腦的早期採用者之一。他們很快就意識到，文字處理程式和印表機讓他們擺脫了依賴他人代為讀寫的困境。其中一些殘疾早期使用者對於科技能夠實現的功能累積了豐富的知識，並藉此知識成為高水準的獨立學習者。他們也獲得了足夠的自信，開始要求教育提供者做出調整，讓殘疾學生能夠更好地使用課程軟體和網路，而不僅僅局限於文字處理。

對於某些殘疾群體而言，電子格式的資訊（無論是電腦端還是網路端）比印刷資訊更易於取得。例如，行動能力有限或手部技能受限的人可能難以取得或持拿印刷材料；視障人士可能難以閱讀印刷文字，甚至完全無法閱讀，但這兩類群體都可以藉助電腦，進而以電子方式獲取資訊。

線上通訊能讓殘疾學生與同儕在平等的基礎上交流。例如，聽障學生或患有亞斯伯格症候群的學生可能難以在面對面的課堂輔導中互動，但在使用文字會議系統時，由於所有人都以打字和閱讀文字進行溝通，他們的互動困難可能會較少。此外，在線上通訊系統中，人們的殘疾狀況不一定會顯露出來，因此殘疾人士無需主動申報自身的殘疾狀況，也不會被視為與眾不同。

英文原文

Disabled people were among the early adopters of personal computers . They were quick to appreciate that word processing programs and printers gave them freedom from dependence on others to read and write for them. Some of these disabled early adopters became very knowledgeable about what could be achieved and used their knowledge to become independent students at a high level. They also gained the confidence to ask that providers of education make adjustments so that disabled students could make better use of course software and the web, rather than just word processing. For some disability groups, information in electronic format (whether computer-based or web- based) can be more accessible than printed information . For example, people who have limited mobility or limited manual skills can find it difficult to obtain or hold printed material; visually impaired people can find it difficult or impossible to read print, but both these groups can be enabled to use a computer and, therefore, access the information electronically. Online communication can enable disabled students to communicate with their peers on an equal basis . For example, a deaf student or a student with Asperger’s syndrome may find it difficult to interact in a face-to-face tutorial, but may have less difficulty interacting when using a text conferencing system in which everyone types and reads text. In addition, people’s disabilities are not necessarily visible in online communication systems; so disabled people do nit have to declare their disability and are not perceived as being different.

#30 Improving literacy (提高讀寫能力) #060030 原文
中文翻譯

世界致力於提升閱讀與寫作的讀寫能力，但這在當今已不再那麼重要。
文字／書面語言究竟是什麼？它是一種用於儲存和提取資訊的古老資訊技術。我們透過書寫來儲存資訊，再透過閱讀來提取資訊。六千至一萬年前，我們許多祖先的狩獵採集社會在土地上定居下來，開啟了所謂的農業革命。這種新的土地定居方式催生了私有財產制度，並促進了商品生產與貿易的增長，帶來了大量新的資訊。由於無法將所有資訊都記在腦中，我們的祖先創造了書面記錄系統，經過數千年的演變，逐漸發展成今日的書面語言。
然而，這種古老的資訊技術已開始走向過時。文字已走完其歷史使命，如今正在我們生活的各個領域迅速被日益多元的新興資訊技術所取代，這些技術以語音、影像和肢體動作為驅動，而非書面文字。
在我看來，這是人類技術演進中積極向前的一步，並為教育的全面正向重塑帶來了巨大潛力。

英文原文

The world engages in improving the literacy of reading and writing, but it is not that important now . What are text/written language anyway? It's an ancient IT for storing and retrieving information . We store information by writing it, and we retrieve it by reading it. Six thousand to 10,000 years ago, many of our ancestors' hunter -- gatherer societies settled on the land and began what's known as the agricultural revolution. That new land settlement led to private property and increased production and trade of goods, generating a huge new influx of information. Unable to keep all this information in their memories, our ancestors created systems of written records that evolved over millennia into today's written language. But this ancient IT is already becoming obsolete . Text has run its historic course and is now rapidly getting replaced in every area of our lives by the ever – increasing array of emerging ITs driven by voice, video, and body movement rather than the written word . In my view, this is a positive step forward in the evolution of human technology, and it carries great potential for a total positive redesign of education .

#原文
1The world engages in improving the literacy of reading and writing, but it is not that important now . What are text/written language anyway? It's an ancient IT for storing and retrieving information . We
2But this ancient IT is already becoming obsolete . #31 Prior knowledge (先前知識) #060031 原文
中文翻譯

先前知識或既有知識，是指學習者在進入一個新的學習情境時所帶來的知識、技能或能力。這包含學習事件發生之前所有已具備的知識，這些知識可透過任何方式、在任何情境下習得或發展而來，包含正式學習情境，以及相當普遍的非正式學習情境。學習者需要具備足夠的先備知識與理解，才能學習新事物；他們也需要協助，以明確建立新知識與舊知識之間的連結。

「激活先前知識」這一過程被認為極具價值。教師通常在開始新主題時會進行這個過程。他們也會在延續前一堂課的課程開始時，運用引導性策略。就教學實務而言，這是一個讓學生思考主題、或回想已學內容的過程。就理論層面而言，這與激活特定的基模有關。

英文原文

Prior knowledge or pre-existing knowledge is the knowledge, skill or ability that a learner brings to a new learning encounter . This includes all knowledge that is available before the learning event, and which has been gathered or developed by any means, and in any situation, including both formal and, quite often, informal learning situations. Learners need enough previous knowledge and understanding to enable them to learn new things; they also need help making links with new and previous knowledge explicit. It is considered to be valuable to go through a process of what has been called 'activating prior knowledge' . Teachers often go through this process at the beginning of a new topic. They also use introductory strategies at the beginning of lessons which are continuations from previous lessons. In terms of the practicalities of teaching, this is a process of making children think about the topic or remember what has been covered already . In terms of theory, it is to do with activating particular schemas .

3terms of the practicalities of teaching, this is a process of making children think about the topic or remember what has been covered already . In terms of theory, it is to do with activating particular schemas .
#32 London (倫敦) #060032 原文
中文翻譯

誰能在1698年想到，當那群來自EC3 Change Alley的Jonathan's Coffee House的小股票經紀人們一邊喝著濃縮咖啡，一邊談天說地之際，竟會成為日後叱吒全球的金融之都的創始成員？

發展過程並非一帆風順。南海泡沫於1720年破裂，咖啡交易所於1748年付之一炬。直至1986年的「金融大爆炸」，那些圓頂禮帽終於功成身退，你也不會押寶倫敦能夠超越紐約、法蘭克福和東京，成為財富之神的
國際樞紐。

然而，如今活躍於英國首都金融核心的32萬5千名從業者，已在所管理的基金規模上（包含離岸業務）超越紐約的對手；他們掌握全球70%的二級債券市場，倫敦金融城更主導著外匯交易。其各大機構於十二月合計發出高達90億英鎊的紅利獎金。「一平方英里」的版圖如今已向東從EC3延伸至金絲雀碼頭，向西則擴張至梅費爾，許多私募股權「蝗蟲」及其對沖基金友人如今便盤踞於此。

對於在金融業打拼的外國人而言，倫敦是非去不可的地方。這裡既無《薩班斯—奧克斯利法案》的束縛，也無歐元的掣肘，然而它能持續高飛，著實出乎意料。倫敦是全球生活費用最高昂的城市之一，交通系統不堪重負，恐怖攻擊的威脅亦如影隨形。但就目前而言，一筆筆交易仍持續越做越大。

英文原文

Who would have thought back in 1698, as they downed their espressos, that the little band of stockbrokers from Jonathan's Coffee House in Change Alley EC3 would be the founder members of what would become the world's mighty money capital? Progress was not entirely smooth . The South Sea Bubble burst in 1720 and the coffee house exchanges burned down in 1748. As late as Big Bang in 1986, when bowler hats were finally hung up, you wouldn't have bet the farm on London surpassing New York, Frankfurt and Tokyo as Mammon's international nexus . Yet the 325,000 souls who operate in the UK capital's financial hub have now overtaken their New York rivals in size of the funds managed (including offshore business); they hold 70% of the global secondary bond market and the City dominates foreign exchange trading . And its institutions paid out £9 billion in bonuses in December. The Square Mile has now spread both eastwards from EC3 to Canary Wharf and westwards into Mayfair, where many of the private equity 'locusts' and their hedge fund pals now hang out. For foreigners in finance, London is the place to be. It has no Sarbanes Oxley and no euro to hold it back, yet the fact that it still flies so high is against the odds. London is one of the most expensive cities in the world to live in, transport systems groan and there's an ever present threat of terrorist attack . But, for the time being, the deals just keep on getting bigger.

#33 Infants’ imitation (嬰兒模仿行爲) #060033 原文
中文翻譯

根據最新研究，與普遍認知相反，幾個月以下的嬰兒對你微笑，並非因為他們在模仿你的笑容。

許多研究指出，嬰兒從出生起便會模仿周圍成人的行為與面部表情。然而，一支由澳洲、南非和英國研究人員組成的團隊本週發表了一項研究，駁斥了這一廣泛流傳的說法。

「1980至90年代有許多研究顯示新生兒並不會模仿，但也有其他研究聲稱確實存在模仿行為，」昆士蘭大學生物學家、本研究共同作者 Virginia Slaughter 說。

「我們希望釐清這一混亂，因為『新生兒會模仿』這個『事實』被廣泛引用，不僅出現在心理學、神經科學和兒科等專業領域，也出現在面向家長的大眾資訊來源中。」

這支國際研究團隊由英國約克大學心理學家 Janine Ostenbroek 主導，讓逾百名嬰兒接觸各式各樣的動作，並分別在他們一週、兩週、六週及九週大時記錄其反應。

這些動作包括社交性動作，例如成人伸出舌頭、皺眉或咧嘴而笑，以及非社交性動作，例如指向某物或打開盒子。

研究結果顯示，嬰兒在出生後頭幾個月所表現的行為，與他們所接觸的動作之間並無關聯。嬰兒做出從未見過的動作的可能性，與重複他們曾見過的動作的可能性一樣高。

舉例來說，無論嬰兒接觸的是指向動作還是打開盒子，而非任何與嘴巴或舌頭相關的動作，他們伸出舌頭的頻率都相同。

英文原文

Contrary to popular belief, babies under a few months don't grin at you because they're copying your own smile, according to new research. Many studies have indicated that from birth, infants imitate the behaviors and facial expressions of the adults around them . However, a team of Australian, South African and British researchers have released a study this week that refutes this widespread belief . "Numerous studies from the 1980s and 90s indicated no imitation by newborns, while others claimed it was there," says Virginia Slaughter, a biologist at the University of Queensland and co-author of the study. "We wanted to clear up the confusion because the 'fact' that newborns imitate is widely cited, not just in the fields of psychology, neuroscience and pediatrics, but also in popular sources for parents." The international research team, led by Janine Ostenbroek, a psychologist at the University of York in the UK, exposed more than 100 infants to a broad range of gestures and recorded their responses at one, two, six and nine weeks of age. The gestures included social cues like adults poking their tongues out, frowning or grinning, as well as non-social cues such as pointing or opening a box. The findings showed no link between behaviors exhibited by babies in their first few months and the gestures they were exposed to. The babies were just as likely to exhibit gestures they had never seen before as repeat ones they had . For instance, babies stuck their tongues out just as frequently if they were being exposed to pointing or opening a box, rather than anything to do with mouths or tongues.

#原文

2The findings showed no link between behaviors exhibited by babies in their first few months and the gestures they were exposed to. The babies were just as likely to exhibit gestures they had never seen before as repeat ones they had .
#34 International trade (國際貿易) #060034 原文
中文翻譯

隨著通訊、運輸與資金流動的速度不斷加快，世界正在迅速縮小。在某個國家開發的產品——Gucci皮包、Sony電子產品、麥當勞漢堡、
日本壽司、德國BMW——已在其他國家獲得熱烈的迴響。聽到一位身穿義大利西裝的德國商人，在一家日本餐廳與英國朋友會面，事後回家喝著俄羅斯伏特加、收看電視節目《與星共舞》，這一點也不令人意外。

過去三十年來，國際貿易蓬勃發展。自1990年以來，全球跨國企業的數量已從30,000家成長至超過63,000家。其中有些跨國企業堪稱真正的巨擘。事實上，在全球最大的150個「經濟體」中，只有81個是國家，其餘69個都是跨國企業。全球最大企業沃爾瑪的年收入，超過了除全球前21大國以外所有國家的GDP。

2000年至2008年間，全球貿易總額每年成長逾7%，輕鬆超越約3%的GDP成長率。儘管近期全球經濟衰退導致世界貿易一度下滑，去年全球商品與服務貿易總值仍超過12兆美元，約佔全球GDP的17%。

許多美國企業長期以來在國際行銷領域表現亮眼：麥當勞、可口可樂、星巴克、奇異、IBM、高露潔、卡特彼勒、波音，以及其他數十家美國企業，已將全世界視為它們的市場。在美國，Sony、豐田、雀巢、IKEA、佳能與諾基亞等品牌，已成為家喻戶曉的名字。其他看似美國產品的商品與服務，實際上是由外國企業生產或持有的。

英文原文

The world is shrinking rapidly with the advent of faster communication, transportation, and financial flows . Products developed in one country—Gucci purses, Sony electronics, McDonald’s hamburgers, Japanese sushi, German BMWs—have found enthusiastic acceptance in other countries. It would not be surprising to hear about a German businessman wearing an Italian suit meeting an English friend at a Japanese restaurant who later returns home to drink Russian vodka and watch Dancing with the Stars on TV. International trade has boomed over the past three decades . Since 1990, the number of multinational corporations in the world has grown from 30,000 to more than 63,000. Some of these multinationals are true giants. In fact, of the largest 150 "economies" in the world, only 81 are countries. The remaining 69 are multinational corporations. Walmart, the world’s largest company, has annual revenues greater than the GDP of all but the world’s 21 largest countries. Between 2000 and 2008, total world trade grew more than 7 percent per year, easily out- stripping GDP output, which was about 3 percent. Despite a dip in world trade caused by the recent worldwide recession, the world trade of products and services last year was valued at more than $12 trillion, about 17 percent of GDP worldwide. Many U·S· companies have long been successful at international marketing : McDonald’s, Coca-Cola, Starbucks, GE, IBM, Colgate, Caterpillar, Boeing, and dozens of other American firms have made the world their market. In the United States, names such as Sony, Toyota, Nestlé, IKEA, Canon, and Nokia have become household words. Other products and services that appear to be American are, in fact, produced or owned by foreign companies .

#35 Learning a Language (學語言) #060035 原文
中文翻譯

多年來，語言教師在兩種教學取向之間交替搖擺：一種著重於語言的實際運用，另一種則聚焦於語言形式或語法分析。這種交替現象源於一個根本性的爭議——究竟是透過直接使用第二語言來學習溝通（例如沉浸式學習），還是透過學習目標語言的詞彙語法——即詞彙與語法結構——來習得溝通能力。換言之，這場爭論的核心在於：達成相同目標的兩種不同途徑，究竟哪一種更為有效。

如同任何長久以來懸而未決的爭議，這個問題並不容易輕易化解。首先，兩種觀點都有各自的支持證據。我們不難發現這樣的學習者：無論出於何種原因，他們身處一個新的國家或本國的新地區，需要學習一門新語言，卻在沒有正規教學輔助的情況下自行習得。若他們已過青春期，或許會保留某種口音，但他們能夠掌握足夠的語言來滿足日常溝通需求。事實上，其中一些人是天生的語言習得者，能以這種方式達到相當高的語言水平。相對地，也有一些學習者對新語言的接觸完全仰賴課堂上的詞彙語法教學，然而他們同樣達到了一定程度的溝通能力，其中某些學習者甚至也達到了相當高的語言水平。由此可以推論，人類是極具適應力的學習者，而某些人天生就具備習得語言的才能，無論在何種環境下都能成功。

英文原文

Over the years, language teachers have alternated between favoring teaching approaches that focus primarily on language use and those that focus on language forms or analysis . The alternation has been due to a fundamental disagreement concerning whether one learns to communicate in a second language by communicating in that language (such as in an immersion experience) or whether one learns to communicate in a second language by learning the lexicogrammar – the words and grammatical structures – of the target language. In other words, the argument has been about two different means of achieving the same end. As with any enduring controversy, the matter is not easily resolved . For one thing, there is evidence to support both points of view .It is not uncommon to find learners who, for whatever reason, find themselves in a new country or a new region of their own country, who need to learn a new language, and who do so without the benefit of formal instruction. If they are postpubescent, they may well retain an accent of some kind, but they can pick up enough language to satisfy their communicative needs. In fact, some are natural acquirers who become highly proficient in this manner. In contrast, there are learners whose entire exposure to the new language comes in the form of classroom instruction in lexicogrammar. Yet they too achieve a measure of communicative proficiency, and certain of these learners become highly proficient as well. What we can infer from this is that humans are amazingly versatile learners and that some people have a natural aptitude for acquiring languages and will succeed no matter what the circumstances.

3certain of these learners become highly proficient as well. What we can infer from this is that humans are amazingly versatile learners and that some people have a natural aptitude for acquiring languages and will succeed no matter what the circumstances.
#36 Small war (小型戰爭) #060036 原文
中文翻譯

在這樣的環境中，戰爭不再純粹針對敵對國家的軍事潛力。它更傾向於滲透這些社會的各個領域，並威脅其存續。 大規模殺傷性武器相對容易取得，尤其是成本較低的生物製劑，是主要關切所在。

無論是政府行為者還是非政府行為者，都傾向於在一種可被稱為「非常規」或「小型戰爭」的戰爭中動用武力。依循慣例所進行的戰爭是一種國家間的現象。「小型戰爭」是戰爭的原型，其中的主角不承認任何規則，並持續嘗試違反現存的慣例。 「小型戰爭」的主角既不遵守國際標準，也不遵守軍備控制協議。 他們利用那些無需擔心任何制裁的領土，因為當地沒有正常運作的國家來執行此類制裁，或者相關國家過於孱弱而無法實施制裁。 這種類型的戰爭不提供任何預警時間。
它不僅挑戰民族國家與國際社會的對外安全，也挑戰其對內的安全穩定。

英文原文

In such an environment, warfare is no longer purely directed against the military potential of adversarial states. It is rather directed at infiltrating all areas of their societies and to threaten their existences . The comparatively easy access to weapons of mass destruction , in particular relatively and low-cost biological agents, is of key concern. Both governmental and non- governmental actors prefer to use force in a war that can be characterized as "unconventional" or also as "small wars." War waged according to conventions is an interstate phenomenon. The "small war" is the archetype of war, in which the protagonists acknowledge no rules and permanently try to violate what conventions do exist . The protagonists of the "small war" observe neither international standards nor arms control agreements . They make use of territories where they do not have to fear any sanctions because there is no functioning state to assume charge of such sanctions or because the state in question is too weak to impose such sanctions. This type of war does not provide for any warning time . It challenges not only the external security of the nation states and international community, but also their internal safety .

#37 Short sleep time (人類缺乏睡眠) #060037 原文
中文翻譯

如果你覺得自己睡眠不足，你並不孤單。一項新研究發現，人類進化後的睡眠時間，遠少於黑猩猩、狒狒或其他任何迄今研究過的靈長類動物。Charles Nunn 與 David Samson 是演化人類學家，專門研究人類行為模式的演化歷程。Nunn 任職於北卡羅來納州達勒姆的杜克大學，Samson 則任職於加拿大多倫多大學密西沙加分校。在這項新研究中，兩人比較了包括人類在內的 30 種不同靈長類的睡眠模式。大多數物種每天睡眠 9 至 15 小時，而人類平均只有 7 小時。然而，根據生活方式與生理因素估算，Nunn 和 Samson 認為人類應該睡 9.55 小時。研究中其他大多數靈長類的實際睡眠量，與科學家預測的相符。Nunn 和 Samson 已於 2 月 14 日在《美國體質人類學期刊》線上發表了研究成果。

研究人員認為，人類生活中兩項長期存在的特徵，可能是導致睡眠時間縮短的原因。第一項源於人類祖先從樹上下來、改在地面睡覺的那個時期。從那時起，人類可能需要花更多時間保持清醒，以防範天敵。第二項或許反映了人類在學習與傳授新技能、以及建立社會連結方面所承受的巨大壓力。這些都壓縮了睡眠的時間。

Nunn 和 Samson 提出，隨著睡眠時間縮短，快速動眼期（REM）睡眠在人類身上扮演了格外重要的角色。REM 睡眠是我們做夢的階段，並且與學習和記憶密切相關。「人類的非快速動眼期睡眠時間如此之短，相當令人驚訝，」Nunn 說，「但隨著睡眠減少，總得有些東西讓步。」

英文原文

If it seems like you’re not getting enough sleep, you’re not alone. People have evolved to sleep much less than chimps, baboons or any other primates studied so far, a new study finds. Charles Nunn and David Samson are evolutionary anthropologists. They study how humans have evolved to behave the way we do. Nunn works at Duke University in Durham, N·C· Samson works at the University of Toronto Mississauga in Canada. In their new study, the two compared sleep patterns in 30 different species of primates, including humans. Most species slept between nine and 15 hours daily. Humans averaged just seven hours of shut-eye. Based on lifestyle and biological factors, however, people should get 9·55 hours, Nunn and Samson calculate. Most other primates in the study typically sleep as much as the scientists predicted they should. Nunn and Samson shared their findings online February 14 in the American Journal of Physical Anthropology. The researchers argue that two long-standing features of human life may play into our short sleep times. The first stems from when humans’ ancestors descended from the trees to sleep on the ground. At that point, people probably had to spend more time awake to guard against predators . The second may reflect the intense pressure humans face to learn and teach new skills and to make social connections . That has left less time for sleep. As sleep declined, rapid-eye movement — or REM — sleep took on an outsize role in humans , Nunn and Samson propose. REM sleep is when we dream. And it has been linked to learning and memory . "It’s pretty surprising that non-REM sleep time is so low in humans," Nunn says. "But something had to give as we slept less."

紅字句（原文）
#原文
1If it seems like you’re not getting enough sleep, you’re not alone. People have evolved to sleep much less than chimps, baboons or any other primates studied so far, a new study finds. Charles Nunn
2times. The first stems from when humans’ ancestors descended from the trees to sleep on the ground. At that point, people probably had to spend more time awake to guard against predators . The second may reflect the intense pressure humans face to learn and teach new skills and to make social connections . That has left less time for sleep. As sleep declined, rapid-eye movement — or REM — sleep took on an outsize role in humans , Nunn and Samson propose. REM sleep is when we dream. And it has been linked to learning and memory .
#38 Farming technique (耕種技術) #060038 原文
中文翻譯

西非村民數百年來沿用的一種耕種技術，能將貧瘠的熱帶雨林土壤轉化為肥沃的農地，或許正是緩解氣候變遷、革新全非洲農業的解答。

一項由研究人員主導的全球性研究，首次對賴比瑞亞和迦納發現的豐饒肥沃土壤進行了鑑定與分析。他們發現，這種古老的西非方法——將木炭與廚餘廢棄物加入高度風化、養分貧乏的熱帶土壤中——能將土地轉變為持久肥沃、富含碳質的黑色土壤，研究人員將其命名為「非洲黑土」。

在南美洲，人們近年發現了由亞馬遜先民在前哥倫布時代所創造的類似土壤——然而這些人究竟採用了何種技術來形成這些土壤，至今仍不得而知。此外，促成這些人為土壤形成的種種活動，在歐洲人征服美洲後大多遭到嚴重破壞。

令人振奮的是，西非研究的研究人員得以在社區中與居民共同生活，親身見證這些肥沃土壤的形成過程。這讓他們得以學習到當地社群婦女所使用的技術——她們將灰燼、骨頭及其他有機廢棄物加以處理，從而創造出非洲黑土。

英文原文

A farming technique practiced for centuries by villagers in West Africa, which converts nutrient-poor rainforest soil into fertile farmland, could be the answer to mitigating climate change and revolutionizing farming across Africa . A global study by researchers has for the first-time identified and analyzed rich fertile soils found in Liberia and Ghana. They discovered that the ancient West African method of adding charcoal and kitchen waste to highly weathered, nutrient poor tropical soils can transform the land into enduringly fertile, carbon-rich black soils which the researchers dub ‘African Dark Earths’. Similar soils created by Amazonian people in pre-Columbian eras have recently been discovered in South America — but the techniques people used to create these soils are unknown. Moreover, the activities which led to the creation of these anthropogenic soils were largely disrupted after the European conquest. Encouragingly researchers in the West Africa study were able to live within communities as they created their fertile soils . This enabled them to learn the techniques used by the women from the indigenous communities who disposed of ash, bones and other organic waste to create the African Dark Earths.

#39 Rosling (羅斯林) #060039 原文
中文翻譯

身為斯德哥爾摩卡羅林斯卡學院的醫學博士及國際衛生學教授，羅斯林以公共教育者的身份聞名於世，他運用統計數據揭示世界正在如何改變。
他選擇擔任這個公共角色，源於兩項重要的發現。
羅斯林的第一項發現是，許多人對全球健康與全球發展的最基本事實毫不知情。透過他所進行的調查，羅斯林發現，在貧困以前所未有的速度下降之際，大多數人卻認為生活在極端貧困中的全球人口比例正在上升。同樣地，他發現許多人嚴重低估了全球平均壽命，也未意識到全球醫療服務（例如疫苗接種）推廣的成功。他發現人們的世界觀往往缺乏事實根據，甚至早在「後事實」時代到來之前就已如此。
羅斯林深信，這種對全球進步的漠然是有其影響的。
他以對抗這種「毀滅性的無知」為己任——正是這種無知讓我們淪為憤世嫉俗者，讓我們錯誤地認為全球發展不過是一場幻影。
羅斯林的第二項發現是，人們對事實知識的匱乏，並非因為對全球發展漠不關心，而是因為那些想了解全球發展的人，難以獲取相關知識。無論是專家還是媒體，都未能呈現全球發展如何改變這個世界。
基於這兩項洞察，漢斯·羅斯林以彌合這一落差為己任，致力於呈現全球發展確實存在的實證。
他傳播全球發展研究的方式，是透過公開演講與資料視覺化的運用。

英文原文

A medical doctor and professor for international health at Stockholm’s Karolinska Institute, Rosling became famous as the public educator who used statistics to show how the world is changing . He chose this public role after making two significant discoveries. Rosling’s first discovery was that many people are not aware of even the most basic facts about global health and global development . Through surveys he conducted, Rosling found that at a time when poverty is falling faster than ever before, the majority of people think that the proportion of the world population living in extreme poverty is rising. Similarly, he found that many underestimate global life expectancy widely, and are not aware of the success of delivering healthcare services—for example, vaccines—globally. He found that people’s worldviews often do not have much grounding in facts, even long before the "post-fact" era. Rosling was convinced that this unawareness of global progress matters. He made it his mission to fight this "devastating ignorance" that turns us into cynics, as we falsely believe that global development must be a mirage. Rosling’s second discovery was that this lack of factual knowledge was not because people are not interested in global development, but because it is too hard for those that want to know about global development to access this knowledge . Neither the experts nor the media were presenting how global development changes the world. Based on these two insights, Hans Rosling made it his mission to bridge this gap and present the evidence that global development is a reality . His approach to communicating research on global development was through public talks and the use of data visualisation.

#41 American English (美式英語) #060041 原文
中文翻譯

毫無疑問，美式英語是當今世界上最具影響力、最強勢的英語變體。造成這一現象的原因有很多。

首先，美國目前是世界上最強大的國家，而這種強大的國力必然帶來相應的影響力。事實上，方言與語言之間的區別，往往是以權力為依據來界定的。正如有人所說，語言不過是擁有軍隊的方言。

其次，美國的政治影響力透過美國流行文化得以延伸，尤其是透過美國電影（當然，他們稱之為 movies）與音樂在全球的廣泛傳播。正如 Kahuna 所指出的，一種文化在國際上的主導地位，會帶來其語言的強勢擴張……而語言的擴張，又反過來為其背後的文化增添聲望。

第三，美式英語在國際上的卓越地位，與通訊技術的飛速發展密切相關。微軟由美國人比爾·蓋茨所擁有，這意味著電腦的預設語言設定為美式英語——當然，使用者可以根據自身需求加以更改。

總而言之，美式英語影響力的提升，源於政治實力及其所帶動的美國文化與媒體的擴散、技術進步，以及通訊技術的迅猛發展。

英文原文

American English is, without doubt, the most influential and powerful variety of English in the world today . There are many reasons for this. First, the United States is , at present, the most powerful nation on earth and such power always brings with it influence . Indeed, the distinction between a dialect and a language has frequently been made by reference to power. As has been said, a language is a dialect with an army. Second, America’s political influence is extended through American popular culture , in particular through the international reach of American films (movies, of course) and music. As Kahuna has pointed out, the internationally dominant position of a culture results in a forceful expansion of its language… the expansion of language contributes… to the prestige of the culture behind it. Third, the international prominence of American English is closely associated with the extraordinarily quick development of communications technology . Microsoft is owned by an American, Bill Gates. This means a computer’s default setting for language is American English, although of course this can be changed to suit one’s own circumstances. In short, the increased influence of American English is caused by political power and the resultant diffusion of American culture and media, technological advance, and the rapid development of communications technology .
