#43 Complain (抱怨) #060043 原文
中文翻譯

人類喜歡互相抱怨，這有助於我們感到不那麼孤單。
想想看，當家人或朋友正在經歷艱難時期，他們會打電話給
一個願意傾聽他們訴說苦水的人。不幸的是，負面連結是許多
群體的預設模式。

在某些家庭中，抱怨是獲得關注的唯一方式。當一個人說「我今天過得很糟」，另一個人就必須蓋過他。「你以為你今天很難熬？我還得做三份TPS報告！」同樣的情形也發生在職場和社交場合。「你的孩子到六個月大才能睡過夜？我的孩子整整一歲才能連續睡超過六小時。」這是一場競相比慘的競賽，最悲慘的處境才是贏家。

在《抱怨即連結——互訴苦水指南》一書中，紐約大學朗格尼醫學院精神病學教授艾琳·S·萊文博士說：
「這些對話讓我們感覺良好，是因為我們感到被理解了」。在負面環境中成長的人很早便學會，正向積極只會讓你
被踢出這個圈子。

當家庭晚餐變成一場抱怨大會，你是不會冒著被孤立的風險說出「哇，我今天過得超棒，你難道不覺得人生很美好嗎？」這句話的。將此轉換到職場環境，人們往往在無意識中
認為保持正向會讓你被排除在圈子之外。當負面情緒提供了人際連結，人類便
不願放棄那個帶給他們慰藉的行為。

英文原文

Humans love to complain to each other. It helps us feel less alone . Think about what happens when a family member or friend is going through a tough time; they call up someone who will listen to their tale of woe. Unfortunately, negative bonding is the default for many groups . In some families complaining is the only way to get attention. When one person says, I had a bad day; the other person has to top it. "You think you had a tough day, I had to do three TPS reports!" The same thing happens at work and social settings. "Your child didn't sleep through the night until 6 months? Mine was a full year old before she went over six hours." It's a race to the bottom, the worst situation wins. In Bitching is Bonding, A Guide To Mutual Complaint, Irene S· Levine, Ph·D·, a professor of psychiatry at the NYU Langone School of Medicine says, "the reason these conversations feel good is because we feel understood" . People raised in negative environments learn early on , being positive gets you thrown out of the club. When family dinner is a complaint fest, you’re not going to risk alienation saying, "Wow, I had an awesome day, don't you just love life?"Translate this into a work setting, people, often unconsciously, believe being positive keeps you out of the cool club . When negativity provides bonding, humans are reluctant to abandon the behavior that brings them comfort .

2someone who will listen to their tale of woe. Unfortunately, negative bonding is the default for many groups .
3the NYU Langone School of Medicine says, "the reason these conversations feel good is because we feel understood" . People raised in negative environments learn early on , being positive gets you
4believe being positive keeps you out of the cool club . When negativity provides bonding, humans are reluctant to abandon the behavior that brings them comfort .
#44 Exercise (鍛煉的好處) #060044 原文
中文翻譯

推廣積極的生活方式有助於我們應對英國當今面臨的一些重要挑戰。提升全民身體活動量，具有改善國民身心健康、降低全因死亡率並提高預期壽命的潛力。它還能顯著減輕慢性疾病對醫療與社會照護服務的負擔，從而節省開支。增加騎自行車和步行的比例，將降低交通成本、節省費用並有益於環境。減少駕車出行可以緩解交通擁堵與污染，改善社區居民的健康狀況。

兒童與青少年身體活動所帶來的其他潛在好處，包括透過積極玩耍培養社交技能（如領導力、團隊合作與協作精神）、提高在校專注力，以及抑制反社會和犯罪行為。體育活動對健康的重要性早在五十多年前便已被確認。1950年代，研究人員對比了久坐的公車司機與活動量較大的公車售票員，以及在辦公室工作的電話接線員與活動量較大的郵差，結果顯示，活動量較大的職業群體患冠心病的比例更低，制服尺寸也更小。

這項研究開啟了後續的深入調查，而如今的證據已清楚表明體育活動在預防疾病方面的重要性。我們在人生的各個階段保持活躍都至關重要。身體活動對嬰兒的正常生長與發育不可或缺。這一重要性延續至學齡期，並貫穿成年與老年階段。保持身體活躍能帶來顯著的健康效益，且有一致的證據表明存在劑量—反應關係，即從事身體活動的總量越大，所獲得的健康效益也越大。

英文原文

Promoting active lifestyles can help us address some of the important challenges facing the UK today . Increasing physical activity has the potential to improve the physical and mental health of the nation , reduce all-cause mortality and improve life expectancy. It can also save money by significantly easing the burden of chronic disease on the health and social care services. Increasing cycling and walking will reduce transport costs, save money and help the environment. Fewer car journeys can reduce traffic, congestion and pollution, improving the health of communities. Other potential benefits linked to physical activity in children and young people include the acquisition of social skills through active play (leadership, teamwork and co-operation), better concentration in school and displacement of anti-social and criminal behavior . The importance of physical activity for health was identified over 50 years ago. During the 1950s, comparisons of bus drivers with more physically active bus conductors and office-based telephonists with more physically active postmen demonstrated lower rates of coronary heart disease and smaller uniform sizes in the more physically active occupations. This research led the way for further investigation, and evidence now clearly shows the importance of physical activity in preventing ill health. It is important for us to be active throughout our lives . Physical activity is central to a baby’s normal growth and development. This continues through school, and into adulthood and older years. Being physically active can bring substantial benefits and there is consistent evidence of a dose–response relationship, i·e· the greater the volume of physical activity undertaken, the greater the health benefits that are obtained.

#45 Writing system (書寫系統) #060045 原文
中文翻譯

書寫的起源在很大程度上仍不清楚。書寫系統在世界各地獨立發展出來。我們所知最早的書寫系統約在五千年前發展於中東地區。但其他
文字系統也在印度、埃及、中國及中美洲各自發明。有人認為其中某些系統可能互相影響，
但這一點尚未得到證實。
這些書寫形式看起來截然不同，遵循不同的規則，且閱讀方式往往也大相逕庭。但它們都具備相同的基本功能。
它們都是記錄語言的視覺媒介。
某些地區所發明的早期文字系統，其知識被周邊地區的民族所習得，
他們便加以採用並改良，以適應自身的需求與語言。
以中文為例，它被日本和韓國所採用，但必須加以調整，才能適用於當地所使用的語言。
記錄資訊的方式因時因地而異。並非所有高度發展的社會都形成了書寫系統，也並非所有記錄資訊的方式都需要文字書寫。
南美洲印加帝國在公元十六世紀達到鼎盛，統轄著一片遼闊的疆域，從現代的厄瓜多和秘魯，延伸至玻利維亞和智利的部分地區。這是一個高度複雜的文明，卻並未發展出書寫系統。

英文原文

The origins of writing are largely unclear. Writing systems were created independently all over the world. The earliest we know of were developed in the Middle East around 5,000 years ago. But other scripts were invented in India, Egypt, China and Central America. It has been suggested that some of these systems may have influenced others , but this has not been proved. These forms of writing look completely different, follow different rules and are often read in completely different ways. But they all perform the same basic function . They are all a visual means of recording language . Knowledge of some early scripts invented in certain regions was picked up by peoples living in surrounding areas . They would then adopt and adapt them to their own needs and language. Chinese, for example, was adopted in Japan and Korea, though it had to be altered to apply to the languages spoken there. Methods of recording information have varied over time and place. Not all sophisticated societies have developed writing systems and not all methods of recording information require writing. The Inca empire of South America was at its height in the sixteenth century AD and held power over a huge area that stretched from modern Equador and Peru, to areas of Bolivia and Chile. It was a complex civilisation, but did not develop a writing system.

#原文
1The origins of writing are largely unclear. Writing systems were created independently all over the
2scripts were invented in India, Egypt, China and Central America. It has been suggested that some of these systems may have influenced others , but this has not been proved.
3completely different ways. But they all perform the same basic function . They are all a visual means of recording language . #46 Khoi (科伊科伊人) #060046 原文
中文翻譯

科伊科伊人（Khoi）

現代人類最早被認為在十萬多年前就已居住在南非。
南非的史前史依據廣泛的技術模式被劃分為兩個階段，即石器時代與鐵器時代。
在湯恩發現古人類化石，以及在斯特克方丹、斯瓦特克蘭斯和克羅姆德拉伊的石灰岩洞穴中發現南方古猿化石之後，這些地區被共同列為世界遺產地。
南非最早的居民被統稱為科伊桑人，科伊人與桑人則分別指稱不同群體。這些族群在班圖擴張期間，被來自西非與中非的遷徙非洲人（班圖人）所取代，或有時被其同化。
雖然部分族群保持了各自的獨立性，其他人則被歸入一個稱為「有色人種」的類別，這是一個多種族族群，包含來自以下兩個或多個群體的混血後裔：科伊桑人、班圖人、英國人、阿非利卡人、南島語族、東亞人及南亞人。
歐洲人對非洲海岸的探索始於十三世紀，當時葡萄牙致力於尋找一條通往中國的絲綢之路替代航線。十四至十五世紀，葡萄牙探險家沿西非海岸南下航行，詳細記錄並繪製了海岸線地圖，並於1488年繞過好望角。
荷蘭東印度公司於1652年在揚·范里貝克的指揮下在開普敦設立了貿易站，定居在開普的歐洲工人被稱為自由市民，並逐漸在荷蘭開普殖民地建立了農場。

英文原文

The first modern humans are believed to have inhabited South Africa more than 100,000 years ago. South Africa's prehistory has been divided into two phases based on broad patterns of technology namely the Stone Age and Iron Age . After the discovery of hominins at Taung and australopithecine fossils in limestone caves at Sterkfontein, Swartkrans, and Kromdraai these areas were collectively designated a World Heritage site. The first inhabitants of South Africa are collectively referred to as the Khoisan, the Khoi and the San separately . These groups were displaced or sometimes absorbed by migrating Africans (Bantus) during the Bantu expansion from Western and Central Africa. While some maintained separateness, others were grouped into a category known as Coloureds, a multiracial ethnic group which includes people with shared ancestry from two or more of these groups: Khoisan, Bantu, English, Afrikaners, Austronesians, East Asians and South Asians. European exploration of the African coast began in the 13th century when Portugal committed itself to discover an alternative route to the silk road that would lead to China. In the 14th and 15th century, Portuguese explorers traveled down the west African Coast, detailing and mapping the coastline and in 1488 they rounded the Cape of Good Hope. The Dutch East India Company established a trading post in Cape Town under the command of Jan van Riebeeck in 1652, European workers who settled at the Cape became known as the Free Burghers and gradually established farms in the Dutch Cape Colony .

2The first inhabitants of South Africa are collectively referred to as the Khoisan, the Khoi and the San separately . These groups were displaced or sometimes absorbed by migrating Africans (Bantus)

#47 Beauty Pageants (選美比賽) #060047 原文
中文翻譯

自從澳洲人珍妮佛·霍金斯與洛琳·伊格分別榮獲環球小姐和國際青少年小姐的后冠以來，澳洲對選美比賽的興趣便大幅攀升。這些勝利也引發了一場辯論：選美比賽究竟只是無傷大雅的舊式價值觀縮影，還是一種倒退回女性僅以外貌獲得尊重的年代的行為。

反對者認為，無論是環球小姐還是國際青少年小姐，選美比賽都是對女性的貶低，與時代格格不入。他們表示，這些比賽不過是衰退的象徵。

過去幾十年來，澳洲在以尊嚴和尊重對待女性方面邁出了不少艱難的步伐。年輕女性在成長過程中被教導她們可以成就任何事，2003年澳洲年度人物菲歐娜·史丹利教授便是醫學界鼓舞人心的典範。在1960和70年代，女性主義運動的首要行動之一便是抗議選美比賽，理由是這個行業推廣了以外貌評斷女性乃屬合理的觀念。時至今日，許多年輕澳洲女性對自己的體型仍感到極度不安，因被以外貌評斷而承受著各種壓力。幾乎所有選美冠軍都身形纖細，不斷強化「瘦即是美」的訊息，完全忽視了男男女女本就有各種體型與身材的事實。在一個多達60%的年輕澳洲人隨時處於節食狀態、70%的女學生表示想要減重（儘管大多數人的BMI完全正常）的國家裡，這樣的訊息對年輕澳洲人的心理健康極為有害。

英文原文

Since Australians Jennifer Hawkins and Lauryn Eagle were crowned Miss Universe and Miss Teen International respectively, there has been a dramatic increase in interest in beauty pageants in this country . These wins have also sparked a debate as to whether beauty pageants are just harmless reminders of old-fashioned values or a throwback to the days when women were respected for how good they looked. Opponents argue that beauty pageants, whether it’s Miss Universe or Miss Teen International, are demeaning to women and out of sync with the times . They say they are nothing more than symbols of decline . In the past few decades Australia has taken more than a few faltering steps toward treating women with dignity and respect. Young women are being brought up knowing that they can do anything, as shown by inspiring role models in medicine such as 2003 Australian of the Year Professor Fiona Stanley. In the 1960s and 70s, one of the first acts of the feminist movement was to picket beauty pageants on the premise that the industry promoted the view that it was acceptable to judge women on their appearance. Today many young Australian women are still profoundly uncomfortable with their body image, feeling under all kinds of pressures because they are judged by how they look. Almost all of the pageant victors are wafer thin, reinforcing the message that thin equals beautiful. This ignores the fact that men and women come in all sizes and shapes. In a country where up to 60% of young Australians are on a diet at any time and 70% of school girls say they want to lose weight , despite the fact that most have a normal BMI, such messages are profoundly hazardous to the mental health of young Australians.

#48 Nurse sharks (護士鲨) #060048 原文
中文翻譯

護士鯊是夜行性動物，白天會聚集成多達40隻的龐大群體，靜止不動地休息。
牠們躲藏在水下岩架或礁石縫隙中，護士鯊似乎偏好固定的棲息地點，每天夜間出獵後都會返回同一地方。到了夜晚，護士鯊則大多單獨行動。護士鯊大部分時間都在翻找海底沉積物以尋覓食物。
牠們的食物以甲殼類、軟體動物、被囊動物及其他魚類為主，例如棘龍蝦、螃蟹、蝦子、海膽、章魚、魷魚、海螺、雙殼貝類，尤其是魟魚。

護士鯊據信會趁機捕食處於休眠狀態的魚類，因為這些魚平時行動過快，難以捕捉。雖然護士鯊的嘴巴較小，限制了獵物的體型，但牠們擁有寬大的咽腔，可作為一種風箱式吸力裝置。藉由這種方式，護士鯊能夠將獵物吸入口中。護士鯊也以啃食藻類和珊瑚而聞名。

護士鯊整體行動緩慢遲鈍，大多數時間都靜臥在海底。曾有觀察記錄顯示，護士鯊會以鰭支撐身體靜臥海底，
這樣的姿態可能為甲殼類動物製造出一個虛假的庇護所，然後趁機將其捕食。必要時，護士鯊甚至可以用寬大的胸鰭在海床上「行走」移動。

英文原文

Nurse sharks are nocturnal animals, spending the day in large inactive groups of up to 40 individuals. Hidden under submerged ledges or in crevices within the reef, the Nurse sharks seem to prefer specific resting sites and will return to them each day after the nights hunting. By night, the sharks are largely solitary . Nurse sharks spend most of their time foraging through the bottom sediments in search of food. Their diet consists primarily of crustaceans, mollusks, tunicates and other fish such as spiny lobsters, crabs, shrimps, sea urchins, octopuses, squid, marine snails and bivalves and in particularly, stingrays. Nurse sharks are thought to take advantage of dormant fish which would otherwise be too fast for the sharks to catch, although their small mouths limit the size of prey items, the sharks have large throat cavities which are used as a sort of bellows valve. In this way, nurse sharks are able to suck in their prey . Nurse sharks are also known to graze algae and coral . Generally slow and sluggish, Nurse sharks spend much of their time resting on the bottom of the ocean . Nurse sharks have been observed resting on the bottom with their bodies supported on their fins, possibly providing a false shelter for crustaceans which they then ambush and eat. If it must move, the Nurse shark may even use its large front (or pectoral) fins to ‘walk’ along the ocean floor.

#49 Indonesian volcano (印尼火山) #060049 原文
中文翻譯

1815年，在印尼松巴哇島上，一座外形壯美、長期沉寂的火山，名為坦博拉，壯觀地爆發，其爆炸與隨之引發的海嘯奪去了十萬人的生命。這是一萬年來規模最大的火山爆發——相當於聖海倫斯火山的一百五十倍，等同於六萬顆廣島原子彈的威力。在那個年代，消息的傳遞速度實在不快。

倫敦《泰晤士報》在事發七個月後，才刊出了一篇短訊——實際上是一位商人的來信。但此時，坦博拉的影響已悄然蔓延。約三百六十立方英里的煙灰、塵埃與沙礫擴散進入大氣層，遮蔽了太陽的光芒，導致地球氣溫下降。日落的景象色彩異常豐富卻帶著朦朧之感——這一效果被畫家J·M·W·透納以令人難忘的方式記錄下來，他本人對此欣喜不已——但大多數時候，整個世界都籠罩在一片壓抑昏暗的陰霾之中。正是這死寂般的幽暗，激發了拜倫寫下上述那些詩行。

春天始終未至，夏天也始終未曾溫暖：1816年被稱為「無夏之年」。各地農作物紛紛歉收。愛爾蘭因饑荒及相關傷寒疫情奪去了六萬五千人的生命。在新英格蘭，這一年被俗稱為「一八○○年活活凍死」。晨霜持續至六月，幾乎所有播下的種子都無法生長。飼料嚴重匱乏，牲畜大量死亡，或被迫提前宰殺。無論從哪個角度看，這都是極為可怕的一年——幾乎可以肯定是近代農民所遭遇的最慘烈的一年。然而，全球氣溫的下降幅度僅約為華氏一點五度。正如科學家後來所認識到的，地球的天然恆溫器是一個極其精密敏感的儀器。

英文原文

In 1815 on the island of Sumbawa in Indonesia, a handsome and long-quiescent mountain named Tambora exploded spectacularly , killing a hundred thousand people with its blast and associated tsunamis. It was the biggest volcanic explosion in ten thousand years—150 times the size of Mount St· Helens, equivalent to sixty thousand Hiroshima-sized atom bombs. News didn’t travel terribly fast in those days . In London, The Times ran a small story— actually a letter from a merchant—seven months after the event. But by this time Tambora’s effects were already being felt . Thirty-six cubic miles of smoky ash, dust, and grit had diffused through the atmosphere, obscuring the Sun’s rays and causing the Earth to cool. Sunsets were unusually but blearily colorful, an effect memorably captured by the artist J· M· W· Turner, who could not have been happier, but mostly the world existed under an oppressive, dusky pall. It was this deathly dimness that inspired the Byron lines above. Spring never came and summer never warmed : 1816 became known as the year without summer. Crops everywhere failed to grow. In Ireland a famine and associated typhoid epidemic killed sixty-five thousand people. In New England, the year became popularly known as Eighteen Hundred and Froze to Death. Morning frosts continued until June and almost no planted seed would grow. Short of fodder, livestock died or had to be prematurely slaughtered. In every way, it was a dreadful year —almost certainly the worst for farmers in modern times. Yet globally the temperature fell by only about one point five degrees Fahrenheit . Earth’s natural thermostat, as scientists would learn, is an exceedingly delicate instrument .

#50 Greenland shark (格陵蘭鲨魚) #060050 原文
中文翻譯

一個由科學家組成的國際團隊，包括來自曼徹斯特大學的一位生理學家，將於本月稍晚前往世界最大的島嶼，調查格陵蘭鯊魚——這種動物被認為是壽命最長的脊椎動物。
Holly Shiels 博士同時也是生理學會的受託人，她將是此次科考任務中唯一一位來自英國的科學家，這次探險乘坐由格陵蘭政府委託的科考船 Sanna 出航。此次任務的目的是進一步了解格陵蘭鯊魚——一種北極的頂級掠食者，其壽命超過 272 年，甚至可能超過 400 年。
這一極端年齡是去年由哥本哈根的科學家所揭示，並發表於《科學》期刊。
關於這種鯊魚如何在北極圈附近的深海中存活，目前所知甚少。它既是獵手也是食腐動物，曾被目擊捕食海豹，也曾在其胃中發現北極熊和鯨魚的殘骸。它也是體型最大的鯊魚物種之一，體長可達約五點五公尺，僅略小於大白鯊。
然而，為確保該物種受到充分保護，仍需要更多資訊，正如 Shiels 博士所解釋的：「格陵蘭鯊魚被列為資料不足物種，」她說，「這意味著我們掌握的資訊不足以制定措施，保護牠們免受過度捕撈、污染或氣候變遷的威脅。」
此次探險匯集了廣泛的專業知識，這意味著我們將能夠充分利用我們所發現的任何鯊魚。

英文原文

An international team of scientists , including a physiologist from The University of Manchester, will head to the largest island in the world later this month to investigate the Greenland shark – believed to be the longest-lived vertebrate animal . Dr Holly Shiels, who is also a trustee of the Physiological Society, will be the only UK-based scientist on the expedition aboard the research vessel Sanna commissioned by the Greenland government. The purpose of the mission is to understand more about the Greenland shark, a top predator in the Arctic , which lives for more than 272 years - possibly more than 400. This extreme age was only revealed by scientists from Copenhagen last year and published in the journal Science. Little else is known about how the shark survives in the deep seas around the Arctic Circle. It is both a hunter and a scavenger and has been seen to feed on seals and been found with the remains of polar bears and whales in its stomach. It is also one of the largest species of shark – growing to about five- and-a-half metres, just a bit smaller than the great white. However, more information is required to ensure the species is adequately protected , as Dr Shiels explained: "Greenland sharks are classified as data deficient," she said. "This means that we don't know enough to put measures in place to protect them from over-fishing, pollution or climate change. This expedition has a broad range of expertise which means that we'll be able to take full advantage of any sharks that we discover.

#51 Living in the countryside (住在農村) #060051 原文
中文翻譯

我知道這是個好主意，因為我以前去過那裡。我生在農場、長在農場，卻有幾年被那種住在城市、在城市工作的「大人物」想法給迷住了——而不只是白天進城去向公車揮揮手。

確實，我對農村生活的一些小缺點並不陌生，例如：時好時壞的私人水源，有時會被各種動植物滲入（其中有一次令人難忘，是一隻死羔羊）；農舍和村舍裡沒有中央暖氣；還有那條單線農場道路，積雪、拋錨的農機或走脫的牲畜都能把它堵死。

但好處也很多，這是我在七○年代中期告訴我年輕妻子時說的話。她土生土長於城市，懷胎八月，即將以一棟溫暖寬敞的科斯托芬排屋，換上一座風吹四面的農場小屋，而且收入還低了許多——要說服她農村比城市更好，恐怕並不容易。

英文原文

I knew it was a good idea because I had been there before . Born and reared on a farm I had been seduced for a few years by the idea of being a big shot that lived and worked in a city rather than only going for the day to wave at the buses. True, I was familiar with some of the minor disadvantages of country living such as an iffy private water supply sometimes infiltrated by a range of flora and fauna (including, on one memorable occasion, a dead lamb), the absence of central heating in farm houses and cottages, and a single track farm road easily blocked by snow, broken down machinery or escaped livestock. But there were many advantages as I told my young wife back in the mid Seventies . Town born and bred, eight months pregnant and exchanging a warm, substantial Corstorphine terrace for a windswept farm cottage on a much lower income, persuading her that country had it over town might have been difficult .

#52 Namibia (納米比亞) #060052 原文
中文翻譯

1990年納米比亞獨立時，少女帕斯科萊娜·弗洛里正在這個國家乾燥荒涼的北部疏林草原上放牧山羊。
她的工作既無薪酬又充滿危險，職責是保護父母的牲畜免遭豺狼和豹子的侵害。
她視野生動物為敵人，納米比亞農村公共土地上許多其他原住民也與她持相同看法。盜獵野生動物的情況十分普遍。
十五年後，31歲的帕斯科萊娜的生活與人生觀已大相徑庭。她在旅遊業建立了一番
過去做夢都想不到的事業，成為首位獲任命為賓客旅館經理的納米比亞黑人。
她所在的村莊以及數百個其他村莊，都直接受益於政府將公共土地的管理與旅遊開發權
下放給原住民保護區管理的舉措。「如今，隨著旅遊業的蓬勃發展，我們視野生動物為創造就業與機會的途徑，」她說。「有野生動物相伴，未來會更美好，不僅是為了工作，也是為了環境。」

英文原文

When Namibia gained independence in 1990 , teenager Pascolena Florry was herding goats in the country dry, desolate northern savannah. Her job, unpaid and dangerous, was to protect her parents' livestock from preying jackals and leopards. She saw wildlife as the enemy , and many of the other indigenous inhabitants of Namibia's rural communal lands shared her view. Wildlife poaching was commonplace. Fifteen years later , 31-year-old Pascolena's life and outlook are very different. She has built a previously undreamed of career in tourism and is the first black Namibian to be appointed manager of a guest lodge. Her village, and hundreds of others, have directly benefited from government efforts to devolve management and tourism development on communal lands to conservancies run by indigenous peoples. "Now we see the wildlife as our way of creating jobs and opportunities as the tourism industry grows," she says. "The future is better with wildlife around, not only for jobs, but also for the environment".

#54 Life expectancy (人均壽命) #060054 大意

隨著壽命的延長，人們的儲蓄愈來愈難以支撐多年有品質的退休生活。

葛瑞頓與史考特提出了一些新想法。人們應在退休後持續更新知識，或發展新的社交圈。

我們應將「休閒娛樂」（recreation）轉化為「重新創造自我」（re-creation）。

People should keep updating their knowledge after retirement or develop a new social circle . - We should make recreation into "re-creation" .

#55 Language Decay (語言衰敗 ) #060055 原文
中文翻譯

讓我們先來探討，為何「語言正在衰退」的信念，遠比「語言正在進步」的信念更為普遍。在一個「適者生存」的觀念與「不可避免的衰退」信念同樣強烈的知識氛圍中，竟然有那麼多人相信英語的品質正在下滑，這實在令人費解——英語如今的使用者估計已達五億人，在過去千年間，使用人數或許增加了百倍之多。人們的第一反應，或許是不禁好奇，這些我們姑且稱之為「反馬虎大隊」的成員，是否正在潛意識中對我們所生活的急速變遷世界作出反應，進而對生活各方面的改變感到憤懣。這在某種程度上很可能是事實。「事情已今非昔比」的感受，以及試圖讓生活維持一成不變的衝動，似乎是面對不安全感的自然反應，也是衰老的症狀。每一代人都無可避免地認為，下一代的衣著、舉止與語言已然退步。因此，我們可以預期，在每個世紀、每種文化中都能找到對保守語言的推崇，而在有文字的社會裡，更有對過去「最佳作者」語言的崇敬。

英文原文

Let us begin by asking why the conviction that our language is decaying is so much more widespread than the belief that it is progressing, in an intellectual climate where the notion of the survival of the fittest is at least as strong as the belief in inevitable decay, it is strange that so many people are convinced of the decline in the quality of English, a language which is now spoken by an estimated half billion people – a possible hundredfold increase in the number of speakers during the past millennium. One’s first reaction is to wonder whether the members of the anti-slovenliness brigade , as we may call them, are subconsciously reacting to the fast-moving world we live in, and consequently resenting change in any area of life . To some extent this is likely to be true. A feeling that ‘fings ain’t wot they used to be’ and an attempt to preserve life unchanged seem to be natural reactions to insecurity, symptoms of growing old. Every generation inevitably believes that the clothes, manners and speech of the following one have deteriorated . We would therefore expect to find a respect for conservative language in every century and every culture and, in literate societies, a reverence for the language of the ‘best authors’ of the past.

#56 RAS (皇家農業協會) #060056 原文
中文翻譯

RAS（皇家農業協會）的演變契合西方更廣泛的趨勢——透過展覽場所推廣民族主義、進步理念與科技，這股風潮最早在1850年代興起。從地方農業展到世界博覽會，各類型的展覽會被用作霸權工具，服務於帝國主義、推動方興未艾的資本主義事業，並塑造階級認同、社會空間與公共空間。視覺文化與展示藝術在定義國家特色的各個面向上變得不可或缺。加拿大和澳洲等殖民地國家尤其致力於發展鮮明的民族認同，以區別於英國帝國勢力。北美的農業展覽起源於十九世紀初，致力於透過各種技術手段，教導在職農民改善畜牧與農作物的耕作方式。

1822年，RAS在一個前提下應運而生：澳洲迫切需要發展更精良的農業技術，以更好地支撐不斷增長的城市人口與出口市場。以農業改良為宗旨的組織在英國頗為盛行，為成員提供情誼聯繫，以及政治與財務上的支持。這些組織一旦移植到殖民地——此處即澳洲——便在為殖民目的開墾和整治土地方面，扮演了不可或缺的角色。

英文原文

The evolution of the RAS (Royal Agricultural Society) fits into the wider Western trend of promoting nationalism, progress and technology through exhibitory venues , which first became popular in the 1850s. Various types of fairs , from local agricultural shows to Worlds Fairs, were used as instruments of hegemony to support imperialism , to promote burgeoning capitalist endeavors, and to shape class identities, social spaces and public spaces. Visual culture and the art of display became essential in defining aspects of national distinction . Colonial nations in particular, such as Canada and Australia, were attempting to develop distinct national identities to differentiate themselves from British imperial power. Agricultural fairs in North America originated at the beginning of the nineteenth century and were devoted to educating practicing farmers in ways of improving their cultivation of livestock and crops through the use of various technologies. In 1822, the RAS was created on the premise that was a dire need in Australia for the development of improved farming skills to better support growing urban populations and export markets . Organizations based on agricultural improvement, which were popular in Britain, provided camaraderie as well as political and financial support for their members. Once transferred to the colonies, in this case Australia, they played an integral part in converting and organizing land for colonial purposes.

#57 Great Managers (管理者) #060057 原文
中文翻譯

他們發掘每個人的獨特之處，並加以善用。管理者的職責，則是將某個人的特定才能轉化為實際績效。普通的管理者下西洋跳棋，而優秀的管理者下西洋棋。管理者只有在能夠識別並運用人與人之間的差異時才能成功，激發每位員工以自己獨特的方式追求卓越。這並不意味著領導者不能成為管理者，或反之亦然。但要在其中一個或兩個角色上出類拔萃，你必須清楚認識每個角色所需要的截然不同的能力。

首先，識別並善用每個人的獨特性可以節省時間。沒有任何員工，無論多麼有才華，是完美全能的。米雪兒本可以花費無數小時輔導傑弗瑞，勸說他對顧客展露笑容、與他們建立友誼、記住他們的名字，但她的努力很可能收效甚微。她的時間用在為傑弗瑞量身打造一個能發揮其天賦能力的角色上，效益要大得多。

其次，善用獨特性能讓每個人更具責任感。米雪兒不只是稱讚傑弗瑞完成特定任務的能力，她更鼓勵他將這項能力作為他對門市貢獻的核心，讓他對這項能力負起責任、加以實踐，並持續精進。

第三，善用每個人的獨特之處能建立更強烈的團隊歸屬感，因為這創造了相互依存的關係。它幫助人們欣賞彼此各自的專長，並了解同事能夠在自己不足之處給予補足。簡而言之，它讓人們彼此需要。老生常談說「team（團隊）裡沒有『I（我）』」，但正如麥可·喬丹曾說過的：「team 裡或許沒有『I』，但 win（贏）裡有。」

英文原文

They discover what is unique about each person and then capitalize on it. The job of a manager, meanwhile, is to turn one person’s particular talent into performance. Average managers play checkers, while great managers play chess. Managers will succeed only when they can identify and deploy the differences among people, challenging each employee to excel in his or her own way . This doesn’t mean a leader can’t be a manager or vice versa. But to excel at one or both, you must be aware of the very different skills each role requires. First, identifying and capitalizing on each person’s uniqueness saves time . No employee, however talented, is perfectly well-rounded. Michelle could have spent untold hours coaching Jeffrey and cajoling him into smiling at, making friends with, and remembering the names of customers, but she probably would have seen little result for her efforts. Her time was much better spent carving out a role that took advantage of Jeffrey’s natural abilities. Second, capitalizing on uniqueness makes each person more accountable . Michelle didn’t just praise Jeffrey for his ability to execute specific assignments. She challenged him to make this ability the cornerstone of his contribution to the store, to take ownership for this ability, to practice it, and to refine it. Third, capitalizing on what is unique about each person builds a stronger sense of team , because it creates interdependency. It helps people appreciate one anothers’ particular skills and learn that their coworkers can fill in where they are lacking. In short, it makes people need one another. The old cliché is that there’s no "I" in "team." But as Michael Jordan once said, "There may be no ‘I’ in ‘team,’ but there is in 'win'."

#58 Columbus (哥倫布) #060058 原文
中文翻譯

1492年，當克里斯多福·哥倫布在他首次橫渡大西洋的航行中抵達伊斯帕尼奧拉島時，
這座島嶼早已有美洲原住民定居約5,000年之久。
那個時代居住在此的，是一群稱為泰諾人的阿拉瓦克印第安人，他們以農耕為生，組成五個酋長國，人口約達50萬（各方估計從10萬到200萬不等）。
哥倫布起初發現他們個性平和、友善待人，直到他和他的西班牙人開始虐待
他們。不幸的是，泰諾人擁有黃金，而西班牙人垂涎這些黃金，卻不願親自動手開採。
於是，征服者將這座島嶼及其印第安人口分配給各個西班牙人，
這些人強迫印第安人以近乎奴隸的身份勞動，無意間將歐亞疾病傳染給他們，並加以殘殺。
1519年，也就是哥倫布抵達後的第27年，原本多達50萬的人口已銳減至約11,000人，其中大多數人在那一年死於天花，使人口進一步降至
3,000人。

英文原文

When Christopher Columbus arrived at Hispaniola during his first transatlantic voyage in the year 1492, the island had already been settled by Native Americans for about 5,000 years . The occupants in Columbus’s time were a group of Arawak Indians called Tainos who lived by farming, were organized into five chiefdoms, and numbered around half a million (the estimates range from 100,000 to 2,000,000). Columbus initially found them peaceful and friendly, until he and his Spaniards began mistreating them. Unfortunately for the Tainos, they had gold, which the Spanish coveted but didn’t want to go to the work of mining themselves . Hence the conquerors divided up the island and its Indian population among individual Spaniards, who put the Indians to work as virtual slaves, accidentally infected them with Eurasian diseases, and murdered them. By the year 1519, 27 years after Columbus’s arrival, that original population of half a million had been reduced to about 11,000, most of whom died that year of smallpox to bring the population down to 3,000 .

2them. Unfortunately for the Tainos, they had gold, which the Spanish coveted but didn’t want to go to the work of mining themselves . Hence the conquerors divided up the island and its Indian population among individual Spaniards,

#59 Skipping breakfast (不吃早飯) #060059 原文
中文翻譯

不吃早餐有其弊端。然而，在美國及其他國家進行的研究均顯示，不吃早餐會影響學習、記憶力與身體健康。不吃早餐的學生在面對問題解析時，篩選關鍵資訊的能力不如有吃早餐的同儕。

對於學齡兒童而言，不吃早餐會削弱其記憶與運用新知識的能力、語言流暢度以及注意力的控制，這是加州大學戴維斯分校兒科學教授 Ernesto Pollitt 的研究結論，其研究專注於早餐對身心表現的影響。不吃早餐同樣也會損害成人的思考能力。

對兒童和成人來說，一碗簡單的牛奶麥片就能為一天提供相當充足的營養開端。 Green-Burgeson 建議選擇低糖麥片——每份含糖量低於五克——並搭配脫脂或百分之一脂肪的牛奶。

加州大學戴維斯醫療集團卡麥可分院的小兒科醫師 Frederick Hirshburg 表示，嬰兒和學齡前幼兒很少不吃早餐，因為「他們通常在一天的開始最感飢餓。」Hirshburg 說，早餐對他們而言後來逐漸成為一種「習得的經驗」，而非對生理需求的回應。

英文原文

Skipping breakfast has drawbacks . However, studies conducted both in the United States and internationally have shown that skipping breakfast can affect learning, memory and physical well-being . Students who skip breakfast are not as efficient at selecting critical information for problem- solving as their peers who have had breakfast. For schoolchildren, skipping breakfast diminishes the ability to recall and use newly acquired information, verbal fluency, and control of attention , according to Ernesto Pollitt, a UC Davis professor of pediatrics whose research focuses on the influence of breakfast on mental and physical performance. Skipping breakfast can impair thinking in adults, also . For both children and adults, a simple bowl of cereal with milk goes a long way toward providing a sufficiently nutritious start to the day . Green-Burgeson recommends choosing a cereal that’s low in sugar — less than five grams per serving — and using nonfat or one percent milk. Frederick Hirshburg, a pediatrician at UC Davis Medical Group, Carmichael, says that babies and other preschoolers rarely skip breakfast because "they’re usually the hungriest at the beginning of the day. Breakfast then becomes more of a "learned experience" than a response to a biological need, Hirshburg says.

#60 Cows and grass (牛吃草) #060060 原文
中文翻譯

牛與草之間的協同演化關係，是自然界中鮮少受到重視的奇觀之一；它同時也是理解現代肉食業幾乎一切面向的關鍵。對於已演化出能承受反芻動物啃食能力的草類而言，牛透過阻止樹木與灌木紮根、遮蔽陽光，得以維護並擴展草類的棲息地；這些動物還會傳播草籽、用蹄子將種子踩入土中，再以糞便為其施肥。

作為回報，草類為反芻動物提供了豐盛且獨享的食物來源。因為牛（與羊、野牛及其他反芻動物一樣）已演化出一種特殊能力，能將草——這種像我們這類單胃動物無法消化的植物——轉化為高品質蛋白質。牠們之所以能做到這一點，是因為擁有自然界中無疑是演化程度最高的消化器官：瘤胃。這個器官大小如同一顆藥球，本質上是一個容量達四十五加侖的發酵槽，槽中常駐的細菌群落以草為食。

英文原文

The co-evolutionary relationship between cows and grass is one of nature’s underappreciated wonders ; it also happens to be the key to understanding just about everything about modern meat. For the grasses, which have evolved to withstand the grazing of ruminants, the cow maintains and expands their habitat by preventing trees and shrubs from gaining a foothold and hogging the sunlight; the animal also spreads grass seed, plants it with his hooves, and then fertilizes it with his manure. In exchange for these services the grasses offer ruminants a plentiful and exclusive supply of lunch. For cows (like sheep, bison, and other ruminants) have evolved the special ability to convert grass – which single-stomached creatures like us can’t digest – into high-quality protein . They can do this because they possess what is surely the most highly evolved digestive organ in nature: the rumen . About the size of a medicine ball, the organ is essentially a forty-five-gallon fermentation tank in which a resident population of bacteria dines on grass.

#原文
1The co-evolutionary relationship between cows and grass is one of nature’s underappreciated wonders ; it also happens to be the key to understanding just about everything about modern meat. For the grasses, which have evolved to withstand the grazing of ruminants, the cow maintains and expands their habitat by preventing trees and shrubs from gaining a foothold and hogging the
2For cows (like sheep, bison, and other ruminants) have evolved the special ability to convert grass – which single-stomached creatures like us can’t digest – into high-quality protein . They can do this because they possess what is surely the most highly evolved digestive organ in nature: the rumen .
#61 Solar energy (太陽能) #060061 原文
中文翻譯

太陽能與其他形式的再生能源相比，其優缺點長期以來受到廣泛討論。雖然太陽能在某些方面明顯優於其他能源形式，但其高昂成本以及依賴地理條件的效率問題，限制了它的吸引力。然而，太陽能擁有眾多優點，值得進一步發展，甚至可能推廣應用於住宅。
太陽能之所以持續受到青睞，在於它既是可再生能源，也是清潔能源。這些優點，加上各國希望最終能藉由太陽能來減緩全球暖化的期望，確保了它的持續普及。
可再生性——太陽能是真正的可再生資源。世界上所有地區都具備收集一定量太陽能的能力，且太陽能每天都可供收集。
清潔性——太陽能不會造成污染。它不像以石油為基礎的能源那樣產生溫室氣體，也不像核能那樣產生需要儲存的廢料。太陽能的發電與利用過程也更為安靜，大幅降低了將能源轉換為可用形式所產生的噪音污染。住宅規模的太陽能系統對周邊環境的影響也極為有限，與風能、水力發電等其他再生能源相比更是如此。
低維護成本
太陽能板沒有活動零件，除定期清潔外幾乎不需要維護。由於沒有會損壞或需要更換的活動零件，在完成初期安裝費用後，後續的維護與修繕費用十分合理。

英文原文

The advantages and disadvantages of solar power compared to other forms of renewable energy have been greatly debated. While obviously superior to some forms of energy, solar power's high cost and efficiency dependent on geography have limited its appeal . However, a large number of advantages also merit further development and even possible adaptation for residences . Solar energy remains popular because it is both a renewable and clean source of energy . These advantages along with the hope that eventually nations can use solar power to decrease global warming ensure its popularity. Renewable solar energy is a true renewable resource . All areas of the world have the ability to collect some amount of solar power and solar power is available for collection each day. Clean solar energy is non-polluting . It does not create greenhouse gases, such as oil based energy does, nor does it create waste that must be stored, such as nuclear energy. It is also far more quiet to create and harness, drastically reducing the noise pollution required to convert energy to a useful form. Residential size solar energy systems also have very little impact on the surrounding environment, in contrast with other renewable energy sources such as wind and hydro electric power. Low Maintenance Solar panels have no moving parts and require very little maintenance beyond regular cleaning. Without moving parts to break and replace, after the initial costs of installing the panels, maintenance and repair costs are very reasonable .

#62 Sphinx (獅身人面像) #060062 原文
中文翻譯

這張臉雖然比雕像其他部分保存得更完好，卻已被數百年的風化與人為破壞所侵蝕。1402年，一位阿拉伯歷史學家記載，一名蘇菲狂熱份子為了「糾正某些宗教錯誤」而將其毀容。然而，仍有線索讓我們得以想像它全盛時期的樣貌。19世紀初的考古發掘出土了其雕刻石質鬍鬚的碎片，以及頭飾上的皇家眼鏡蛇徽飾。臉部至今仍可見紅色顏料的殘跡，使研究人員得出結論：獅身人面像的整張臉曾經被塗成紅色。其他部位殘留的藍色與黃色顏料則讓萊納推測，獅身人面像昔日曾以俗豔的漫畫色彩裝飾一身。

數千年來，沙漠將這座巨像掩埋至肩部，使其成為撒哈拉東緣一顆孤懸於沙海之上的龐大頭顱。直到1817年，熱那亞探險家喬瓦尼·巴蒂斯塔·卡維利亞上尉率領160名工人，發起近代首次挖掘獅身人面像的嘗試。然而他們始終無法阻擋沙土，沙子湧入挖掘坑的速度幾乎與他們挖出的一樣快。埃及考古學家塞利姆·哈桑終於在1930年代末將這座雕像從沙中解放出來。「獅身人面像就此從彷彿無法穿透的遺忘陰影中重現於世間，」《紐約時報》如此宣告。

英文原文

The face , though better preserved than most of the statue, has been battered by centuries of weathering and vandalism . In 1402, an Arab historian reported that a Sufi zealot had disfigured it "to remedy some religious errors." Yet there are clues to what the surface looked like in its prime . Archaeological excavations in the early 19th century found pieces of its carved stone beard and a royal cobra emblem form its headdress. Residues of red pigment are still visible on the face, leading researchers to conclude that at some point, the Sphinx’s entire visage was painted red. Traces of blue and yellow paint elsewhere suggest to Lehner that the Sphinx was once decked out in gaudy comic book colors. For thousands of years, sand buried the colossus up to its shoulders , creating a vast disembodied head atop the eastern edge of the Sahara. Then, in 1817, a Genoese adventurer , Capt· Giovanni Battista Caviglia, led 160 men in the first modern attempt to dig out the Sphinx . They could not hold back the sand, which poured into their excavation pits nearly as fast as they could dig it out. The Egyptian archaeologist Selim Hassan finally freed the statue from the sand in the late 1930s. "The Sphinx has thus emerged into the landscape out of shadows of what seemed to be an impenetrable oblivion ," the New York Times declared.

#63 Infra-Red Wave (紅外波) #060063 原文
中文翻譯

我們所看見的顏色，是光在一段狹窄波長範圍內反射的結果——這就是我們所說的可見光譜。但陽光的波長範圍遠不止於此，其中有些是我們肉眼無法看見的。人類看不見紫外線波長，而許多其他動物卻能看見。
但有一段波長是所有生物都無法察覺的——那就是近紅外線（NIR）波長。了解鳥類羽毛如何與這些波長相互作用，不僅對鳥類本身至關重要，對人類也同樣意義深遠，因為這有助於提升熱能效率。
墨爾本大學生物科學學院的研究發現，部分澳洲鳥類能夠透過反射陽光中的近紅外線波長來調節體溫、避免過熱。
我們蒐集了90種澳洲鳥類的資料，發現棲息於炎熱乾旱地區與反射較高比例近紅外線光之間，存在非常強烈的關聯性。
動物體色領域的研究人員長期以來對近紅外線光關注甚少，原因在於它難以測量，且目前也沒有證據顯示動物能夠看見這些波長。
由於這些波長是不可見的，因此不會影響偽裝效果或對異性的吸引力——而這兩者在動物世界中至關重要。這意味著許多動物能夠在不影響隱蔽能力或求偶吸引力的前提下，透過調整對近紅外線光的反射來控制自身體溫。

英文原文

The colours that we see are a result of the light reflected within a narrow range of wavelengths – what we call the visible spectrum . But sunlight also spans wavelengths that we cannot see. Humans can’t see ultraviolet wavelengths, which many other animals can see. But there’s one set of wavelengths that elude all of us – these are near infra-red (NIR) wavelengths . And understanding how bird feathers interact with these wavelengths is important, not just for birds, but also for humans through the potential for improvements in thermal efficiency. Our research in the School of BioSciences at the University of Melbourne suggests that some Australian birds can control their temperature and avoid overheating by reflecting near-infrared wavelengths of sunlight. We collected information on 90 species of Australian birds and found a very strong link between living in hot, arid regions and reflecting a higher proportion of near-infrared light . Researchers in the field of animal colouration have largely ignored near-infrared light, because it isn’t easy to measure and there’s no evidence that animals can see these wavelengths. Because these wavelengths are invisible, they don’t affect camouflage or sexual attractiveness, which are very important in the animal world. This means that many animals can control their temperature by altering reflection of near-infrared light without compromising their ability to hide or attract a mate .

#64 Negotiation (協商) #060064 原文
中文翻譯

協商是商業中常見的流程，主要用於解決雙方之間的商業糾紛。妥協是一種基本的協商狀態，雙方各自放棄某些想要的事物，以換取更重要的目標。妥協通常發生在不對等的情況下，當利益是固定的餅需要分配時，一方所得即為另一方所失。在妥協的情境中，雙方都無法完全得到自己真正想要的，但各自做出讓步，以達成雙方都能接受的協議。雙方通常可以透過妥協實現雙贏的概念。然而，若有一方不願意解決問題，協商便無法化解所有衝突。

英文原文

Negotiation is a common process in business to mainly solve business conflicts between both parties . Compromise is a basic negotiation state in which both parties give up something that they want in order to get something else they want more. Compromise usually occurs in unfair parties when there is a fixed pie to be divided up , and whatever on one side gets, the other side loses. In compromise situations, neither side gets all of what they really want , but they each make concessions in order to reach an agreement that is acceptable to both. Both parties usually can reach a win-win concept through compromise . However, negotiation cannot resolve all the conflict if one party is unwilling to resolve the problem .

紅字句（原文）
#原文
1Negotiation is a common process in business to mainly solve business conflicts between both parties . Compromise is a basic negotiation state in which both parties give up something that they want in order to get something else they want more. In compromise situations, neither side gets all of what they really want , but they each make concessions in order to reach an agreement that is acceptable to both. Both parties usually can reach a win-win concept through compromise . However, negotiation cannot resolve all the conflict if one party is unwilling to resolve the problem .
#65 Ecology (生態學) #060065 原文
中文翻譯

生態學是研究生物體之間以及生物體與其環境之間交互作用的學科。它致力於理解自然界中的規律（例如生物體在空間和時間上的分布），以及支配這些規律的過程。氣候學是研究大氣層物理狀態的學科——包括大氣的瞬時狀態或天氣現象、季節到年際的變異性、長期平均狀況或氣候，以及氣候如何隨時間變化。這兩個科學研究領域截然不同。生態學是生物科學中的一門學科，其核心原則是自然選擇。氣候學是地球物理科學中的一門學科，以應用物理學和流體動力學為基礎。然而，兩者擁有共同的歷史淵源。

這兩門科學的起源歸功於亞里斯多德和泰奧弗拉斯托斯，以及他們分別撰寫的《氣象學》和《植物探究》，但其現代發展的起點可追溯至博物學與植物地理學。十七、十八和十九世紀的博物學家與地理學家在探索新地區時觀察到植被的變化，並為生態學與氣候學的發展奠定了基礎，因為他們試圖為這些地理規律尋找解釋。亞歷山大·馮·洪堡於十九世紀初觀察到，若氣候相似，相距遙遠的地區會擁有結構和功能相似的植被。阿爾豐斯·德·康多爾假設熱帶、溫帶和北極植被的緯度地帶是由溫度所決定，並於1874年提出了附有相應溫度限制的正式植被地帶劃分。

英文原文

Ecology is the study of interactions of organisms among themselves and with their environment . It seeks to understand patterns in nature (eg, the spatial and temporal distribution of organisms) and the processes governing those patterns. Climatology is the study of the physical state of the atmosphere – its instantaneous state or weather, its seasonal-to-interannual variability, its long- term average condition or climate, and how climate changes over time. These two fields of scientific study are distinctly different . Ecology is a discipline within the biological sciences and has as its core the principle of natural selection. Climatology is a discipline within the geophysical sciences based on applied physics and fluid dynamics. Both, however, share a common history. The origin of these sciences is attributed to Aristotle and Theophrastus and their books Meteorological and Enquiry into Plants, respectively, but their modern beginnings trace back to natural history and plant geography. Seventeenth, eighteenth, and nineteenth century naturalists and geographers saw changes in vegetation as they explored new regions and laid the foundation for the development of ecology and climatology as they sought explanations for these geographic patterns. Alexander von Humboldt, in the early 1800s, observed that widely separated regions have structurally and functionally similar vegetation if their climates are similar. Alphonse de Candolle hypothesized that latitudinal zones of tropical, temperate, and arctic vegetation are caused by temperature and in 1874 proposed formal vegetation zones with associated temperature limits.

#66 Television viewing(小孩看電視) #060066 原文
中文翻譯

父母為何應該管控孩子看電視，又應管控到什麼程度？電視本身當然並無不妥之處。問題在於孩子看了多少電視，以及電視對他的生活產生了什麼影響。研究顯示，隨著看電視的時間增加，孩子花在功課與學習上的時間，以及投入其他重要生活面向（如社交發展和體能活動）的時間，都會隨之減少。

電視必然對孩子產生巨大影響，無論是每週看電視的時數，還是所看的內容皆然。當父母擔憂電視帶來的影響時，應考慮幾個面向：電視在知識與資訊方面能給孩子帶來什麼、這個年齡的孩子每週應該看多少小時的電視、暴力與性的衝擊，以及廣告的影響。

那麼，從整個家庭的角度來看又是如何？電視機是否是你家中的核心家具？是否有人一進空屋就立刻打開電視？白天時電視是否一直開著？電視是否成為你家庭生活中的背景噪音？你是否以自身的收視行為示範，告訴孩子電視應該有所選擇地收看？

英文原文

Why and to what extent should parents control their children’s TV watching? There is certainly nothing inherently wrong with TV . The problem is how much television a child watches and what effect it has on his life . Research has shown that as the amount of time spent watching TV goes up, the amount of time devoted not only to homework and study but other important aspects of life such as social development and physical activities decreases. Television is bound to have it tremendous impact on a child , both in terms of how many hours a week he watches TV and of what he sees. When a parent is concerned about the effects of television, he should consider a number of things: what TV offers the child in terms of information and knowledge, how many hours a week a youngster his age should watch television, the impact of violence and sex, and the influence of commercials. What about the family as a whole ? Is the TV set a central piece of furniture in your home! Is it flicked on the moment someone enters the empty house? Is it on during the daytime? Is it part of the background notice of your family life? Do you demonstrate by your own viewing that television should be watched selectively?

#67 Office Space (辦公室環境) #060067 原文
中文翻譯

辦公空間在促進或抑制工作表現方面具有一定作用，這一觀點有充分的研究支持。哈佛大學與麻薩諸塞州總醫院合作開展的一項研究顯示，改善員工的實體工作環境之所以能提升生產力，並非因為工作環境變得更加美觀，而是因為這些改變讓員工感受到被重視與關懷。一份瑞典研究報告揭示，員工所處的辦公室類型與其整體工作滿意度及健康狀況之間存在密切關聯。此類研究已帶來多項重要發現。盆栽與綠色植物顯然能對心理健康產生實質影響。在獨立辦公室工作的人，健康狀況往往優於在開放式辦公環境工作的員工。充足的光線能降低員工的病假率並提高生產力，而舒適美觀的辦公室則能讓員工感受到更多關懷，從而對公司更加忠誠。上述觀點大多有其合理依據。然而，部分企業並不滿足於僅僅提升員工的健康、生產力與滿足感。谷歌、華特迪士尼與戴森等先驅企業，已嘗試打造能身兼多重功能的辦公空間，從促進員工之間的協作，到激發他們的創意靈感。「環境——無論是實體環境還是文化氛圍——都能成就或埋沒創造力。」《我真希望我在那裡工作！商業領域最具創意空間深度探訪》一書的作者柯斯提·葛羅芙斯如此說道。充滿刺激性的空間能讓人接觸到各種有意設計或隨機出現的刺激元素，以引導人們以不同的方式思考。具有沉思性質的空間則能促進資訊在腦中的沉澱整合，讓思維得以建立連結。一個能鼓勵團隊建立信任、自由發揮的環境，是激發創新不可或缺的關鍵要素。

英文原文

The notion that office space has a role in promoting or inhibiting performance is backed up by solid research . A recent study conducted by Harvard University and Massachusetts General Hospital showed that improvements to the physical surroundings of workers impacted on productivity not because the working environment was more attractive, but because the changes made employees feel cared for. A Swedish research paper revealed a strong link between the type of office an employee worked in and their overall job satisfaction and health . Various findings have emerged as a result of studies such as this. Pot plants and greenery can apparently have a real impact on psychological well-being . Those who work in a private room tend to be in better health than workers based in open-plan offices. Sufficient light can reduce sickness among workers and increase productivity, and an attractive office can make workers feel more cared for and therefore more loyal to their company . Most of these points make good rational sense. But some companies aren’t content simply to increase the health, productivity and contentment of their employees. Pioneers such as Google, Walt Disney and Dyson have tried to create offices that will do everything from promoting collaboration between workers to stimulating their creative juices . "Environment, both physical and cultural, can make or break creativity." says Kursty Groves, author of I Wish I Worked There! A look inside the most creative spaces in business. Stimulating spaces expose the mind to a variety of stimuli - planned or random - In order to encourage people to think differently. Reflective spaces promote the filtering of information into the brain slowing it to make connections. An environment which encourages a team to build trust and to play freely is an essential ingredient for innovation .

#68 Online teaching (在線教育) #060068 原文
中文翻譯

網路教學之所以獨特，在於它以網際網路，尤其是全球資訊網，作為主要的溝通媒介。因此，當你在網路上授課時，你不必身處某個特定地點才能教學。你不必拎著裝滿文件的公事包或筆電趕去教室，不必站在講台前、在黑板上潦草書寫（甚至不必使用高科技的互動式「智慧白板」），也不必在學生考試時悶在一間教室裡批改試卷。你甚至不用坐在辦公室裡等學生來諮詢。你可以在週末或晚餐後舉行「線上辦公室時間」。無論你住在懷俄明州的小鎮還是曼谷這樣的大城市，這一切你都能做到——即便你任職的學院行政辦公室遠在佛羅里達或杜拜。你可以在夏威夷參加一場重要會議的同一天，透過當地咖啡館的無線熱點或飯店房間的高速網路登入，在紐澤西進行你的課程教學。或者，你只需掏出智慧型手機，快速查看學生的最新貼文、電子郵件或簡訊。

網路學習也為學生提供了更多自由。他們可以透過網路搜尋課程，在自己的學校，甚至放眼全球，尋找符合需求的學程、課程與教師。找到合適的課程後，他們可以線上報名註冊、選購教科書、閱讀文章、聆聽講課、繳交作業、與教師討論，並收到最終成績——全部在線上完成。

他們可以組建虛擬教室，與來自不同地區的學生相聚一堂，建立起傳統課堂中不可能形成的連結與友誼——傳統課堂通常只限於特定地理範圍內的學生。

英文原文

What makes teaching online unique is that it uses the Internet, especially the World Wide Web, as the primary means of communication . Thus, when you teach online, you don’t have to be someplace to teach. You don’t have to lug your briefcase full of paper or your laptop to a classroom, stand at a lectern, scribble on a chalkboard (or even use your high-tech, interactive classroom "smart" whiteboard), or grade papers in a stuffy room while your students take a test. You don’t even have to sit in your office waiting for students to show up for conferences. You can hold "office hours" on weekends or at night after dinner. You can do all this while living in a small town in Wyoming or a big city like Bangkok, even if you are working for a college whose administrative office is located in Florida or Dubai. You can attend an important conference in Hawaii on the same day you teach your class in New Jersey, logging on from your laptop via the local café’s wireless hotspot or your hotel room’s high-speed network. Or you may simply pull out your smartphone to quickly check on the latest postings, email, or text messages from students. Online learning offers more freedom for students as well . They can search for courses using the Web, scouring their institution or even the world for programs , classes, and instructors that fit their needs. Having found an appropriate course, they can enroll and register, shop for their books, read articles, listen to lectures, submit their homework assignments, confer with their instructors, and receive their final grades-all online. They can assemble virtual classrooms, joining other students from diverse geographical locales , foraging bonds and friendships not possible in conventional classrooms, which are usually limited to students from a specific geographical area.

#69 Primary carer (初級護工) #060069 原文
中文翻譯

約五分之一（19%）的護工為初級護工（共47萬5千人）。也就是說，他們是某位在行動、溝通或自我照護等核心日常活動方面受到限制者的主要照護者。初級護工與更龐大的其他護工群體（近200萬人）共同為年長者及殘障人士的福祉作出貢獻。然而，由於初級護工所照護的對象若缺乏協助便難以完成基本日常活動，因此各界對初級護工格外關注，包括他們的貢獻、身心狀況、勞動力參與經驗、照護動機，以及所獲得的支持。

與其他護工相比，初級護工更可能協助與自己同住的人（81%對76%）。與整體護工情況相同，成為初級護工的可能性隨年齡增長而提高，在55至64歲時達到高峰，每二十人中即有一人為初級護工。然而，此比例在更年長的群體中並未隨之下降，而是維持在相近的水準。因此，初級護工的年齡結構略比其他護工年長。初級護工的年齡中位數為52歲，而其他護工則為47歲。

與其他護工相比，初級護工更可能為女性（71%對50%），且參與勞動力市場的比例較低（39%對60%）。未參與勞動力市場的女性是初級護工中佔比最高的單一群體（44%）。相較之下，全職受雇男性是其他護工中最大的單一群體（25%）。

由於勞動力參與率較低，初級護工的個人收入也低於其他護工（每週毛收入中位數為237美元，其他護工則為327美元），且更可能以政府退休金或補貼作為主要收入來源（55%對35%）。

英文原文

Slightly less than one in five carers (19%) were primary carers (475,000 people). That is, they were the main carer of a person who was limited in carrying out the core everyday activities of mobility, communication or self-care. Both primary carers and the larger group of other carers (close to 2 million) contribute to the wellbeing of older people and people with disabilities . However, because they care for people who otherwise would have difficulty carrying out basic everyday activities, there is particular interest in primary carers: in the contribution they make, their wellbeing, labor force experiences, motivations and the support they receive in caring. Primary carers were more likely than other carers to be assisting someone who lived in the same household (81% compared with 76%). As with caring as a whole, the likelihood of being a primary carer increased with age to peak at age 55-64 years, where one in twenty people were primary carers. However, rather than then declining, the likelihood of being a primary carer remained at around this level among the older age groups. Consequently, primary carers had a somewhat older age profile than other carers .The median age of primary carers was 52 years, compared with 47 years for other carers. Primary carers were more likely than other carers to be female (71% compared with 50%) and less likely to be in the labor force (39% compared with 60%). Women not in the labor force were by far the largest single group among primary carers (44%). In contrast, men employed full-time were the largest single group among other carers (25%). Consistent with their lower labor force participation, primary carers had lower personal incomes than other carers (a median gross income of $237 per week compared with $327 per week) and were more likely to have a government pension or allowance as their main source of income (55% compared with 35%).

#70 South Africa (南非) #060070 原文
中文翻譯

現今南非所在的地區，數千年來一直有人類居住。
桑人是這片土地上最早的原住民，他們是遊牧民族，以約 15 至 20 人為單位組成小型群體生活。
他們靠捕魚、打獵以及採集根莖與其他野生食物維生。 他們不建造永久性住所，而是以岩石洞穴作為臨時棲身之所。
大約 2,000 年前，科伊科伊牧民遷徙至沿海地區。 在現今南非東部，使用鐵器的社會可追溯至約公元 300 年。索托-茨瓦納人與恩古尼人
大約在公元 1,200 年前後遷入這一地區。
他們以農耕與畜牧為生，開採黃金、銅與錫礦，獵取象牙，並建造以石牆圍起的城鎮。數百年來，這些社會與科伊桑人之間有著多元的往來接觸。
桑人與科伊科伊人因爭奪獵物資源而產生衝突，最終科伊科伊人取得主導地位。 這些民族居住在現今南非西部，統稱為科伊桑人。

英文原文

The area that is now South Africa has been inhabited by humans for millennia. The San, the original inhabitants of this land, were migratory people who lived in small groups of about 15 to 20 people. They survived by fishing and hunting and by gathering roots and other wild foods . They did not build permanent dwellings but used rock shelters as temporary dwellings. Around 2,000 years ago Khoikhoi pastoralists migrated to the coast . In the eastern part of present-day South Africa, iron-working societies date from about 300 AD. The Sotho-Tswana and Nguni peoples arrived in this region around 1,200 AD . They lived by agriculture and stock farming, mined gold, copper and tin and hunted for ivory and built stone-walled towns. Over the centuries, these societies had diverse contacts with the Khoisan. Strife between the San and the Khoikhoi developed over competition for game; eventually the Khoikhoi became dominant . These peoples lived in the western part of present-day South Africa and are known collectively as the Khoisan .

4Strife between the San and the Khoikhoi developed over competition for game; eventually the Khoikhoi became dominant . These peoples lived in the western part of present-day South Africa and are known collectively as the Khoisan .
#71 IBM (IBM) #060071 原文
中文翻譯

說到預測，請記住，IBM 董事長曾在五〇年代預言全世界最多只需要大約六台電腦；英國教育部似乎在八〇年代認為我們所有人都需要學會用 BASIC 編程；而微軟在九〇年代未能預見網際網路的迅猛發展。

誰能預料到，汽車帶來的一個主要影響竟是讓全國各地的小店紛紛破產？

早期的電話開發者是否曾預見到，電話會發展成一種人與人之間點對點的通訊媒介，而非廣播形式的傳播工具？

我們所有人，包括那些「專家」，似乎都特別不擅長預測自身技術的可能發展走向，哪怕只是預測到明年。當然，我們可以嘗試從過去技術的經驗中進行推斷，就如我在下文所做的，將網際網路技術與其他資訊及通訊技術的發展相比較，並審視廣播與印刷技術早期的發展歷程。

但我這樣做是否站得住腳，仍是一個開放性的問題。 你或許會覺得英法兩國的視訊文字系統——Prestel 與 Minitel——的歷史頗具參考價值。

然而，我並不完全確信它們有多大的相關性，也不知道你能在哪裡找到有關它們的線上資料，因此，與其在此佔用篇幅，我已在另一篇獨立文章中對它們作了簡要介紹。

英文原文

As far as prediction is concerned, remember that the chairman of IBM predicted in the fifties that the world would need a maximum of around half a dozen computers, that the British Department for Education seemed to think in the eighties that we would all need to be able to code in BASIC and that in the nineties Microsoft failed to foresee the rapid growth of the Internet. Who could have predicted that one major effect of the automobile would be to bankrupt small shops across the nation? Could the early developers of the telephone have foreseen its development as a medium for person to person communication, rather than as a form of broadcasting medium? We all, including the 'experts', seem to be peculiarly inept at predicting the likely development of our technologies , even as far as the next year. We can, of course, try to extrapolate from experience of previous technologies , as I do below by comparing the technology of the Internet with the development of other information and communication technologies and by examining the earlier development of radio and print. But how justified I might be in doing so remains an open question . You might conceivably find the history of the British and French videotext systems, Prestel and Minitel, instructive. However, I am not entirely convinced that they are very relevant, nor do I know where you can find information about them online, so, rather than take up space here, I've briefly described them in a separate article.

#72 Australian voting (澳洲投票) #060072 原文
中文翻譯

一個民主國家應該有權決定是否投票。奇怪的是，在澳洲人爬了幾十年的美國政治後背之後，澳洲人卻沒有這種權利。因為不投票而被罰款，讓我想起那句老話：「你可以把馬牽到水邊，但你無法強迫牠喝水。」

罰款的對象不是沒有投票的人，而是沒有在名單上劃掉自己名字的人！強迫人們做出決定，只會讓他們做出最省事、最快速的選擇，而不是最好的選擇。強制投票要能發揮作用，需要一個有充分認識的選民群體。

然而，現實是沒有人真正了解候選人，競選資料也不容易取得。我寧願有八成的人不去投票，也不願他們全部只是在選票上隨便圈一個最眼熟的名字。這樣至少政府是由那兩成關心政治、做出明智決定的人所選出來的。否則，誰當選在很大程度上只是碰運氣。

此外，強制投票並不能確保全體選民真正參與民主進程。那些不想投票的人，大可以出現、讓名字被劃掉，甚至連鉛筆都不用碰一下。但如果你真的以為那些不在乎政治的人出現在投票所時都是這樣做的，那你就是在嚴重自欺欺人了。自願投票至少能確保，去投票的人都是真正在乎投票這件事的人。

或許有人可以告訴我，就我所知，為什麼澳洲是唯一實行強制投票的「民主」國家。強制投票在美國、英國、加拿大、紐西蘭、菲律賓，或任何我所知道的其他歐洲或亞洲民主國家，肯定都不是強制性的。然而，強制投票在大多數共產政權中卻是必行之制。

英文原文

A democratic country should have the right to decide whether to vote or not . It is strange that after decades of crawling up the political backside of the US, Australians don't have that right . Being fined for not voting reminds me of the old saying "you can lead a horse to water but you cannot make him drink". The fine is not for failing to vote but for failing to have your name marked off a list! Forcing people to make a decision just means they'll make the easiest, quickest decision they can, not the best one. You need an informed electorate for compulsory voting to work. However, the reality is that nobody knows anything about the candidates and promotional material is not readily available . I'd rather 80% of people didn't vote than have them all just pick the first recognizable name on the ballot sheet. Then at least the government is elected by the 20% who care and make informed decisions. Otherwise it is largely pot chance who gets elected. Furthermore, compulsory voting doesn't ensure that the entire electorate is engaged in the democratic process . Those who don't want to vote can simply turn up and get their name marked off, without even putting pencil to paper. But you're seriously deluding yourself if you think that this is what all those who don't care about government do when they turn up to the polling booth. Voluntary voting at least ensures those who vote are the ones that care enough to do so . Perhaps somebody could enlighten me as to the reason why, to the best of my knowledge, Australia is the only 'democracy' that has compulsory voting. It is certainly not compulsory in the USA, England, Canada, New Zealand, Philippines or any other European or Asian democracy that I am aware of. Compulsory voting is, however, mandatory in most communist regimes.

#73 Guinness (吉尼斯紀錄) #060073 原文
中文翻譯

昨天，吉尼斯世界紀錄在國家海事博物館頒發了一項相當不尋常的獎項。經過100天的測試，這座被稱為「時鐘B」的計時器——為防止人為干預而被密封在透明塑膠箱中——被吉尼斯官方正式認定為世界上「在自由空氣中擺動的擺錘機械鐘中最為精準的時鐘」。
這已是一項引人入勝的獎項。但真正令人驚嘆的是，這座時鐘的設計者距今已逾250年，他當年因「近乎精神失常症狀的語無倫次與荒謬絕倫」而飽受嘲弄，其鐘錶設計方案更被塵封了兩個世紀之久。

這些嘲弄皆指向約翰·哈里森——這位英國鐘錶匠憑藉其航海天文鐘，徹底革新了18世紀的航海事業（他亦是達娃·索貝爾所著《經度》一書的主角）。他隨後聲稱，自己將製造出一座擺錘計時器，能在100天內將誤差控制在一秒以內——此言一出，引發廣泛嘲笑。眾人皆認定，這根本是不可能完成的任務。

然而如今，笑到最後的是哈里森。在昨日於格林威治舉行的「哈里森解碼：邁向完美擺鐘」研討會上，天文台科學家揭露，一座完全按照哈里森設計規格製作的時鐘，在官方測試中持續運行100天，期間僅誤差八分之五秒。

英文原文

One of Guinness World Records’ more unusual awards was presented at the National Maritime Museum yesterday. After a 100-day trial, the timepiece known as Clock B – which had been sealed in a clear plastic box to prevent tampering – was officially declared, by Guinness, to be the world’s "most accurate mechanical clock with a pendulum swinging in free air" . It was an intriguing enough award. But what is really astonishing is that the clock was designed more than 250 years ago by a man who was derided at the time for "an incoherence and absurdity that was little short of the symptoms of insanity", and whose plans for the clock lay ignored for two centuries . The derision was poured on John Harrison, the British clockmaker whose marine chronometers had revolutionized seafaring in the 18th century (and who was the subject of Longitude by Dava Sobel). His subsequent claim – that he would go on to make a pendulum timepiece that was accurate to within a second over a 100-day period – triggered widespread ridicule. The task was simply impossible, it was declared. But now the last laugh lies with Harrison . At a conference, Harrison Decoded: Towards a Perfect Pendulum Clock, held at Greenwich yesterday, observatory scientists revealed that a clock that had been built to the clockmaker’s exact specifications had run for 100 days during official tests and had lost only five-eighths of a second in that period.

#74 Eat of Animals (肉食者) #060074 原文
中文翻譯

珀西·雪萊在1813年預言，終有一天，「壟斷性的食肉者將不再以一頓飯消耗一英畝土地來毀損自己的體魄」。他解釋道：「用來催肥一頭牛軀體的大量植物性營養物質，若直接從大地母懷中採取，可提供十倍的食物供給。」

兩百年後，主流農學家和營養學家終於趕上了這位詩人的見解。越來越多的科學共識認為，以穀物和豆類餵養動物是一種低效且奢侈的人類糧食生產方式，牧草地的數量有限，世界將難以為預測中90億的人口提供與當今工業化世界同等豐富的肉食飲食，而且這種飲食本身也並不健康。

除此之外，牲畜對全球暖化也有顯著貢獻，根據聯合國一項廣為引用的估計，牲畜產生了全球人為溫室氣體排放量的14.5%。既然問題已被確認，挑戰在於如何說服富裕國家的人們少吃肉。

這看似是一項艱鉅的任務，但各國政府已成功透過公共資訊宣導、法規管制與稅收課徵的組合手段，說服人們戒菸。

英文原文

A day would come, Percy Shelley predicted in 1813, when "the monopolizing eater of animal flesh would no longer destroy his constitution by eating an acre at a meal". He explained: "The quantity of nutritious vegetable matter consumed in fattening the carcass of an ox would afford 10 times the sustenance if gathered immediately from the bosom of the earth." Two hundred years later, mainstream agronomists and dietitians have caught up with the poet. A growing scientific consensus agrees that feeding cereals and beans to animals is an inefficient and extravagant way to produce human food , that there is a limited amount of grazing land, that the world will be hard-pressed to supply a predicted population of 9 billion people with a diet as rich in meat as the industrialized world currently enjoys, and that it's not a very healthy diet anyway. On top of this, livestock contribute significantly towards global warming , generating 14·5% of all manmade greenhouse gas emissions, according to one much-quoted estimate from the United Nations. Now that the problem has been identified, the challenge is to persuade people in wealthy countries to eat less meat . That might seem a tall order, but governments have successfully persuaded people to quit smoking through a combination of public information, regulation and taxation .

#75 Hookham Bookstore (書店) #060075 原文
中文翻譯

HOOKHAM AND CARPENTER書商（以下簡稱「Hookham」）位於倫敦新龐德街，其帳冊記錄橫跨了十八世紀政治最動盪的十年——1790年代。常光顧Hookham的顧客主要來自貴族或紳士階層。事實上，在Hookham的全部買家中，有22%為貴族，而其中35%的貴族（共214位顧客）購買了小說。我們也可以有把握地推測，無封號的女性顧客屬於紳士階層的收入水準，因為她們的住址主要位於倫敦時髦的「西區」。

Hookham的帳簿不僅揭示了與早期有關省級女性的研究相比，女性小說購買者的比例有大幅增加，還揭示出女性購買由女性所著小說的比例也有顯著增長。

這一顯著的增長說明，Hookham有閒暇的女性顧客能夠購買更多小說。此外，這些貴族及紳士階層的女性以自己的名義開立帳戶，而非以丈夫之名，這一事實表明，相較於省級女性，這些城市富裕女性擁有更高程度的自主性與獨立性。然而，由於我們的研究未涵蓋對男性顧客的審視，我們在聲稱這些女性是否符合「女性是十八世紀小說主要消費者」這一刻板印象方面，能夠提出的論點極為有限。

此外，儘管更多的可支配收入和閒暇時間確實解釋了1790年代女性購買由女性所著小說的顯著增長，但這一增長也強烈表明，女性讀者渴望參與這個充滿政治張力的時代。因此，閱讀小說為女性讀者提供了一種途徑，使她們得以參與由男性主導的政治世界。

英文原文

THE BOOKSELLERS OF HOOKHAM AND CARPENTER (hereafter referred to only as ‘Hookham’) were located on New Bond Street in London, and their records span the most politically turbulent decade of the eighteenth-century – the 1790s. Clients who frequented Hookham were primarily from the aristocratic or gentry classes. In fact, of Hookham’s total buyers, 22% were aristocracy and 35% (214 customers) of the aristocracy purchased novels. We can also confidently assume that untitled female customers were of gentry income, because their addresses were primarily in London’s fashionable ‘West End’. Hookham’s ledgers not only reveal a dramatic increase in the proportion of female purchasers of novels by comparison to earlier studies of provincial women , but they also reveal a remarkable increase in the proportion of female purchases of novels authored by females. Such a marked increase illustrates that Hookham’s leisured female customers were able to buy more novels. Furthermore, the fact that these female aristocrats and gentry have accounts under their own name , not their husbands’, demonstrates the greater degree of agency and independence that these urban, moneyed women had relative to provincial women . However, because our study does not include an examination of male customers, we are very limited in what claims we can make about whether or not these women behaved according to the cliché that women were the predominant consumers of novels in the eighteenth-century. Moreover, while more disposable income and leisure time certainly accounts for the significant increase in female purchases of novels authored by women in the 1790s, this increase also strongly suggests a desire on the part of women readers to engage in this politically charged decade . Thus, novel-reading provided women readers with the means through which they were able to participate in the male-dominated world of politics .

#76 Autism (自閉症) #060076 原文
中文翻譯

自閉症是一種以溝通障礙、社交互動缺陷及重複性行為為特徵的疾患。
在過去40年間，自閉症的測量盛行率大約增加了10倍。雖然在了解與風險增加及盛行率上升相關的部分因素方面已有所進展，但目前沒有人確切知道自閉症的成因，也不知道是什麼導致自閉症盛行率如此急遽攀升。

然而，學界日益意識到，僅聚焦於個人風險因素——例如接觸毒性物質、產前併發症或父母教育程度——不足以解釋自閉症盛行率何以增長得如此驚人。社會與制度性過程很可能扮演著重要角色。

舉例而言，診斷標準的變化，以及投入自閉症診斷的資源大量湧入，可能是理解盛行率上升的關鍵。意識的提升與社會影響已被視為自閉症及各種類似疾患盛行率上升的相關因素，在這些案例中，社會過程模仿了傳染效應。

研究已針對診斷標準變化及診斷替代效應對自閉症盛行率上升的貢獻進行了檢視，但制度性因素、診斷資源，以及更廣泛的社會意識，至今尚未獲得系統性的評估。然而，社會學文獻中關於健康與不平等的研究，為探討個人層面與社區層面的效應如何共同形塑自閉症診斷的可能性，提供了充分的研究動機。

英文原文

Autism is a disorder characterized by impairments in communication, social interaction, and repetitive behaviors. Over the past 40 years, the measured prevalence of autism has multiplied roughly 10-fold. While progress has been made in understanding some of the factors associated with increased risk and rising prevalence, no one knows with certainty what causes autism or what caused autism prevalence to rise so precipitously. There is , however, a growing awareness among scholars that focusing solely on individual risk factors such as exposure toxicants, prenatal complications, or parental education is insufficient to explain why autism prevalence rates have increased so stunningly. Social and institutional processes likely play an important role . For example, changes in diagnostic criteria and an influx of resources dedicated to autism diagnosis may be critical to understanding why prevalence rates have risen. Increased awareness and social influence have been implicated in the rise of autism and a variety of comparable disorders, where social processes mimic the effects of contagion. Studies have examined the contribution of changes in diagnostic criteria and diagnostic substitution to rising autism prevalence rates, but the importance of institutional factors, resources for diagnosis, and greater awareness have not been systematically assessed. The sociological literature on health and inequality, however, provides substantial motivation for exploring how individual- and community- level effects operate to shape the likelihood of an autism diagnosis .

2There is , however, a growing awareness among scholars that focusing solely on individual risk factors such as exposure toxicants, prenatal complications, or parental education is insufficient to explain why autism prevalence rates have increased so stunningly. Social and institutional processes likely play an important role .
3greater awareness have not been systematically assessed. The sociological literature on health and inequality, however, provides substantial motivation for exploring how individual- and community- level effects operate to shape the likelihood of an autism diagnosis .
#77 Africa (非洲發展潛力) #060077 原文
中文翻譯

非洲在國際上所受到的負面印象，對那些在發展上實際表現良好的非洲國家而言是非常不公平的，因為這片大陸擁有五十多個國家，蘊藏著尚未完全開發的豐富自然資源與多元文化，而勤勞的非洲人正努力應對貧困、疾病與戰爭等問題，因此若能獲得國際社會的共同支持與援助，非洲可以成為商業發展與文化旅遊的理想之地。這種偏頗的觀感忽視了這片大陸充滿活力的現實與巨大潛力。

非洲擁有巨大潛力，多年前便已為部分企業帶來了豐厚利益。歷史上的商業合作已證明，具有前瞻思維的企業能夠在此取得成功。事實上，非洲是投資回報率最高的地區。這裡是投資者與探險者的樂土，但仍需要國際援助。與非洲人做生意是有益的，因為雙方都能獲得財務收益，並享有長期的成長前景。此外，超越商業層面，非洲同樣美麗動人，擁有壯闊的自然景觀與豐富的文化遺產，使其成為文化旅遊的頂級目的地，為訪客帶來深刻難忘的體驗。

然而，若要誠實地談論非洲，就必須正視其所面臨的種種困境。非洲飽受頻繁戰亂之苦，其成因錯綜複雜，根植於歷史遺留問題與資源爭奪，而非其人民的任何固有特質。非洲人清楚知道自身發展所需，但在技術轉讓、基礎設施融資及能力建設等領域仍需要外部協助。

英文原文

The negative impression of Africa held internationally is very unfair to those African countries that are actually doing well in their development , because this continent has more than 50 countries rich in natural resources which have not been completely exploited and cultural diversity, and hardworking Africans are struggling to address issues of poverty, disease and war, so Africa can be an attractive place for business development and cultural tourism if concerted international support and assistance are provided. This skewed perception overlooks the vibrant reality and immense potential of the continent. Africa has a lot of potential, and years ago it brought benefits to some companies . Historical engagements have proven that forward-thinking businesses can find success. In fact, Africa is the region with the best investment returns. It is a paradise for investors and adventurers, but it still needs international aid. It is good to do business with Africans because of the mutual money and long-term growth prospects. Furthermore, beyond business, Africa is also beautiful, boasting landscapes and cultural heritage that make it a premier destination for cultural tourism, offering profound experiences for visitors. However, to discuss Africa honestly, one must also acknowledge its struggles . Africa suffers from frequent wars and the causes are complex, rooted in historical legacies and competition over resources , not in any inherent trait of its people. Africans know what is needed in their development but need assistance in areas like technology transfer, infrastructure financing, and capacity building .

#78 Honey (蜜蜂的好處) #060078 原文
中文翻譯

根據 Ron Fessenden 醫學博士、公共衛生碩士的研究，美國人平均每年消耗超過 150 磅的精製糖，另外還要再加上 62 磅的高果糖玉米糖漿。相較之下，美國人平均每年只攝取約 1.3 磅的蜂蜜。

根據最新研究，如果你能將精製糖的攝取改換成純天然原蜜，對健康帶來的益處將會是巨大的。

什麼是原蜜？它是蜜蜂以花蜜為原料所製成的純淨、未過濾、未殺菌的天然甜味劑。現今市面上大多數的蜂蜜都是經過加熱與過濾處理的加工蜂蜜。與加工蜂蜜不同，原蜜不會流失其驚人的營養價值與對健康的功效。

原蜜有哪些功效？它幾乎可以幫助改善從體力不足、睡眠問題到季節性過敏等各種狀況。與含糖或高果糖玉米糖漿的飲食相比，改用原蜜甚至有助於減重。我很高興今天能向你進一步介紹這款我最喜愛的天然甜味劑之一，希望能說服你多吃蜂蜜、少吃糖。

英文原文

According to Dr· Ron Fessenden, MD, MPH, the average American consumes more than 150 pounds of refined sugar, plus an additional 62 pounds of high fructose corn syrup every year. In comparison, we consume only around 1·3 pounds of honey per year on average in the U·S. According to new research, if you can switch out your intake of refined sugar and use pure raw honey instead, the health benefits can be enormous . What is raw honey? It’s a pure, unfiltered and unpasteurized sweetener made by bees from the nectar of flowers . Most of the honey consumed today is processed honey that’s been heated and filtered since it was gathered from the hive. Unlike processed honey, raw honey does not get robbed of its incredible nutritional value and health powers . What are some of the benefits of raw honey ? It can help with everything from low energy to sleep problems to seasonal allergies . Switching to raw honey may even help weight-loss efforts when compared to diets containing sugar or high fructose corn syrup. I’m excited to tell you more about one of my all-time favorite natural sweeteners today, which I hope will convince you to eat honey more and sugar less.

#79 Plunging oil price (油價下降) #060079 原文
中文翻譯

近幾個月來，油價的急劇下跌已將英國通膨率拖低至零。但分析師表示，零售價格的下跌不能僅僅歸因於石油。

折扣零售商持續從傳統行業巨頭手中搶奪市場份額，在食品和非食品市場中均佔據了更大的份額。正如零售分析師尼克·巴布所指出的，「大型超市不得不以降低自家『宰客』價格來應對這一局面」。其結果是整個零售業的收銀台結帳價格全面下降。

網路零售商的崛起也帶動了價格下降，部分原因在於消費者可以輕易比較價格，一旦在競爭對手網站上發現更便宜的商品，便可立即轉往他處購買。據零售分析師理查德·海曼表示，零售商也不願在實體店和網路商店提供不同的價格，這意味著商家被迫在高街上削價競爭。

海曼先生認為，門市種類的不斷擴張也是原因之一。「產能過剩是影響價格的最大問題，」他說。「過去十年間，僅網路購物一項就增加了相當於一億一千萬平方英尺的交易空間——這大約相當於六十五座西田倫敦購物中心的額外面積。零售商供給的增加，在需求毫無增長的情況下，已使整個行業嚴重供過於求。」

英文原文

A plunging oil price has dragged UK inflation to zero over recent months. But analysts say the fall in retail prices cannot solely be attributed to oil . Discount retailers continue to steal market share from established industry giants , taking an increased chunk of both food and non-food markets. And, as retail analyst Nick Bubb notes, "the big supermarkets have had to respond to this by bringing down their own ‘rip off’ prices". The result is a sector-wide fall in prices paid at the till . The growth of online retailers has also brought prices down , in part due to the ease with which customers can compare prices and purchase goods elsewhere if they find an item cheaper on a competitor’s site. Retailers are also reluctant to offer different prices in their physical and online stores, according to retail analyst Richard Hyman, which means shops are forced to cut prices on the high street. An ever-expanding range of shops is also to blame , according to Mr· Hyman. "Overcapacity is the biggest of the issues affecting prices," he says. "In the last 10 years, online alone has added the equivalent of 110m square feet of trading space — that’s roughly equal to 65 additional Westfield London shopping malls. An increase in supply of retailers, with no increase in demand, has left the industry massively oversupplied."

#80 Songbirds (唱歌的小鳥) #060080 原文
中文翻譯

研究人員指出，針對雄性鳴禽已有大量研究，但對雌鳥鳴唱行為的了解卻相當有限。傳統觀點認為，雄鳥鳴唱是為了吸引雌鳥，因此雌鳥幾乎沒有鳴唱的理由。然而，研究團隊也指出，2013年一項由國際研究人員進行的先期研究顯示，約有71%的雌性鳴禽確實會鳴唱——只是方式和原因與雄鳥有所不同。

在這項最新研究中，研究人員試圖進一步了解雌性超凡仙鷦鷯為何鳴唱，以及何時鳴唱，並探究此舉是否會給牠們帶來問題，例如引來天敵。他們在澳洲野外72個巢址附近設立監測站，對這些鳥類進行了長達兩年的活動記錄。在研究雌雄鳥的行為時，研究人員發現雌鳥通常只有在伴侶鳴唱後才會回應——這種鳥是一夫一妻制的。雄鳥從覓食返巢時會以鳴唱宣告自身存在，雌鳥則以相同的歌聲回應，只是聲量較為低沉。研究人員指出，配對之間的對唱在築巢期間最為頻繁。為了探究雌鳥的回應是否會危及鳥蛋或雛鳥，研究團隊設置了放有鵪鶉蛋的人工鳥巢，播放雌鳥的鳴唱聲，並調整每小時的鳴叫頻率。當每小時鳴唱次數設為20次時，天敵取食鳥蛋的機率為40%；但當每小時設為6次時，機率僅為20%，這顯示雌鳥的鳴唱確實會對後代造成風險。研究人員據此推測，演化的機制或許並非在選擇強化雄性鳴禽的鳴唱能力，而是實際上一直在抑制雌性的鳴唱。

英文原文

Much study has been conducted regarding male songbirds, the researchers note, but little research has been done to better understand singing in female birds. Traditionally, the thinking has been that males sing to attract the females; thus females have little to no reason to sing. But, as the group also note, a prior study by an international team of researchers back in 2013 showed that approximately 71 percent of female songbirds sing—they just don't do it in the same ways or for the same reasons. In this new effort, the researchers sought to learn more about why female superb fairy wrens sing and when, and if it causes problems for them, such as attracting predators. They set up monitoring stations near 72 nesting sites in the wilds of Australia, home to the birds, and recorded their activities over a two-year period. In studying the behaviour of both the males and females, the researchers found that the females generally only sang in response to singing from their mate—the birds are monogamous . Males announced their presence when returning to the nest from foraging, the females replied with the same song, though it was muted. The back and forth sing-song between mated pairs was more prominent, the researchers noted, during nest building. To find out if the female returning the call put her eggs or chicks at risk, the team set up some artificial nests with quail eggs in them and played female songs from them, varying the number of calls per hour. Predators ate the eggs 40 percent of the time when the song rate was set at 20 songs per hour, but only did so 20 percent of the time when it was set at 6 calls per hour, showing that such calling did indeed put the offspring at risk . These findings, the researchers propose, suggest that it might be possible that evolution, rather than selecting for male songbird singing, has actually been selecting against female singing .

2that the females generally only sang in response to singing from their mate—the birds are monogamous . Males announced their presence when returning to the nest from foraging, the females
3time when it was set at 6 calls per hour, showing that such calling did indeed put the offspring at risk . #81 Geothermal energy (地熱能) #060081 原文
中文翻譯

對於那些能源需求不斷增加、飽受頻繁停電困擾、又無力在國際石油市場上競爭的國家，解決方案是什麼？至少就東非而言，專家認為地熱能是答案。更令人振奮的是，肯亞政府和國際投資者似乎正在傾聽這個聲音。許多人認為這正逢其時，因為有關嚴峻能源危機的說法正四處流傳，原因在於高油價、人口激增以及乾旱問題。
地熱能的運作原理是將水抽入基岩，水在那裡被加熱後以蒸汽形式返回地表，蒸汽可直接用作熱能來源，或用來驅動發電。資料來源：
美國能源信息署，《美國西部及夏威夷的地熱能》。

目前肯亞超過60%的電力來自水力發電，但隨著不規律的降雨模式加劇了季節性變化問題，水力發電的可靠性正日益下降。替代能源已刻不容緩；肯亞的主要能源供應商——肯亞發電公司（KenGen）希望在2020年前將地熱能源在其總用電量中的佔比從13%提升至25%。該地區地熱能的潛力最初由聯合國開發計畫署在國際層面發現，當時地質學家觀察到東非裂谷系統地下存在熱異常現象。當地居民數百年來一直善加利用這項資源；他們利用蒸汽孔為溫室創造理想的濕度，或只是在眾多天然溫泉湖中享受游泳的樂趣。

沿著從紅海延伸至莫三比克、全長6000公里的裂谷，研究人員進行了地球化學、地球物理及熱流量測量，以找出適合鑽鑿地熱井的區域。其中一處地點毗鄰已熄滅的奧爾卡里亞火山，位於地獄之門國家公園內，其地下擁有地球上最薄的大陸地殼之一。

這是地殼因板塊拉張而變薄的結果，導致地球表面以下較熱的物質上湧，從而形成更高的溫度。這層薄地殼非常適合鑽鑿地熱井，井深可達約3000公尺，該深度的溫度高達342°C，遠高於此深度通常90°C的正常溫度。周圍岩石中的水受熱轉化為蒸汽，蒸汽可用來驅動渦輪機發電。

英文原文

What is the solution for nations with increasing energy demands, hindered by frequent power cuts and an inability to compete in the international oil market? For East Africa at least, experts think geothermal energy is the answer . More promising still, the Kenyan government and international investors seem to be listening . This is just in time according to many, as claims of an acute energy crisis are afoot due to high oil prices, population spikes and droughts . Geothermal energy works by pumping water into bedrock, where it is heated and returns to the surface as steam which is used directly as a heat source or to drive electricity production. Source: Energy Information Administration, Geothermal Energy in the Western United States and Hawaii . Currently over 60% of Kenya’s power comes from hydroelectric sources but these are proving increasingly unreliable as the issue of seasonal variation is intensified by erratic rain patterns . Alternative energy sources are needed; and the leading energy supplier in Kenya, Kenya Electricity Generating Company (KenGen), hopes to expand its geothermal energy supply from 13% to 25 % of its total usage by 2020 . The potential of geothermal energy in the region was first realized internationally by the United Nations Development Program, when geologists observed thermal anomalies below the East African Rift system . Locals have been utilizing this resource for centuries; using steam vents to create the perfect humidity for greenhouses, or simply to enjoy a swim in the many natural hot lakes . Along the 6000 km of the rift from the Red Sea to Mozambique, geochemical, geophysical and heat flow measurements were made to identify areas suitable for geothermal wells . One area lies next to the extinct Olkaria volcano, within the Hell’s Gate National Park, and sits over some of the thinnest continental crust on Earth . This is a result of the thinning of the crust by tectonic stretching, causing hotter material below the Earth’s surface to rise, resulting in higher temperatures . This thin crust was ideal for the drilling of geothermal wells, reaching depths of around 3000 m, where temperatures get up to 342°C, far higher than the usual temperature of 90°C at this depth . Water in the surrounding rocks is converted to steam by the heat. The steam can be used to drive turbines and produce electricity.

#82 Assessment (評估) #060082 原文
中文翻譯

評估是教育中的核心過程。如果學生能學會所教的內容，我們就根本不需要評估；只需記錄我們教了什麼就夠了。

但正如每位老師所知，許多學生並未學會所教的內容。事實上，當我們看他們的作業時，有時很難相信他們真的在課堂上聽過課。

實際上，我們無法確切預測學生在一系列特定課堂活動後究竟會學到什麼。而且，若不了解學生的起點，我們就無法有效教學，因此必須進行評估。即使所有學生都從同一起點出發（這種情況極為罕見），在很短的時間內，每位學生對所學材料也會形成不同的理解。

這就是為什麼評估是教學與學習之間的橋梁——只有透過評估，我們才能了解課堂中所發生的一切是否產生了我們預期的學習效果。

當然，評估在教育中也用於其他目的，這使得整體情況更加複雜。

在所有國家，對個別學生表現的評估被用來決定哪些學生具備、哪些學生不具備進入後續教育階段的資格，同時也用於決定學生應接受哪種類型的教育。

英文原文

Assessment is a central process in education . If students learned what they were taught, we would never need to assess; we could instead just keep records of what we had taught. But as every teacher knows, many students do not learn what they are taught . Indeed, when we look at their work, it is sometimes hard to believe that they were in the classroom. In fact, it is impossible to predict with any certainty what students will learn as the result of a particular sequence of classroom activities . And because we cannot teach well without finding out where our students are starting from, we have to assess. Even if all our students started out at the same point (a highly unlikely situation), each of them will have reached different understandings of the material being studied within a very short period of time. That is why assessment is the bridge between teaching and learning —it is only through assessment that we can find out whether what has happened in the classroom has produced the learning we intended. Of course, assessment is also used for other purposes in education , which makes the picture much more complicated. In all countries, assessments of the performance of individual students are used to determine which students are, and which students are not, qualified for subsequent phases of education, and also to decide which kinds of education students should receive.
