#83 Muggy weather (悶熱的天氣) #060083 原文
中文翻譯

**什麼讓天氣感覺悶熱？**

和熱指數一樣，「悶熱」是一種「體感」狀態，只不過它更關乎空氣「是否好呼吸」的感受，而非單純的炎熱程度。

天氣越悶熱，你越難感到涼爽，原因在於蒸發速率下降。這也是為什麼以下幾種天氣條件都與最悶熱的白天和夜晚密切相關：氣溫偏高（一般在華氏 70 度以上，氣溫越高，空氣所能容納的水分就越多）；濕度高（空氣中水分越多，感覺就越「沉重」）；以及風速低（風越小，流經皮膚、協助蒸發散熱的空氣分子就越少）。

由於悶熱程度反映的是空氣濕潤的感受，你或許會認為相對濕度是衡量戶外悶熱程度的好指標。

然而，露點溫度其實是衡量悶熱程度更好的指標。

為什麼呢？露點不僅能反映空氣的濕潤程度，還能反映溫度的高低——因為露點溫度最高只能等於、永遠不會超過實際氣溫。

因此，若露點偏高，往往代表空氣濕度和氣溫也同樣偏高。

英文原文

What Makes It Muggy? Like the heat index, muggy is a "feels-like" condition , except it has to do more with how "breathable" the air feels than how hot it feels. The muggier the weather, the less chance you'll feel cool because of decreased evaporation rates , which is why the following weather conditions are notoriously linked to the muggiest of days and nights: Warm air temperatures, generally of 70°F or above (the warmer the air, the more moisture it's able to hold); High moisture (the more moisture there is in the air, the "heavier" it feels); and Low winds (the less wind there is, the fewer air molecules there are passing over your skin evaporating and cooling you off). Since mugginess expresses how moist the air feels, you might think that relative humidity would be a good indicator of how muggy it feels outside. However, dewpoint temperature is actually a better measure of mugginess . Why? Dewpoint not only gives you an indication of how moist air is, but how warm it is as well (since dew point temperature can go as high as, but never higher than the actual air temperature). So if the dew point is high, it means both air moisture and temperature probably are, too .

#84 Eating history (飲食曆史) #060084 原文
中文翻譯

在過去兩個世紀裡，食物與飲食在澳洲大眾意識中所扮演的角色發生了深刻的變化。公眾對食物的討論，在很大程度上僅限於供應、分配與價格等問題。進入十九世紀末，部分報紙開始定期刊登關於家政主題的專欄建議，包括菜單規劃與食譜。然而，飲食基本上仍屬私人活動，即便是與他人共餐時亦然。

到了二十世紀末，食物與飲食已成為顯著的公眾關注焦點。這場深刻的文化重估有大量佐證。例如在書店裡，烹飪及一切與之相關的書籍往往佔據較大的陳列空間。市面上也出現了各種專賣店，販售各式各樣的廚具、餐具，以及其他與飲食相關的周邊用品。

或許最能說明問題的，是大眾媒體名人現象的延伸——烹飪界人士也躋身其中。學界同樣趕上了商品化的潮流。如今，美食學學位似乎正在複製1980年代MBA的熱潮，食物也已成為哲學家、社會學家、歷史學家、文化理論家、生態學家及眾多學者競相探討的正當研究課題。

然而，令人意外的是，這個問題對大多數歷史學家而言似乎幾乎毫無吸引力。近兩個世紀以來，他們在書寫殖民與建國的歷史時，對於移民及其後代如何餵飽自己這一問題，幾乎鮮有著墨。

英文原文

In the past two centuries there has been a dramatic change in the role of food and eating in Australian public consciousness . Public discussion of food was largely confined to matters of supply, distribution and price. Towards the end of the nineteenth century some newspapers were offering regular columns of advice on housekeeping topics, including menu planning and recipes. However, eating remained essentially a private activity , even when undertaken in company. By the late twentieth century, food and eating had become prominent public preoccupations . Evidence of this dramatic cultural revaluation abounds. In bookstores, for example, cookery and all things related to it are often among the larger displays. There are specialty stores selling all manner of cookware, tableware and other paraphernalia associated with food, eating and drinking. Perhaps most telling is the extension of the phenomenon of mass media celebrity to include culinary personalities . Scholars, too, have jumped on the commodification bandwagon. Now degrees in gastronomy seem set to emulate the MBA phenomenon of the 1980s and food has become a respectable subject for investigation with philosophers, sociologists, historians, cultural theorists, ecologists and many others all having a go at it. However, surprisingly, the question seems to have held little fascination for most historians . For the best part of two centuries they have managed to write their accounts of colonization and nationhood with only scant reference to how the settlers and their descendants fed themselves.

#85 Wright brothers (懷特兄弟) #060085 原文
中文翻譯

奧維爾與威爾伯·萊特是住在俄亥俄州代頓市的兄弟。兩人從1890年代開始製造
腳踏車，以每輛18美元（相當於今日的475美元）販售他們的「萊特特製款」，經營著一家成功的小型生意。
這段打造輕巧堅固機械的經驗，在兩兄弟的興趣轉向飛行之後的
數年間，將被證明是極為寶貴的。

在萊特兄弟開始將好奇心投向天際之際，美國其他人也正在研發飛行器。塞繆爾·蘭利於
1896年駕駛了一架無人駕駛的蒸汽動力飛行器。奧克塔夫·沙努特等人在那個年代末期也在芝加哥附近駕駛滑翔機。然而，
直到萊特兄弟開始著手研究這個問題，「飛行難題」才終於
得以解決。

從1899年開始，兄弟倆設計並建造了一系列滑翔機，以驗證他們對於
飛行機器的各種想法。他們建造了一座風洞，使他們得以在無需建造實體模型的情況下測試設計方案。他們甚至為飛行器自行打造了汽油動力引擎。

英文原文

Orville and Wilbur Wright were brothers living in Dayton, Ohio. The two had started making bicycles during the 1890s and had a successful small business selling their Wright Specials for $18 each ($475 in today’s green). This experience with building light, strong machines would prove valuable in the coming years after the brothers’ interest turned to flight . Others in the United States were also developing aircraft at the time the Wright brothers started turning their curiosity skyward. Samuel Langley had flown an unmanned steam-powered aircraft in 1896. Octave Chanute and others were flying gliders near Chicago late in the decade as well. But it wasn’t until the Wright brothers started working on the matter that the "flying problem" would finally be solved. Beginning in 1899, the brothers designed and built a series of gliders to test their various ideas on a flying machine . They constructed a wind tunnel that allowed them to test designs without having to build a full-size model. They even built their own gasoline-powered motor for their aircraft.

#86 Compulsory voting (強制投票) #060086 原文
中文翻譯

強制投票常被提倡為解決投票率下降問題的方案。但除了提升選舉參與率之外，強制投票對個人和國家還有哪些影響？ Shane Singh 深入探討強迫公民投票在社會、經濟與政治層面所帶來的後果。

近來，有關強制投票的討論相當熱烈。尤其在英國，隨著選民投票率持續下滑，許多評論者與政治人物開始倡議強制選舉參與。支持強制投票者往往援引社會各階層全面參與的重要性。 他們主張，民主國家的公民本就被強制履行許多涉及公共利益的義務，包括擔任陪審員及讓子女接受教育，而全面參與對整個國家有益。反對 強制投票者則常從民主理論的角度主張，投票權隱含著不投票的權利。 他們認為，這種棄權的權利比高投票率可能帶來的任何社會利益都更為重要。 事實上，強制投票的反對者往往認為，若那些本不願投票的人不被推促參與公共事務，對國家或許反而更有益處。

無論上述哪一方的論點更具說服力，強制投票在世界各地均已普遍實施。數個歐洲民主國家規定公民必須投票，澳大利亞及大多數拉丁美洲國家亦然。透過評估這些國家的成果，便 能夠對強制投票的運作機制與實際效果加以評估。

英文原文

Compulsory voting is often suggested as a solution to the problem of declining turnout . But how are individuals and countries affected by compulsory voting beyond boosting electoral participation? Shane Singh investigates the social, economic, and political consequences of compelling citizens to vote. There has been a lot of discussion about compulsory voting these days. In the United Kingdom, in particular, as voter turnout rates have declined, many commentators and politicians have begun advocating for mandatory electoral participation. Those in favor of compulsory voting often adduce the importance of participation among all segments of society . Citizens of democracies are forced to do many things in the interest of the public good, they maintain, including serving on juries and educating their children, and full participation serves the country as whole. Those opposed to compulsory voting often argue that, from a democratic theory perspective, the right to vote implicitly includes a right not to vote . Such a right of abstention, they argue, is more important than any societal good that might accompany high turnout. In fact, opponents of compulsory voting often contend that the country may be better off if those who are disinclined to vote are not pushed to participate in public affairs. Regardless of whether one of these sets of arguments is more persuasive than the other, compulsory voting is commonly used around the world. Several European democracies mandate voting, as do Australia and most of the countries in Latin America. By evaluating results from these countries, it is possible to assess the mechanics and effects of compulsory voting .

3educating their children, and full participation serves the country as whole. #87 Social network (社交網絡) #060087 原文
中文翻譯

十年前，Barsky 與 Purdon（2006）發現，透過社交媒體擴展溝通的社群網路日益普及，相關成本也進一步降低。然而，圖書館主管們並未察覺，這樣的現象如何能成為圖書館與資訊服務的一部分。他們認為，使用者應自行沉浸於社交媒體，而圖書館則繼續扮演其傳統角色（De Rosa et al., 2007）。

Charnigo 與 Barnett-Ellis（2007）的情況亦是如此，他們對 126 位學術圖書館員進行調查，結論顯示，54% 的受訪館員認為 Facebook 並無學術用途。

這些館員持此看法的理由，在於他們認為社交媒體是學生彼此互動的空間。

因此，圖書館員的介入並不受歡迎，因為這可能被視為侵犯個人空間。然而，時間證明，隨著社交媒體技術日益普及，使用者與館員培養出數位素養，圖書館眼見周遭社交媒體的爆炸式成長，也被迫重新審視自身立場。Taylor & Francis（2014）在一項涵蓋 497 位國際圖書館員的調查中，發現超過 70% 的館員如今認為，社交媒體的使用至關重要。

儘管這股浪潮始於公共圖書館（Mon, 2015），時至今日，各類型圖書館若非已在社交媒體上建立存在感，便是正認真考慮加入。因此，圖書館運用社交媒體已成為主流。

英文原文

Ten years ago, Barsky and Purdon (2006) discovered that social networks that are expanding communication through social media are becoming popular and the costs involved are getting further reduced . Yet, library executives did not see how such a phenomenon could become a part of library and information services . They felt that the users should be left to their social media while the library carried on with its traditional roles (De Rosa et al·, 2007). This was also the case when Charnigo and Barnett-Ellis (2007) conducted a survey of 126 academic librarians and concluded that 54% of the librarians surveyed did not believe that there was an academic purpose for Facebook. The rationale behind these librarians’ belief was that social media was a space where students interact with each other . Hence, the librarian was not welcome as their coming in might be viewed as an invasion of space. But time has proved that as the technology of social media became more popular , users and librarians acquired digital literacy, and libraries, seeing an explosion of social media around it, were forced to reconsider their stance. In a survey involving 497 international librarians, Taylor & Francis (2014) discovered that over 70% of librarians now feel that the use of social media is important . Though the wave began with public libraries (Mon, 2015), today, libraries of every type either have a social media presence or they are seriously considering it. Hence, the use of social media by libraries has become mainstream .

紅字句（原文）

#88 Parents’ birth order (家長出生順序) #060088 原文
中文翻譯

家長自身的出生順序，可能在他們養育的家庭中造成問題——當新家庭的互動模式複製了他們自己成長的原生家庭時，這一點尤為明顯。

Agati 列舉了常見的例子，例如身為長子女的家長與長子女孩子之間爆發「激烈衝突」。「兩人都習慣要說最後一句話，雙方都非得佔理不可。但家長必須扮演成年人的角色，從這場爭執中退一步，」他如此建議。

當排行最小的孩子成為家長時，Agati 提醒，由於他們「可能從來沒有被寄予很高的期望，因此他們也可能看不見自己孩子的能力」。但他也指出，由於排行最小的孩子往往較為善於社交，「排行最小的家長能夠幫助他們的長子女——後者在社交場合可能比較吃力。這些家長可以幫助他們的老大放鬆，不要對自己那麼嚴苛。」

媽媽 Susan Ritz 說，她自己的出生順序似乎並未影響她的教養方式，直到她的三個孩子中最小的 Julie 出生後才有所不同。Julie 比 Ritz 的大兒子 Joshua 小九歲，這個年齡差距與 Susan 和她自己的哥哥之間的差距如出一轍。「我會看到 Joshua 對 Julie 做出我哥哥當年對我做的事，」她這樣描述年長許多的兄姐對弟妹的嘲弄與捉弄。「我不得不努力克制自己，不要總是站在 Julie 那一邊。」

正如 Lori Silverstone 所指出的，無論你自己排行幾，偏見都可能浮現出來。「我自己是排行中間的孩子，我可能對我較大的女兒更嚴格——因為我記得我姐姐打過我，」她如此描述自己對女兒們爭吵時的反應。

英文原文

Parents' own born order can become an issue when dynamics in the family they are raising replicate the family in which they were raised . Agati notes common examples, such as a firstborn parent getting into "raging battles" with a firstborn child . "Both are used to getting the last word. Each has to be right. But the parent has to be the grown up and step out of that battle," he advises. When youngest children become parents, Agati cautions that because they "may not have had high expectations placed on them, they in turn may not see their kids for their abilities" . But he also notes that since youngest children tend to be more social, "youngest parents can be helpful to their firstborn, who may have a harder time with social situations. These parents can help their eldest kids loosen up and not be so hard on themselves. Mom Susan Ritz says her own birth order didn't seem to affect her parenting until the youngest of her three children, Julie, was born. Julie was nine years younger than Ritz's oldest, Joshua, mirroring the age difference between Susan and her own older brother. "I would see Joshua do to Julie what my brother did to me," she says of the taunting and teasing by a much older sibling." I had to try not to always take Julie's side." Biases can surface no matter what your own birth position was , as Lori Silverstone points out. "As a middle myself, I can be harder on my older daughter, I recall my older sister hitting me," she says of her reactions to her daughters' tussles.

#89 Online safety (網上安全) #060089 原文
中文翻譯

當提姆·柏納斯-李發明全球資訊網時，他大概沒有預料到兒童最終會成為其主要使用者之一。大多數兒童平均從三歲開始使用網路——
而近期研究顯示，兒童現在花在網路上玩耍和社交的時間，已經超過觀看電視節目的時間。
鑑於這種習慣上的改變，近期一份上議院報告將網路安全與網路行為列為重要議題，並不令人意外。該報告指出，對兒童而言，學習在網路主導的世界中生存，應與讀寫能力同等重要。
上議院通訊委員會也警告，兒童不應在缺乏「對數位世界全面理解」的情況下離開學校。委員會並建議政府考慮實施新的法律要求，以及企業必須遵守的行為準則，以協助將網路提升至「對兒童友善的標準」。
當然，試圖彌補這種缺乏兒童為中心設計的問題並非易事，而是需要眾多領域的合作與善意。這將需要納入科技、教育、法律與政策專家的意見。同時，讓兒童與年輕人也參與其中，也會是一個好主意。

英文原文

When Tim Berners-Lee invented the world wide web, he surely didn’t anticipate that children would end up becoming some of its main users. Most start using the internet at the average age of three – and as recent research shows, children now spend more time playing and socializing online than watching television programs . Given this change in habits, it is not surprising that a recent House of Lords report has raised online safety and behavior as an important issue . The report said that for children, learning to survive in a world dominated by the internet should be as important as reading and writing. The House of Lords Communications Committee also warned that children should not be leaving school without "a well-rounded understanding of the digital world" . It also suggested that the government should think about implementing new legal requirements and a code of conduct companies would have to adhere to , which would help to bring the internet up to "child- friendly standards". Of course, trying to rectify this lack of child-centered design is not an easy task, but one that requires the cooperation and goodwill of many sectors . It will need to involve consultation with technology, education, legal and policy experts. And it would also be a good idea to make children and young people part of the process.

#90 Nap (小憩) #060090 原文
中文翻譯

午間小憩能救你一命嗎？如果以希臘男性的經驗作為參考，答案或許是肯定的。

在昨日發表的一項研究中，哈佛公共衛生學院與雅典的研究人員
指出，習慣每天午睡30分鐘的希臘人，在六年內死於心臟病的機率，比從不午睡的人低37%。科學家追蹤了逾23,000名成年人，
發現午睡的益處在職場男性身上最為顯著。
研究人員早已注意到，地中海地區的成年人死於心臟病的比率低於美國人及北歐人。富含橄欖油及其他有益心臟健康食物的飲食，被認為是部分原因，但科學家對午睡所可能發揮的作用同樣深感興趣。
該研究得出結論：午睡比飲食或體能活動更能降低心臟病發作及其他致命心臟疾病的發生率。
未參與此研究的專家表示，有充分的生化學理由支持午睡有助於預防心臟病。他們指出，本質上，無論何時入睡，睡眠就像一個閥門，能釋放日常生活中的壓力。

英文原文

Could midday nap save your life? If the experience of Greek men is any guide, the answer just may be yes. In a study released yesterday, researchers at the Harvard School of Public Health and in Athens reported that Greeks who took regular 30-minute napping were 37% less likely to die of heart disease over a six-year period than those who never napped . The scientists tracked more than 23,000 adults, finding that the benefits of napping were most pronounced for working men . Researchers have long recognized that Mediterranean adults die of heart disease at a rate lower than Americans and Northern Europeans. Diets rich in olive oil and other heart-healthy foods have received some of the credit, but scientists have been intrigued by the potential role of napping. The study concluded that napping was more likely than diet or physical activity to lower the incidence of heart attacks and other life-ending heart ailments . Specialists not involved with the study said there are sound biochemical reasons to believe that a nap may help protect against heart disease. Essentially, they said, sleep at any time of day acts like a value to release the stress of everyday life .

#91 Brand loyalty (品牌忠誠度) #060091 原文
中文翻譯

當消費者重複購買你的品牌，而非在各品牌之間隨意更換，品牌忠誠度便由此形成。學界普遍認為，開發新客戶的成本遠高於維繫現有客戶的成本，因此品牌忠誠度對於實現高利潤至關重要。對於慈善機構而言，將提升品牌忠誠度列為行銷目標至關重要。若能說服現有捐款人為該機構設立自動扣款，其現金流將大幅改善。

提升或重塑品牌形象

雖然部分品牌歷久彌新（Marmite 已有逾百年歷史），但其他品牌因消費者口味與生活方式的改變而逐漸失去吸引力。此時，企業必須更新品牌形象，使產品持續貼近目標市場的需求，並須訂立明確的目標。例如：我們希望塑造哪些品牌特質？我們希望品牌代表什麼？

重新定位

當企業旨在改變品牌形象，使品牌吸引全新的目標市場時，重新定位便應運而生。McVitie's 在 Hobnobs 餅乾品牌推出十二年後，決定對其進行重新定位。Hobnobs 原本定位為面向中年消費者、樸實且較為健康的餅乾。市場調查為 McVitie's 指引了新的方向：更年輕、更偏向男性，且風格更為活潑。於是，品牌推出了全新包裝，並搭配更加鮮明亮眼的廣告宣傳活動一併上市。2013 年，Hobnobs 的銷售額達 3,600 萬英鎊，較前一年成長 9%。

英文原文

Brand loyalty exists when consumers repeat-purchase your brand rather than swapping and switching between brands. It is widely agreed that it is far more expensive to have to find a new customer than to keep existing ones happy, so brand loyalty is crucial for achieving high-profit margins . For charities, it is important to set a marketing objective of improving brand loyalty. If existing donors can be persuaded to set up a direct debit to the charity, its cash flow will improve significantly. To enhance, or reposition a brand's image Although some brands stay fresh for generations (Marmite is over 100 years old) others become jaded due to changes in consumer tastes and lifestyles. At this point, the firms need to refresh the brand image to keep the products relevant to the target market. A clear objective must be set . For instance: what brand attributes do we want to create? What do we want the brand to stand for? Repositioning This occurs when a firm aims to change a brand's image, so that the brand appeals to a new target market . Twelve years into its life cycle, McVitie’s decided to reposition its Hobnobs biscuit brand. Hobnobs had been positioned as a homely, quite healthy biscuit for middle-aged consumers. Research pointed McVitie’s in a new direction: younger, more male, and less dull. So new packaging was designed and then launched in conjunction with a new, brighter advertising campaign. In 2013 Hobnobs sales were worth 36 million pounds, 9 percent up on the previous year.

#92 Books and television (書本與電視) #060092 原文
中文翻譯

要理解電視主導的觀念新聞市場，與印刷術主導的世界中所形成的市場為何如此不同，其最根本的原因在於：必須區分電視觀眾所體驗的生動性，與讀者所體驗的「生動性」之間的本質差異。我認為，閱讀文字時所體驗到的生動性，會自動受到大腦推理中樞持續激活的調節——這些中樞在重現作者意圖描繪的現實圖像的過程中始終運作。相比之下，電視所呈現的那種發自肺腑的生動性，具有觸發本能反應的能力，足以媲美現實本身所引發的反應——且不受邏輯、理性與反思思考的調節。

電視媒體所達成的現實模擬，其令人驚嘆的生動程度與說服力，遠超過印刷文字所傳達的現實再現，這已遠不止是人們獲取資訊方式上的漸進式改變。當然，書籍同樣能傳達引人入勝、栩栩如生的現實再現。然而，讀者在閱讀時會主動參與其中，共同召喚出書籍作者試圖描繪的現實。此外，人類大腦中主導推理過程的區域，會在閱讀印刷文字的過程中持續被激活：文字由抽象符號——即字母——所組成，這些字母本身並無固有意義，直到它們串聯成可辨識的序列為止。

相比之下，電視則向觀眾呈現一個更為完整成形的現實再現——無需文字向來所要求的那種創意性協作。

英文原文

To understand the final reason why the news marketplace of ideas dominated by television is so different from the one that emerged in the world dominated by the printing press, it is important to distinguish the quality of vividness experienced by television viewers from the "vividness" experienced by readers. I believe that the vividness experienced in the reading of words is automatically modulated by the constant activation of the reasoning centers of the brain that are used in the process of concreating the representation of reality the author has intended. By contrast, the visceral vividness portrayed on television has the capacity to trigger instinctual responses similar to those triggered by reality itself—and without being modulated by logic, reason, and reflective thought. The simulation of reality accomplished in the television medium is so astonishingly vivid and compelling compared with the representations of reality conveyed by printed words that it signifies much more than an incremental change in the way people consume information. Books also convey compelling and vivid representations of reality, of course. But the reader actively participates in the conjuring of the reality the book’s author Is attempting to depict. Moreover, the parts of the human brain that are central to the reasoning process are continually activated by the very act of reading printed words : Words are composed of abstract symbols—letters— that have no intrinsic meaning themselves until they are strung together into recognizable sequences. Television, by contrast, presents to its viewers a much more fully formed representation of reality—without requiring the creative collaboration that words have always demanded.

#93 Phoenician (腓尼基語) #060093 原文
中文翻譯

他們的貿易網絡使腓尼基人致富，同時也以前所未有的方式促進了東西方之間的文化交流與傳播：其中最重要的，是字母文字的擴散——這套文字系統被整個地中海地區所採用。

腓尼基字母是一套由22個符號組成的書寫系統，每個符號恰好對應一個發音（音素）。「alphabet」（字母）一詞源自序列中前兩個符號的名稱，aleph（「牛」）與 beit（「房屋」）：這些名稱同時也反映了字母的形狀，每個字母均源自某件物品的圖像，而該物品的名稱正以對應的音開頭。

字母文字簡單易學，無需像掌握楔形文字或埃及象形文字那樣耗費數年的專項訓練。專業教育因此變得不再必要，識字能力也從宮殿和神廟的制度性框架中解放出來——在那些場所，傳統文字依然持續使用。字母文字非常契合長途商人的需求：他們需要隨時記錄商務往來，且出於保密與節省開支的考量，往往寧願親自書寫，而非雇用專業抄寫員。由於這套文字能夠輕易用來記錄任何語言，在西元前第一千年間，它先後被改造用於書寫阿拉姆語、希伯來語、希臘語、弗里吉亞語、呂底亞語、伊特魯里亞語和拉丁語，僅舉其中數例而已。

英文原文

Their trade networks made the Phoenicians rich but also enabled cultural exchange and transfer between East and West in an unprecedented way : the most significant was the spread of the alphabetic script which was adopted all over the Mediterranean. The Phoenician alphabet is a writing system consisting of only 22 signs representing exactly one sound (phoneme) each . The term "alphabet" derives from the names of the first two signs in the sequence, aleph ("cattle") and beit("house"): these names also reflect the letters' shapes, each derived from the picture of an object whose name starts with the relevant sound. The alphabetic script is simple enough to learn quickly, without the years of dedicated training required to master writing systems such as cuneiform or Egyptian hieroglyphs. Specialized schooling was unnecessary , and literacy was therefore disengaged from the institutional context of palaces and temples where the traditional scripts continued to be used. The alphabet suited the needs of long- distance merchants who needed to be able to record their business affairs on the go and who, for reasons of confidentiality and money, often preferred to write themselves rather than employ a specialist scribe. As the script could easily be used to record any language, it was , in the course of the first millennium BC, adapted for Aramaic, Hebrew, Greek, Phrygian, Lydian, Etruscan and Latin, to name but a few .

紅字句（原文）
#原文
1Their trade networks made the Phoenicians rich but also enabled cultural exchange and transfer between East and West in an unprecedented way : the most significant was the spread of the
2The Phoenician alphabet is a writing system consisting of only 22 signs representing exactly one sound (phoneme) each . The term "alphabet" derives from the names of the first two signs in the sequence,
3The alphabetic script is simple enough to learn quickly, without the years of dedicated training required to master writing systems such as cuneiform or Egyptian hieroglyphs. Specialized schooling was unnecessary , and literacy was therefore disengaged from the institutional context of palaces and
4specialist scribe. As the script could easily be used to record any language, it was , in the course of the first millennium BC, adapted for Aramaic, Hebrew, Greek, Phrygian, Lydian, Etruscan and Latin, to name but a few .
#94 Legumes (豆科植物) #060094 原文
中文翻譯

園丁可以透過種植豆科植物來養活家人並改善土壤，例如四季豆、大豆、扁豆和豌豆。豆科植物的根部能自行產生氮素，氮素是所有植物生長所需的主要肥料養分。氮素在豆科植物根部形成的根瘤中產生，根瘤內含有根瘤菌。這些細菌從空氣中吸取氮氣，並將其轉化為植物可吸收利用的形式。

當豆科植物在秋季被拔起時，根瘤中多餘的氮素便留存於土壤中。這些多餘的有機氮可供其他植物在下一個生長季節使用。之所以稱為有機氮，是因為它是自然產生的，這使得四季豆或豌豆成為有機作物生產體系中極佳的輪作作物。

有機農夫偏好有機氮，原因在於其天然來源，以及它在土壤中分解緩慢的特性，從而在整個生長季節中持續緩慢地為植物提供養分。合成氮肥往往釋放氮素較快，對環境的衝擊也較大。合成氮肥通常在生長季節中分次施用，以模擬有機氮源緩慢釋放的效果。

每種豆科植物通常需要特定類型的根瘤菌，才能在其根部形成根瘤。從未種過四季豆的園丁可以從大多數知名蔬菜種子目錄購買小袋裝的接種劑或細菌。播種前，打開包裝，將粉塵狀的細菌倒入種子中，搖晃包裝後再進行播種。根瘤會隨著根部的發育而形成。這些細菌將留存於土壤中，因此明年無需再次為種子接種。

切勿對豆類作物額外施用氮肥。這樣做會使根瘤中的細菌變得懶惰，促使它們停止自行產生氮素。在家庭蔬菜園中特別受歡迎的豆科植物包括利馬豆、豌豆、食用大豆、扁豆和蠶豆。在最近一項調查中，透過新墨西哥州立大學「園藝師培訓計畫」受訓的園丁中，有44%表示他們在自家菜園中種植了四季豆及其他豆科植物。種植時，請務必為每種豆科植物購買適合的根瘤菌菌株。

英文原文

Gardeners can feed their families and enrich the soil by growing legumes , such as green beans, soybeans, lentils and peas. Legume roots produce their own nitrogen, which is a major fertilizer nutrient needed by all plants for growth. Nitrogen is produced in nodules that form on the roots of legumes, which contain Rhizobium bacteria . The bacteria take nitrogen from the air and convert it into a form the plants can use. When legumes are pulled up in the fall, excess nitrogen from the nodules is left in the soil . The excess organic nitrogen can be used by other plants the following growing season . It's considered organic nitrogen because it was produced naturally, making green beans or peas great rotational crops in an organic crop production system. Organic growers prefer organic nitrogen because of its natural origins and because it breaks down slowly in the soil , thus slowly feeding plants throughout the growing season. Synthetic nitrogen fertilizers tend to release nitrogen quickly and are harsher on the environment. Synthetic nitrogen fertilizers are generally applied in split applications during the season to mimic the slow release of organic nitrogen sources. Each specific legume generally requires a specific type of Rhizobium bacteria to produce nodules on their roots. Gardeners who have never grown green beans before can purchase small bags of inoculum or bacteria from most popular vegetable seed catalogs. Before planting beans, open the package and pour in the dust-like bacteria among the seed. Shake the package and then plant. Nodules will form on the roots as they develop. The bacteria will remain in the soil, making it unnecessary to inoculate the seed next year. Do not apply extra nitrogen fertilizer to bean crops . Doing so makes bacteria in the nodules lazy, encouraging them to stop producing their own nitrogen. Legumes that are particularly popular in the home vegetable garden include lima beans, peas, edible soybeans, lentils and fava beans. In a recent survey, 44 percent of gardeners trained through New Mexico State University's Master Gardener Program said they grew green beans and other legumes in their home gardens. When planting, be sure to purchase appropriate strains of Rhizobium bacteria for each type of legume.

#95 House mice (家鼠) #060095 原文
中文翻譯

根據最新研究，家鼠（Mus musculus）是人類定居的理想生物標記，因為牠們往往會偷偷藏匿在板條箱或船隻中，最終跟著人類的足跡抵達各地。Searle 表示，以老鼠作為人類遷徙的替代指標，能夠補充現有考古資料所揭示的資訊，並回答那些文物稀缺地區的重要問題。

人類走到哪裡，老鼠就跟到哪裡，牠們常常藏身於乾草車或船隻之中。儘管家鼠的自然活動範圍僅有100公尺（109碼），且演化起源地靠近巴基斯坦，卻已成功遍布各大洲，這使牠成為 Searle 等研究人員的有力研究工具。Searle 早先在約克大學進行的研究支持了一項理論，認為澳洲的老鼠起源於不列顛群島，可能是在18世紀末至19世紀初，隨著被遣送至澳洲開拓殖民地的囚犯一同漂洋過海而來。

在這項維京人研究中，他與來自冰島、丹麥和瑞典的研究夥伴更進一步，利用從10至12世紀考古遺址採集的古代老鼠 DNA，並結合現代老鼠的樣本進行分析。

他希望在下一個研究計畫中實現這一目標——該計畫涉及追蹤老鼠及其他物種（包括植物）的遷徙路徑，橫跨印度洋，從南亞延伸至東非。

英文原文

According to new research, house mice (Mus musculus) are ideal biomarkers of human settlement as they tend to stow away in crates or on ships that end up going where people go. Using mice as a proxy for human movement can add to what is already known through archaeological data and answer important questions in areas where there is a lack of artifacts , Searle said. Where people go, so do mice, often stowing away in carts of hay or on ships. Despite a natural range of just 100 meters (109 yards) and an evolutionary base near Pakistan, the house mouse has managed to colonize every continent , which makes it a useful tool for researchers like Searle. Previous research conducted by Searle at the University of York supported the theory that Australian mice originated in the British Isles and probably came over with convicts shipped there to colonize the continent in the late 18th and 19th centuries. In the Viking study, he and his fellow researchers in Iceland, Denmark and Sweden took it a step further , using ancient mouse DNA collected from archaeological sites dating from the 10th to 12th centuries, as well as modern mice. He is hoping to do just that in his next project, which involves tracking the migration of mice and other species , including plants, across the Indian Ocean, from South Asia to East Africa.

#96 Shifting birds (候鳥遷徙) #060096 原文
中文翻譯

隨著較暖的冬季氣溫越來越普遍，部分動物的調適方式之一是將其分布範圍向北遷移。但一項針對59種北美鳥類的新研究指出，這樣做並非輕而易舉——許多鳥類花了約35年才遷移到足夠北方、使冬季氣溫與其歷史棲息地相近的地區。

研究人員利用北美聖誕節鳥類調查35年的數據，將冬季氣溫與鳥類的目擊地點進行比對。他們對59種鳥類逐一進行測試，發現各物種對氣候變化的反應不盡相同。綜合所有鳥類物種的數據後，有明確證據顯示存在約35年的強烈滯後現象。

舉例而言，黑美洲鷲在過去35年間已向北擴張，如今的冬季棲息地北至麻薩諸塞州，當地的最低冬季氣溫與1975年馬里蘭州的氣溫相近。另一方面，瀕危的紅頭啄木鳥儘管面臨暖化趨勢，其分布範圍卻毫無改變，可能是因為其極為特殊的棲息地需求阻礙了範圍遷移。

La Sorte表示，這兩種情況對鳥類而言都可能造成問題。無法跟上氣候變化的物種可能會逼近其生理耐受極限，或者隨著其他物種超越它們，可能失去重要的棲息地條件，例如偏好的食物來源。但若牠們所依賴的棲息地條件同樣傾向於落後於氣候變化，牠們也無法過快地遷移分布範圍。

若暖化趨勢減緩，如過去幾年所見，鳥類或許能夠迎頭趕上。然而，隨著全球碳排放持續增加，加速暖化的可能性極高，這可能對鳥類造成額外壓力。該研究凸顯了這些挑戰，以及氣候變化對自然系統造成破壞的巨大潛力。它也強調了生態學家在同時預測氣候變化對眾多物種長期影響時所面臨的重重挑戰。

英文原文

As warmer winter temperatures become more common, one way for some animals to adjust is to shift their ranges northward . But a new study of 59 North American bird species indicates that doing so is not easy or quick -- it took about 35 years for many birds to move far enough north for winter temperatures to match where they historically lived. The researchers used 35 years of data from the North American Christmas Bird Count to match winter temperatures to where birds were seen. They tested 59 bird species individually and found that they responded differently to climate change . When summarized across bird species, there was evidence for a strong delay lasting about 35 years. For example, black vultures have spread northward in the last 35 years and now winter as far north as Massachusetts, where the minimum winter temperature is similar to what it was in Maryland in 1975. On the other hand, the endangered red-cockaded woodpecker did not alter its range at all despite the warming trend, possibly because its very specific habitat requirements precluded a range shift. Both of these scenarios could represent problems for birds, La Sorte said. Species that do not track changes in climate may wind up at the limits of their physiological tolerance , or they may lose important habitat qualities, such as favored food types, as those species pass them by. But they also can't move their ranges too fast if the habitat conditions they depend on also tend to lag behind climate. If warming trends weaken, as they did over the past few years, birds may be able to catch up. But accelerated warming , which is likely as global carbon emissions continue to increase, may put additional strain on birds . The study highlights these challenges and the high potential climate change has for disrupting natural systems . It also underscores the challenges ecologists face ipredicting the long-term consequences of climate change for many species simultaneously .

#97 ethics (倫理學) #060097 原文
中文翻譯

倫理學是一套道德規範，用以界定我們在實踐與決策中的是非對錯。許多
專業領域都建立了一套正式的倫理規範體系，以引導從業人員的職業行為。例如，
醫生通常會宣誓希波克拉底誓言，其中明確規定醫生不得對患者「造成傷害」。工程師則遵循一套倫理準則，要求他們「將公眾的安全、健康與福祉置於首位」。在這些專業領域以及科學界，這些原則已深入人心，從業者幾乎不需要刻意思考如何遵守倫理——它已成為他們執業方式的一部分。

違反倫理被視為極其嚴重的行為，至少會受到業內處罰（例如吊銷執照），
有時甚至會受到法律制裁）。科學倫理要求在科學實踐的各個階段都保持誠實與正直，從如實呈報研究結果，到正確標註合作者貢獻。
這套倫理體系貫穿科學實踐的全程，從數據收集到
發表乃至後續各環節。與其他專業領域一樣，科學倫理已深刻融入
科學家的工作方式之中，他們深知自身研究成果的可信度以及整體科學知識的可靠性，都有賴於對這套倫理的堅守。
科學中的許多倫理原則都與生產無偏見的科學知識有關，這對於其他人嘗試在研究成果的基礎上加以延伸或拓展至關重要。科學倫理所要求的數據公開發表、同儕審查、重複驗證與協作合作，都有助於驗證研究成果、確認結果或提出質疑，從而推動科學不斷向前發展。

英文原文

Ethics is a set of moral obligations that define right and wrong in our practices and decisions . Many professions have a formalized system of ethical practices that help guide professionals in the field . For example, doctors commonly take the Hippocratic Oath, which, among other things, states that doctors do no harm "to their patients. Engineers follow an ethical guide that states that they "hold paramount the safety, health, and welfare of the public." Within these professions as well as within science, the principles become so ingrained that practitioners rarely have to think about adhering to the ethic - it's part of the way they practice. And a breach of ethics is considered very serious, punishable at least within the profession (by revocation of a license, for example, and sometimes by the law as well). Scientific ethics calls for honesty and integrity in all stages of scientific practice , from reporting results regardless to properly attributing collaborators. This system of ethics guides the practice of science, from data collection to publication and beyond. As in other professions, the scientific ethic is deeply integrated into the way scientists work , and they are aware that the reliability of their work and scientific knowledge in general depends upon adhering to that ethic. Many of the ethical principles in science relate to the production of unbiased scientific knowledge which is critical when others try to build upon or extend research findings. The open publication of data, peer review, replication, and collaboration required by the scientific ethic all help to keep science moving forward by validating research findings and confirming or raising questions about results.

#98 Soil (土壤的重要性) #060098 原文
中文翻譯

我們很容易忘記腳下土地裡藏著什麼，以及為什麼保護它如此重要。一湯匙的土壤中所含的生物數量，超過了地球上的人口總數；數十億個細菌、真菌和其他微生物，與礦物質、水、空氣和有機物質結合，形成一個支撐植物生長、進而維繫所有生命的活體系統。

健康的土壤每公頃可儲存多達 3,750 噸的水，從而降低洪澇風險；氣候變遷政府間專家小組（IPCC）也指出，若能改善土壤健康狀況，89% 的農業排放量即可獲得緩解。

良好的土壤管理還能提升牲畜的抗病能力，並最終為農民帶來更高的利潤——然而，土壤及其對動物健康的影響，在過去數十年間卻一直是英國農業中最被忽視的一環。

過去 50 年來，農業對化學肥料的依賴日益加深，如今的施用量約為 1950 年代的 10 倍。農民往往認為化學肥料 NPK（氮、磷、鉀）已能提供植物所需的全部養分，但它同時也對土地的長期健康造成損害：研究顯示，世界上許多地區的土壤，剩餘的可耕收穫次數已不足 100 次。

英文原文

It’s very easy to forget about what’s in the ground beneath our feet and why it’s so important to protect it. One tablespoon of soil contains more organisms than there are people on Earth ; billions of bacteria, fungi and other microorganisms combine with minerals, water, air and organic matter to create a living system that supports plants and, in turn, all life. Healthy soil can store as much as 3,750 tons of water per hectare, reducing the risk of flooding , and the International Panel on Climate Change (IPCC) has said that 89% of all agricultural emissions could be mitigated if we improved the health of our soil. Good soil management also increases disease resistance in livestock and ultimately drives profits for farmers – yet soil and its impact on the health of our animals has, over recent decades, been one of the most neglected links in UK agriculture. Over the last 50 years’ agriculture has become increasingly dependent on chemical fertilizers , with applications today around 10 times higher than in the 1950s. Farmers often think the chemical fertilizer NPK (nitrogen, phosphorous and potassium) provides all the nutrition a plant requires , but it also has a detrimental effect on the long-term health of the land: research suggests there are fewer than 100 harvests left in many of the world’s soils .

#99 British Crime (英國犯罪問題) #060099 原文
中文翻譯

英國內政部定期發布的「英國犯罪調查」估計，真實的犯罪水平（無論如何，是那些反映在官方數字中的類型）約為年度統計數字所登錄數量的四倍。
企業，尤其是金融服務業的企業，常常因為害怕損害公眾形象而不舉報針對自身的犯罪行為。現今許多市民並未投保汽車失竊或財產損失險（因為他們負擔不起保費），因此即使成為受害者，也沒有動機向警方報案。

犯罪統計數字的急劇攀升，有時並非源於某類行為的真實增長，而是來自新的執法政策——1980年代曼徹斯特某12個月內，「猥褻舞蹈」的違規案件上升了約300%，但這僅僅是因為熱心盡責的警察局長詹姆斯·安德頓在同性戀夜總會部署了大量警力所致。
有時，一批新罪行的立法，或以新方式觸犯舊有罪行的可能性（例如涉及欺詐與欺騙的電腦犯罪），也會導致犯罪數字驟然上揚。剛公布的數字顯示街頭搶劫案件驚人地躍升，但其中很大一部分似乎屬於非常特定的犯罪類型：竊取如今無處不在的手機。
反之，若飆車兜風及部分傷人案件被排除在年度統計所衡量的類別之外——事實確是如此——則官方數字甚至無法反映向警方舉報的實際犯罪狀況。
內政部匯編犯罪統計數字的方式同樣值得關注。從1998年4月起，警察部隊開始以一種新方式統計犯罪，據政府表示，此方式將提供「更為穩健的統計衡量標準」。
根據新規定，犯罪以每名受害者計一宗的方式登錄。某些犯罪，如傷人案，一向以此方式登錄，因此這項改變的主要影響將體現在財產罪行方面。以店鋪盜竊為例，舊規定以犯罪者計算，現在改為以受害者計算。在設有閘欄的停車場內，多輛汽車遭竊的案件以往計為一宗罪行，現在則計算為獨立的個別罪行。

英文原文

The Home Office’ s periodic British Crime Survey estimates that the true level of crime (the sorts, anyway, which inform the official figures) is about four times that which is registered in the annual statistics. Quite often, especially in the financial services sector, businesses do not report crimes against themselves for fear of lowering their public image. Many citizens today are not insured against car theft or property loss (because they cannot afford the premiums) so they have no incentive to tell the police if they become victims. A steep statistical rise in crime can sometimes arise not from a real growth in a particular type of conduct but from a new policing policy - offences of "lewd dancing" rose by about 300 per cent during 12 months in the 1980s in Manchester, but only because the zealous Chief Constable James Anderton had deployed a great many officers in gay night clubs. Sometimes the enactment of a new range of offences or the possibility of committing old offences in a new way (like computer offences involving fraud and deception) can cause an upward jolt in crime levels. The figures just released show a startling jump in street robbery but much of this seems to be a very particular crime: the theft of the now ubiquitous mobile phones. Conversely, if crimes like joyriding and some assaults are kept out of the categories measured in the annual statistics, as is the case, the official figures do not reflect even what is reported to the police as criminal. The way that criminal statistics are compiled by the Home Office is also relevant. From April 1998, police forces started to count crime in a way which, according to the government, will give "a more robust statistical measure" . Under the new rules, crime is recorded as one crime per victim . Some crimes, like assaults, have always been recorded in this way, so the main impact of the change will be in the area of property offences. Shop thefts, for example, were the old rules counted offenders, will now count victims. Multiple thefts from cars in a car park with a barrier were previously counted as one offence but are now counted as separate offences.

#100 Take-all disease (通吃的疾病) #060100 原文
中文翻譯

土壤真菌「通吃病」對全球穀物作物的根部造成毀滅性的危害
是英國小麥作物面臨的重大病害問題。
然而，英國生物技術與生命科學研究委員會（BBSRC）旗下的洛桑研究所近期田間試驗數據顯示，
農民可透過選擇特定小麥品種來控制這種毀滅性病害——這些品種在第一期種植時能減少通吃病菌在土壤中的累積。
小麥是重要的主食作物，光對英國經濟的貢獻每年便高達16億英鎊。這項由生物技術與生命科學研究委員會（BBSRC）、環境食品與農村事務部（Defra）及HGCA共同資助的研究，
將協助農民提升產量、應對全球糧食安全挑戰，並促進英國經濟成長。

通吃病由真菌 Gaeumannomyces graminis var. tritici 引起，會降低穀物產量與品質，並導致收成後土壤中殘留更多施用的氮肥。

儘管已採用化學、生物及農藝等防治方法，通吃病菌仍是最難防治的小麥病原體之一。第二期與第三期小麥受通吃病感染的風險，與第一期小麥收割後土壤中殘留的病菌量直接相關。

洛桑研究所發表於《植物病理學》期刊的這項研究，已證實不同小麥品種在促進通吃病菌累積方面存在差異。

種植低累積品種（如 Cadenza）作為第一期小麥，可用於調控土壤中通吃病菌的接種量，從而在第二期與第三期小麥中獲得更佳的產量。研究觀察到，第二期小麥每公頃產量最多可提升2噸。

英文原文

The soil dwelling fungus ‘take-all’ inflicts devastating stress to the roots of cereals crops worldwide and is a major disease problem in UK wheat crops . However, recent field trial data from Rothamsted Research, an institute of the BBSRC, has demonstrated that farmers could control this devastating disease by selecting wheat cultivars that reduce take-all build up in the soil when grown as a first wheat. Wheat is an important staple crop worth 1·6 Billion a year to the UK economy alone . This work funded by the Biotechnology and Biological Sciences Research Council (BBSRC), the Department for the Environment, Food and Rural Affairs (Defra) and the HGCA will help farmers to increase yields, combating global food security and contributing to UK economic growth. Take-all disease, caused by the fungus, Gaeumannomyces graminis var· tritici, reduces grain yield and quality and results in an increased amount of residual applied nitrogen fertilizer left in the soil post- harvest . Despite the use of chemical, biological and cultural control methods the take-all fungus is still one of the most difficult pathogens of wheat to control. The risk of take-all infection in second and third wheat crops is directly linked to the amount of fungus remaining in the soil after the first wheat is harvested. The Rothamsted Research study, published in Plant Pathology, has demonstrated that wheat cultivars differ in their ability to build-up the take-all fungus . Growing a low building cultivar, such as Cadenza, as a first wheat crop can be used to manipulate take- all inoculum levels in the soil resulting in better yields from the second and third wheat crops. Yield increases of up to 2 tons per hectare in 2nd wheats have been observed.

#101 Dendrochronology (年輪學) #060101 原文
中文翻譯

以下是年輪學的運作原理。如果你在今天砍倒一棵樹，從樹的外側向內數年輪是非常直觀的。因此，樹木橫截面中的年輪序列就像摩斯密碼中的訊息，過去曾用於發送電報；摩斯密碼中的點點劃點劃，對應年輪序列中的寬寬窄寬窄。

年輪專家（稱為樹輪年代學家）的研究方式是：記錄在近期已知年份被砍伐的樹木中，寬窄年輪的排列順序，同時也記錄過去不同時期被砍伐的樹木木梁中的年輪序列。藉由這種方式，樹輪年代學家已建構出年輪記錄，在世界某些地區可追溯數千年之久。年輪學的額外收穫是，每個年輪的寬度與內部結構反映了該年的降雨量以及降雨的季節。因此，年輪研究也讓我們得以重建過去的氣候。

英文原文

Here’s how tree ring dating, known to scientists as dendrochronology, works. If you cut a tree down today, it’s straightforward to count the rings inwards, starting from the tree’s outside. Hence the sequence of the rings in a tree cross-section is like a message in Morse code formerly used for sending telegraph messages; dot-dot-dash-dot-dash in the Morse code, wide-wide- narrow-wide-narrow in the tree ring sequence. Tree ring specialists (known as dendrochronologists) proceed by noting the sequence of wider and narrower rings in a tree cut down in a known recent year , and also noting the sequences in beams from trees cut down at various times in the past. In that way, dendrochronologists have constructed tree ring records extending back for thousands of years in some parts of the world . A bonus of dendrochronology is that the width and substructure of each ring reflect the amount of rain and the season at which the rain fell during that particular year. Thus, tree ring studies also allow one to reconstruct the past climate .

#102 World Wide Web (萬維網) #060102 原文
中文翻譯

他是過去一百年來改變世界最深的人。提姆·伯納斯-李爵士或許是個生活低調、居住在波士頓的溫文儒雅學者，但身為全球資訊網的發明者，他同時也是一位革命者。他是一位科學家，不僅改變了人們的思維方式，也改變了人們的生活方式。

自從全球資訊網二十年前普及全球，我們購物、聆聽音樂與溝通的方式已徹底改變。這對政治、文學、經濟——甚至恐怖主義——都帶來了深遠影響，因為個人現在能夠與菁英階層獲取同等的資訊。社會將永遠不再相同。

這位來自牛津的電腦科學家，在被禁止使用某台大學電腦後，用一個電視螢幕和零件自行組裝了電腦，他既是文化思想的引領者，也是科技領域的先驅。

「我們走到今天這一步真是令人驚嘆，」他說。「但你總是在思考下一個瘋狂的想法是什麼，並努力確保網路仍是一個統一的網路，確保網際網路保持開放。沒有太多時間坐下來回顧與反思。」

他說，他發明全球資訊網，是因為他對無法在同一個地方找到所有想要的資訊感到沮喪。這是一個他親手實現的想像概念。

英文原文

He is the man who has changed the world more than anyone else in the past hundred years. Sir Tim Berners-Lee may be a mild-mannered academic who lives modestly in Boston, but as the inventor of the world wide web he is also a revolutionary . He is a scientist who has altered the way people think as well as the way they live . Since the web went global 20 years ago, the way we shop, listen to music and communicate has been transformed . There are implications for politics, literature, economics — even terrorism — because an individual can now have the same access to information as the elite. Society will never be the same. The computer scientist from Oxford, who built his own computer from a television screen and spare parts after he was banned from one of the university computers, is a cultural guru as much as a technological one. "It is amazing how far we’ve come," he says. "But you’re always wondering what’s the next crazy idea, and working to make sure the web stays one web and that the internet stays open. There isn’t much time to sit back and reflect." He invented the web, he says, because he was frustrated that he couldn’t find all the information he wanted in one place. It was an imaginary concept that he realized .

#103 Hunter-Gatherers (遊牧民族) #060103 原文
中文翻譯

大約在距今2300年前，一群被稱為桑人的遊牧採集者在今日博茨瓦納境內獲得了家畜。他們的人口不斷增長，並遍布南非西半部。他們是南非最早的牧民，自稱科伊科伊人（或科伊人），意思是「人中之人」或「真正的人民」。這個名字是為了彰顯他們對自身歷史與文化的自豪。科伊科伊人為南非以及桑人帶來了全新的生活方式，而桑人是獵採者，而非牧民。這導致了兩個族群之間的誤解，進而引發衝突。

科伊科伊人是17世紀中葉最早與荷蘭定居者接觸的原住民族。隨著荷蘭人佔領土地開闢農場，科伊科伊人遭到驅逐、屠殺或淪為奴隸，人口因此急劇減少。歐洲定居者稱科伊科伊人為「霍屯督人」，因為他們語言的發音與任何歐洲語言都截然不同，歐洲人無法發出其中許多詞語和音節。

英文原文

In around 2300 BP (Before Present), hunter gatherers called the San acquired domestic stock in what is now modern day Botswana . Their population grew, and spread throughout the Western half of South Africa . They were the first pastoralists in southern Africa, and called themselves Khoikhoi (or Khoe), which means 'men of men' or 'the real people'. This name was chosen to show pride in their past and culture. The Khoikhoi brought a new way of life to South Africa and to the San , who were hunter gatherers as opposed to herders. This led to misunderstandings and subsequent conflict between the two groups . The Khoikhoi were the first native people to come into contact with the Dutch settlers in the mid-17th century. As the Dutch took over land for farms, the Khoikhoi were dispossessed, exterminated, or enslaved and therefore their numbers dwindled . The Khoikhoi were called the ‘Hottentots’ by European settlers because the sound of their language was so different from any European language, and they could not pronounce many of the words and sounds.

#104 3D Printing (3D打印) #060104 原文
中文翻譯

Madeline Gannon 是卡內基梅隆大學建築學院的研究員與講師，也是計算設計博士候選人——但這還不是全部。她立志要向世界敞開3D打印無限的設計可能性。

「目前，你必須具備大量技術背景，才能參與為3D打印機創作作品，」Gannon說。「在我們如何建立數位模型這件事上，仍然存在巨大的知識門檻。」

隨著技術的進步，價格已大幅下降，Gannon指出，現在任何人都可以花幾百美元購買一台3D打印機。然而，並非任何人都能為3D打印成品創作出原創設計。

為了將真正的創作力交到普通3D打印機用戶手中，Gannon開發了一套名為「Tactum」的創新新系統。

Tactum 是一種新型軟體，讓使用者只需觸碰投影圖像，便能為3D打印機創作出屬於自己的獨特設計。使用者透過天生的手勢動作，可以戳按、摩擦，並以其他方式操控即將成為3D打印物件的投影圖像，並即時看到它隨之改變形狀。為了實現設計流程民主化的目標，Gannon 將她第一系列的 Tactum 成品設計在一個人人都能自由取用、本能操控的載體上——那就是人體本身。

「我的目標是將數位帶入實體世界，帶到你的身體上，」Gannon說。連同一個名為 Reverb 的配套專案——負責將這些使用者創作的設計轉換為可打印的網格——這股衝勁催生出了手鍊與項鍊設計的壯觀多樣性，從平滑的地景輪廓、繁複的紋理和自由奔放的混沌形態，到源自19世紀計時圖藝術的精緻幾何造型，不一而足。

英文原文

Madeline Gannon is a researcher, teacher at the Carnegie Mellon University School of Architecture and Ph·D· candidate in Computational Design — but that’s not all. She is on a mission to open up the infinite design possibilities of 3D printing to the world . "Currently you have to have a lot of technical background in order to participate in creating things for 3D printers," Gannon says. "There is still a huge knowledge barrier for how we create digital models." As the technology has advanced, prices have plummeted, and now anyone can buy a 3D printer for a few hundred dollars, Gannon notes. However, not just anyone can create original designs for 3D- printed artifacts . To put true creative power into the hands of any ordinary 3D printer owner, Gannon has developed an innovative new system called "Tactum" . Tactum is a new type of software that lets users create their own unique designs for 3D printers by simply touching a projected image . Using their innate hand gestures, someone using Tactum can poke, rub and otherwise manipulate the projected image that will become their 3D printed object, and see it instantly change shape in response. In keeping with the goal of democratizing the process, Gannon designed her first series of Tactum artifacts on a surface that everyone can access freely and manipulate instinctively, that being the human body. "My goal was to bring the digital out to the physical world and out onto your body," says Gannon. Along with a companion project called Reverb — which translates these user-created designs into rintable meshes — that impulse has resulted in a spectacular diversity of bracelet and necklace designs , ranging from smooth landscapes, intricate textures and chaotic free forms to delicate geometries derived from the 19th century art of chronograph.

#105 Modern Art (現代藝術) #060105 原文
中文翻譯

廣義而言，關於現代藝術有兩種不同的思考方式，或者說有兩種不同版本的詮釋故事。其中一種方式，是將藝術視為一種可以被實踐（並被理解）為與日常生活或世俗關懷截然分離的活動。
從這個角度來看，藝術被認為是「自主於」社會之外的——也就是說，它被視為自給自足、自我指涉的。
這個故事中一個特別具有影響力的版本認為，現代藝術應被視為一個過程：在此過程中，對某一特定藝術分支而言多餘的元素將被逐步淘汰，畫家或雕塑家將專注於其領域中特有的問題。
另一種關於現代藝術的思考方式，是將其視為對現代世界的回應，並將現代藝術家看作深入投身於社會衝突與挑戰之中的人。換言之，部分現代藝術家積極尋求方式，傳達歐洲在商業化（日常生活的商品化）與城市化這兩大進程推動下所產生的變遷體驗。
從這個角度來看，現代藝術是一種對那些催生出我們以「現代性」這一簡略說法所稱呼之事物的歷史轉變進行反思的方式。

英文原文

Broadly speaking, there are two different ways of thinking about modern art, or two different versions of the story . One way is to view art as something that can be practiced (And though of) as an activity radically separate from everyday life or worldly concerns. From this point of view, art is said to be "autonomous" from society – that is, it is believed to be self- sustaining and self-referring. One particularly influential versions of this story suggest that modern art should be viewed as process by which features extraneous to a particular branch of art would be progressively eliminated, and painters or sculptors would come to concentrate on problems specific to their domain. Another way of thinking about modern art is to view it as responding to the modern world, and to see modern artists immersing themselves in the conflicts and challenges of society . That is to say, some modern artists sought ways of conveying the changing experiences generated in European by the twin processes of commercialization (the commodification of everyday life) and urbanization. From this point of view, modern art is a way of reflecting on the transformation that created what we call, in a sort of shorthand, "modernity" .

2Another way of thinking about modern art is to view it as responding to the modern world, and to see modern artists immersing themselves in the conflicts and challenges of society . That is to say, some

#106 Upper Paleolithic (石器時代) #060106 原文
中文翻譯

舊石器時代晚期人們的生活方式，可以從散落在他們爐灶周圍的飲食殘跡，以及大量工具、武器和製作過程中留下的廢料中得以了解。這些人是獵人採集者，完全依靠自然界中所能獲取的食物維生，既不從事農業，也不從事畜牧。他們獵捕大型草食動物，而漿果、葉子、根莖、野果和蘑菇在他們的飲食中也可能扮演著重要角色。他們的狩獵毫無選擇性；或許因為當時動物數量龐大，他們無需顧及懷孕的雌性動物或幼獸。例如，在恩萊內洞穴中，發現了大量馴鹿和野牛胎兒的骨骸。顯然，舊石器時代晚期的人們像其他肉食動物一樣狩獵，優先獵殺最弱的獵物。然而，他們有時也會集中捕獵洄游的鮭魚群和遷徙的馴鹿群。與大眾對穴居人的普遍認知相反，舊石器時代晚期的人們並不居住在洞穴深處。他們更傾向於選擇懸崖腳下，尤其是當懸岩能提供良好遮蔽時。在平原和山谷中，他們用所獵殺動物的獸皮製成帳篷。有時，在廣袤的俄羅斯平原上，他們會用從哺乳動物骨骸上收集的巨大骨骼和象牙建造小屋。

男性主要使用長矛狩獵，弓箭很可能直到舊石器時代晚期末期的馬格達連期才被發明出來。以木材或馴鹿鹿角製成的工具和武器，通常鑲有燧石切刃。燧石打製工匠技藝精湛，燧石打製的傳統延續了數千年。這種延續性意味著他們必定仔細思考過如何尋找優質的燧石結核，以及如何打製它們，從而製作出刀具、鑿形工具或刮削器，這些工具可用於各種不同的用途。

英文原文

The ways of life Upper Paleolithic people are known through the remains of meals scattered around their hearths, together with many tools and weapons and the debris left over from their making. The people were hunter-gathers who lived exclusively from what they could find in nature without practicing either agriculture or herding. They hunted the bigger herbivores, while berries, leaves, roots, wild fruit and mushrooms probably played a major role in their diet. Their hunting was indiscriminate ; perhaps because so many animals were about they did not need to spare pregnant females or the young. In the cave of Enlene, for example, many bones of reindeer and bison fetuses were found. Apparently, upper Paleolithic people hunted like other predators and killed the weakest prey first. They did, however, sometimes concentrate on salmon suns and migrating herds of reindeer. Contrary to popular beliefs about cave man, upper Paleolithic people did not live deep inside caves . They rather chose the foot of cliffs , especially when an overhang provided good shelter. On the plains and in the valleys, they used tents made from hides of the animals they killed. At time, on the great Russian plains, they built huts with huge boned and tusks collected from skeletons of mammals. Men hunted mostly with spears , the bow and arrow were probably not invented until the Magdalenian period that came at the end of the Upper Paleolithic. Tools and weapons, made out of wood or reindeer antlers, often had flint cutting edges. Flint nappers were skillful and traditions in flint napping were purchased for thousands of years. This continuity means that they must have been carefully thought about how to find good flint modules and how to nap them in order to make knives, bruins (chisel-like tools) or scrapers, which could be used for various purposes.

#107 Volunteer program (志願者項目) #060107 原文
中文翻譯

如果你渴望為全球和平與發展採取具體行動，不妨了解聯合國志願人員（UNV）項目。

每年，多達8,000名來自約160個不同國籍、具備資格與經驗的男女志願者，將至少六個月的時間奉獻給幫助他人的事業。

這些聯合國志願人員在約130個國家開展工作，致力於促進和平、應對災難、賦能社區，並協助建立可持續的生計與持久的發展成果。

聯合國志願人員來自數十種不同的專業背景，但他們都是推動積極變革的催化劑。他們被鼓勵發揮創造力與創業精神，並在任務內外積極推廣服務於和平與發展的志願精神。他們深入社區核心，與各國政府、聯合國各機構及公民社會攜手合作。

擔任聯合國志願人員並非一份職業（目前服務年限上限為四年），但它蘊含豐富的機遇與經歷，並帶來巨大的個人收穫。作為聯合國志願人員，你將獲得志願者生活津貼（VLA），用以涵蓋基本生活需求、住房及水電費用。

此外，聯合國志願人員組織還將提供安置補助金、人壽保險、醫療保險及永久傷殘保險、往返機票，以及象徵性的重新安置津貼。

英文原文

If you are inspired to take concrete action for global peace and development, take a look at the United Nations Volunteers (UNV) program . Every year, up to 8,000 qualified and experienced women and men of some 160 different nationalities volunteer at least six months of their lives to help others . These UN Volunteers work in some 130 countries promoting peace, responding to disasters, empowering communities and helping to build sustainable livelihoods and lasting development. UN Volunteers come from dozens of professional backgrounds but all of them are catalysts of positive change . They are encouraged to be creative and entrepreneurial, and foster volunteerism for peace and development both within and beyond their assignments. They work at the heart of communities in partnership with governments, United Nations entities and civil society. Being a UN Volunteer is not a career (you are currently limited to four years of service), but it is rich with opportunities and experience and offers huge personal rewards . As a UN Volunteer you receive a Volunteer Living Allowance (VLA) which covers basic needs, housing and utilities. Additionally, UNV will provide a settling-in-grant, life, health, and permanent disability insurance, return airfares and a nominal resettlement allowance.

#108 Overqualified (資曆過高) #060108 原文
中文翻譯

如果你的招募活動吸引到經驗過於豐富的求職者——在這個疲軟的勞動市場中幾乎是必然的情況——你應該考慮採取一種與大多數招募主管慣常做法相悖的應對方式：不要一口回絕這些申請者，而是更仔細地審視他們。最新研究顯示，資歷過高的員工往往比其他員工表現更好，而且他們離職的時間也不會更早。 此外，一個簡單的管理策略——賦權——能夠緩解他們可能感受到的不滿。

對於能力過強員工的偏見十分普遍。 企業往往傾向於選擇「完美匹配」的申請者，而非那些智識、學歷或經驗超出職位需求的人。表面上，這種偏見似乎有其道理：多項研究一再顯示，自認資歷過高的員工會表現出較高程度的不滿情緒。 例如，資歷過高與工作不滿足感之間存在明顯相關性，這一點在以色列研究者索爾·費恩（Saul Fine）與巴魯克·內沃（Baruch Nevo）於2008年針對156名客服中心員工所做的研究中得到了印證。而且，與基於年齡或性別的歧視不同，以資歷過高為由拒絕錄用求職者，在法律上完全合規。

但即使在經濟衰退之前，資歷過高的求職者供過於求就已是全球性問題，在發展中國家尤為突出——當地教育水準的提升使勞動者具備的技能，已超過不斷擴張的服務業所需。如果管理者能夠突破傳統思維的框限，這批持續增長的優質求職者其實是一大機遇。來自奧勒岡州波特蘭州立大學的柏林·爾多安（Berrin Erdogan）與塔莉亞·鮑爾（Talya N. Bauer）發現，給予資歷過高的員工決策上的自主權，能夠消弭他們的不滿情緒。 在員工未感受到充分授權的門市中，「學歷過高」的員工所表現出的不滿明顯高於同事，也更傾向於表示有離職的意願。但在自評自主性較高的門市中，這種差異便消失了。

英文原文

If your recruiting efforts attract job applicants with too much experience—a near certainty in this weak labor market—you should consider a response that runs counter to most hiring managers’ MO: Don’t reject those applicants out of hand. Instead, take a closer look. New research shows that overqualified workers tend to perform better than other employees, and they don’t quit any sooner . Furthermore, a simple managerial tactic—empowerment—can mitigate any dissatisfaction they may feel. The prejudice against too-good employees is pervasive . Companies tend to prefer an applicant who is a "perfect fit" over someone who brings more intelligence, education, or experience than needed. On the surface, this bias makes sense: Studies have consistently shown that employees who consider themselves overqualified exhibit higher levels of discontent . For example, over- qualification correlated well with job dissatisfaction in a 2008 study of 156 call-center reps by Israeli researchers Saul Fine and Baruch Nevo. And unlike discrimination based on age or gender, declining to hire overqualified workers is perfectly legal. But even before the economic downturn, a surplus of overqualified candidates was a global problem , particularly in developing economies, where rising education levels are giving workers more skills than are needed to supply the growing service sectors. If managers can get beyond the conventional wisdom, the growing pool of too-good applicants is a great opportunity. Berrin Erdogan and Talya N· Bauer of Portland State University in Oregon found that overqualified workers’ feelings of dissatisfaction can be dissipated by giving them autonomy in decision making . At stores where employees didn’t feel empowered, "overeducated" workers expressed greater dissatisfaction than their colleagues did and were more likely to state an intention to quit. But that difference vanished where self-reported autonomy was high .

#109 Asda (阿斯達) #060109 原文
中文翻譯

阿斯達（Asda）憑藉與里茲大學的知識轉移夥伴關係（KTP），成為全國首家衡量顧客可透過減少食物浪費節省多少費用的食品零售商。KTP 背後的理念是由大學利用阿斯達的顧客洞察資料，將其研究成果應用於識別、調查並實施幫助顧客減少食物浪費的方法。這是大型零售商首次嘗試推動大規模永續發展改變之一，這個為期兩年的專案被視為阿斯達在此領域定位自身為真正創新者的途徑。

這項活動的重點是為顧客提供涵蓋食品儲存、標籤說明到剩菜創意食譜等各方面的建議。與此同時，店內活動鼓勵顧客在自己家中做出改變。事實上，已有兩百萬名顧客表示願意改變在家中處理食物浪費的方式，平均每位顧客可節省 57 英鎊，同時也減少了廢棄物。

KTP 的一個關鍵環節是由大學聘用一名合作夥伴，前往企業工作並協助達成 KTP 的預期成果。在與阿斯達的合作中，蘿拉·巴布斯（Laura Babbs）被賦予推動該零售商永續發展改變的任務。由於她工作成果卓著，蘿拉最終成為阿斯達團隊的正式成員。

英文原文

Asda has become the first food retailer in the country to measure how much customers can save by cutting back on food waste, thanks to a Knowledge Transfer Partnership (KTP) with the University of Leeds. The idea behind the KTP was for the University, using Asda’s customer insight data, to apply its research to identify, investigate and implement ways of helping customers to reduce their food waste. This was one of the first times that a major retailer had tried to deliver large-scale sustainability changes, with the two-year project seen as a way for Asda to position themselves as true innovators in this area . The campaign focused on providing customers with advice on everything from food storage and labelling, to creative recipes for leftovers . Meanwhile, in-store events encouraged customers to make changes in their own homes. In fact, two million customers have said they will make changes to how they deal with food waste in their own homes, leading to an average saving of 57 pounds per customer, as well as a reduction in waste. A key aspect of a KTP is that an associate is employed by the University to work in the firm and help deliver the desired outcomes of the KTP . As a part of the collaboration with Asda, Laura Babbs was given the task of driving forward the sustainability changes in the retailer. As a result of the success of her work, Laura eventually became a permanent member of the team at Asda.

#110 Blindness (白內障手術) #060110 原文
中文翻譯

科學家認為他們可能已找到一種方法，能夠預防白內障手術後可能出現的併發症，而白內障手術是全球失明的主要原因。
東英吉利大學（UEA）的研究人員詳細說明了手術後可能出現併發症的原因：儘管白內障手術能有效恢復視力，但手術後眼內總會殘留少量天然晶狀體細胞。隨著時間推移，眼睛的傷口癒合反應會導致這些細胞擴散至人工晶狀體的底面，從而干擾視力，造成所謂的「後囊膜混濁」，即次發性白內障。
主導該研究的UEA生物科學學院學者麥可·沃姆斯通博士表示：「次發性視力喪失對雷射手術治療反應良好。但隨著預期壽命的延長，白內障與後囊膜混濁的問題，無論是在患者健康福祉還是經濟負擔方面，都將變得更加嚴峻。我們必須在未來找到更好的方式來處理這一病症。」
因此，研究人員正在設計一種新型人工晶狀體，可置入保持開放狀態的囊袋中，而非像現行做法那樣收縮密封。研究人員相信，透過這種新方法，眼內液體可以在人工晶狀體周圍流動，從而稀釋並沖走促進細胞再生長的細胞信號分子。

英文原文

Scientists believe they may have found a way to prevent complications that can arise following cataract surgery , the world’s leading cause of blindness. Detailing why complications can occur after surgery, researchers from the University of East Anglia (UEA) explained that while cataract surgery works well to restore vision, a few natural lens cells always remain after the procedure. Over time, the eye’s wound-healing response leads these cells to spread across the underside of the artificial lens, which interferes with vision, causing what’s known as ‘posterior capsule opacification’ or secondary cataract. UEA’s School of Biological Sciences academic, Dr· Michael Wormstone, who led the study, said: "Secondary visual loss responds well to treatment with laser surgery. But as life expectancy increases, the problems of cataract and posterior capsule opacification will become even greater in terms of both patient well being and economic burden . It’s essential that we find better ways to manage the condition in future." As a result, researchers are designing new artificial lenses that can be placed into a capsular bag that stays open, instead of shrink-wrapping closed, which currently occurs. It is believed that, through the new approach, fluid in the eye can flow around the artificial lens, therefore diluting and washing away the cell-signaling molecules that encourage cell re-growth .

#111 Comparative advantage (相對優勢) #060111 原文
中文翻譯

相較於美國，中國、印度及其他開發中國家擁有大量低廉勞動力，因此這些國家專注於生產勞動密集型產品並不令人意外。基於類似原因，美國則因擁有相對豐富的高學歷勞動力與技術先進的設備，而專注於生產人力資本與實體資本密集型產品。

這種全球生產的分工，應能帶來比各國自行生產兩類商品更高的全球總產出。舉例而言，美國生產勞動密集型產品的成本較高，因其勞動力較昂貴；而開發中國家生產人力資本與實體資本密集型產品的成本也較高，因為這些生產要素在當地相對匱乏。由此邏輯可推論，美國不太可能成為綠色技術生產領域的主要全球競爭者——前提是這類技術並非相對依賴人力資本與實體資本。

然而，在新技術發展的早期階段，美國在生產由這些創新所帶動的產品方面具有比較優勢。然而，一旦這些技術廣為人知，且生產流程經過設計可運用較低技能的勞動力，生產便會向勞動力成本更低廉的國家轉移。

英文原文

With an abundance of low priced labor relative to the United States, it is no surprise that China, India and other developing countries specialize in the production of labor intensive products . For similar reasons, the United States will specialize in the production of goods that are human and physical capital intensive because of the relative abundance of a highly educated labor force and technically sophisticated equipment in the United States. This division of global production should yield higher global output of both types of goods than would be the case if each country attempted to produce both of these goods itself. For example, the United States would produce more expensive labor intensive goods because of its more expensive labor and the developing countries would produce more expensive human and physical capital intensive goods because of their relative scarcity of these inputs. This logic implies that the United States is unlikely to be a significant global competitor in the production green technologies that are not relatively intensive in human and physical capital. Nevertheless, during the early stages of the development of a new technology, the United States has a comparative advantage in the production of the products enabled by this innovation. However, once these technologies become well understood and production processes are designed that can make use of less skilled labor; production will migrate to countries with less expensive labor .

紅字句（原文）
#原文
1With an abundance of low priced labor relative to the United States, it is no surprise that China, India and other developing countries specialize in the production of labor intensive products . For similar reasons, the United States will specialize in the production of goods that are human and physical capital intensive because of the relative abundance of a highly educated labor force and technically
2This division of global production should yield higher global output of both types of goods than would
3comparative advantage in the production of the products enabled by this innovation. However, once these technologies become well understood and production processes are designed that can make use of less skilled labor; production will migrate to countries with less expensive labor .
#112 Plant Research (植物研究) #060112 原文
中文翻譯

植物是能量進入生物圈的管道，提供人類所需的食物與材料，並塑造我們的環境。根據 Ehrhardt 與 Frommer 的說法，當代人類面臨的三大挑戰是糧食、能源與環境惡化，而這三者都與植物息息相關。

我們所有的食物都由植物生產，無論是直接食用，或是間接透過以植物為食的動物而來。植物是 能源生產的來源，並與氣候變遷密切相關，也是各種環境問題的重要因素，包括農業擴張及其對棲地破壞與水道污染的影響。

此外，這些問題彼此之間並非相互獨立。氣候變遷對糧食供應及各類棲地造成額外壓力。因此，植物研究對於應對上述所有問題、邁向未來至關重要。為了使植物研究大幅向前推進，Ehrhardt 與 Frommer 表示科技發展至關重要，既要用於驗證現有假說，也要用於獲取新資訊並提出新假說。他們指出，若要在理解這些關鍵生物體的運作方式、並為永續未來奠定基礎方面取得進展，就必須將現有最先進的技術應用於植物生命的研究。

英文原文

Plants serve as the conduit of energy into the biosphere , provide food and materials used by humans, and they shape our environment. According to Ehrhardt and Frommer, the three major challenges facing humanity in our time are food, energy, and environmental degradation. All three are plant related. All of our food is produced by plants, either directly or indirectly via animals that eat them. Plants are a source of energy production . And they are intimately involved in climate change and a major factor in a variety of environmental concerns , including agricultural expansion and its impact on habitat destruction and waterway pollution. What’s more, none of these issues are independent of each other. Climate change places additional stresses on the food supply and on various habitats. So, plant research is instrumental in addressing all of these problems and moving into the future . For plant research to move significantly forward, Ehrhardt and Former say technological development is critical , both to test existing hypotheses and to gain new information and generate fresh hypotheses. If we are to make headway in understanding how these essential organisms function and build the foundation for a sustainable future, then we need to apply the most advanced technologies available to the study of plant life , they say.

#113 Human Remains (人類遺體) #060113 原文
中文翻譯

人類遺體是考古記錄的基本組成部分，為我們了解過去個人與群體的生活提供了獨特的視角。與許多考古材料相同，人類遺體需要獨特且專業的採集、分析與詮釋方法，而技術創新與專業知識的積累，使考古學家得以從骨骼材料的集合中提取出愈來愈豐富的資訊。除了對新出土文物的分析之外，這些進展也持續為博物館、大學及其他機構所收藏的現有人類遺體帶來新的啟示。鑑於死者遺體所承載的強烈情感、社會與宗教意涵，人類遺體為考古學家帶來一套獨特的倫理問題，這或許並不令人意外。

隨著原住民權利運動的興起與後殖民國家的出現，人類遺體的取得與所有權成為一個極具爭議、且帶有濃厚政治色彩的議題。世界各地博物館館藏中的許多人類遺體，代表著殖民剝削的痕跡以及已遭否定的偽科學種族理論，這一點日益清晰。在這些討論與觀念轉變的背景下，部分人類遺體被歸還或送返其原屬社群，這一過程延續至今。近年來，針對人類遺體研究的一批新挑戰從一個相當意想不到的方向浮現：英國政府修訂了其對十九世紀埋葬法規的詮釋，此舉將大幅限制考古學家研究在英格蘭與威爾斯境內出土、任何年代人類遺體的能力。本文審視這些非比尋常的事件，以及其所引發的法律、政治與倫理問題。

英文原文

Human remains are a fundamental part of the archaeological record, offering unique insights into the lives of individuals and populations in the past . Like many archaeological materials human remains require distinctive and specialized methods of recovery, analysis and interpretation, while technological innovations and the accumulation of expertise have enabled archaeologists to extract ever greater amounts of information from assemblages of skeletal material. Alongside analyses of new finds, these advances have consistently thrown new light on existing collections of human remains in museums, universities and other institutions. Given the powerful emotional, social and religious meanings attached to the dead body, it is perhaps unsurprising that human remains pose a distinctive set of ethical questions for archaeologists . With the rise of indigenous rights movements and the emergence of post-colonial nations, the acquisition and ownership of human remains became a divisive and politically loaded issue . It became increasingly clear that many human remains in museum collections around the world represented the traces of colonial exploitation and discredited pseudo-scientific theories of race. In the light of these debates and changing attitudes, some human remains were returned or repatriated to their communities of origin, a process which continues to this day . Recently a new set of challenges to the study of human remains has emerged from a rather unexpected direction: the British government revised its interpretation of nineteenth-century burial legislation in a way that would drastically curtail the ability of archaeologists to study human remains of any age excavated in England and Wales. This paper examines these extraordinary events and the legal, political and ethical questions that they raise.

#114 Giant panda (大熊貓) #060114 原文
中文翻譯

根據中國政府最新調查，全球野生大熊貓數量在過去十年間增加了268隻。野生大熊貓總數因此達到1,864隻。
與2003年上一次大熊貓調查相比，此次種群增長幅度達16.8%。野生大熊貓是全球野生動物保育的象徵，僅分布於中國四川、陝西及甘肅三省。
根據這份正式名稱為「第四次全國大熊貓調查」的報告，大熊貓在中國境內的 地理分布範圍同樣有所擴大。中國野生大熊貓目前的棲息地總面積達2,577,000公頃，自2003年以來擴增了11.8%。「這些成果充分證明了中國政府在保育工作上的卓越成就，」世界自然基金會中國區執行總監劉曉海表示。「野生大熊貓保育工作正在大力推進， 政府在整合各方努力、與包括世界自然基金會在內的保育組織攜手合作方面表現出色」。
這份報告是中國國家林業局每十年進行一次的系列調查中的第四次，於2011年在世界自然基金會的資金與技術支持下啟動。大熊貓種群數量的增加， 在很大程度上得益於中國政府推行的一系列保育政策，包括天然林保護工程及退耕還林工程。

英文原文

The worldwide population of wild giant pandas increased by 268 over the last decade according to a new survey conducted by the government of China. The increase in population brings the total number of wild giant pandas to 1,864. The population increase represents 16·8% rise compared to the last panda survey in 2003. Wild giant pandas, a global symbol of wildlife conservation, are found only in China's Sichuan, Shaanxi and Gansu provinces. According to the report, formally known as the Fourth National Giant Panda Survey, the geographic range of pandas throughout China also increased . The total area inhabited by wild giant pandas in China now equals 2,577,000 hectares, an expansion of 11·8% since 2003. "These results are a testament to the conservation achievements of the Chinese government," said Xiaohai Liu, executive director of programs, WWF-China. "A lot of good work is being done around wild giant panda conservation, and the government has done well to integrate these efforts and partner with conservation organizations including WWF" . The report, the fourth in a series of decadal (10 year) surveys conducted by the State Forestry Administration of China, began in 2011 with financial and technical support from WWF. Much of the success in increasing the panda population comes as a result of conservation policies implemented by the Chinese government , including the Natural Forest Protection Project and Grain for Green.

#115 National Prohibition Act (禁酒令) #060115 原文
中文翻譯

1920年，美國憲法第十八修正案為美國葡萄酒產業帶來了又一次沉重打擊。《全國禁酒法》，又稱《沃爾斯特法》，禁止以飲用為目的製造、銷售、運輸、進口、配送或持有含酒精飲料。

或許更值得注意的是，禁酒令允許任何人每年生產最多兩百加侖的果汁或蘋果酒。這種果汁有時會被製成濃縮液，非常適合用來釀酒。人們會從加州購買葡萄濃縮液，再運送到東岸。容器頂部印有醒目的粗體警語：注意：請勿添加糖或酵母，否則將會發酵！這批產品中有一部分流入了全美各地的非法酒販手中，他們偏偏就這麼做了。但好景不長，因為政府出手介入，禁止葡萄汁的銷售，遏制了非法釀酒活動。葡萄園停止種植，美國葡萄酒產業就此陷入停滯。

英文原文

In 1920, the eighteenth Amendment to the United States Constitution created yet another setback for the American wine industry. The National Prohibition Act, also known as the Volstead Act, prohibited the manufacture, sale, transportation, importation, delivery, or possession of intoxicating liquors for beverage purposes . Perhaps more important, prohibition allowed anyone to produce up to two hundred gallons yearly of fruit juice or cider . The fruit juice, which was sometimes made into concentrate, was ideal for making wine. People would buy grape concentrate from California and have it shipped to the East Coast. The top of the container was stamped in big bold letters: caution: do not add sugar or yeast or else fermentation will take place! Some of this yield found its way to bootleggers throughout America who did just that. But not for long, because the government stepped in and banned the sale of grape juice, preventing illegal wine production. Vineyards stopped being planted, and the American wine industry came to a halt .

#116 Language (語言) #060116 原文
中文翻譯

當人們開始思考語言這個議題時，腦中浮現的第一個問題往往是：語言對人類來說是否是天生的？——就像豬天生會咕嚕叫、狗天生會吠叫那樣。或者，語言只不過是我們碰巧學到的東西？——就像狗可以學會乞食、大象可以學會華爾滋、人類可以學會彈吉他那樣。

顯然，從某種意義上說，孩子會「學習」任何接觸到的語言，無論是中文、努特卡語還是英語。因此沒有人會否認「學習」非常重要。但關鍵問題在於：就語言而言，孩子出生時腦中是否是一張「白紙」——還是說人類天生就被「預設程式」了某種對語言結構的基本認知。

這個關於語言究竟部分源於天性、還是完全源於學習或後天培育的問題，通常被稱為先天與後天之爭，幾個世紀以來一直被人們討論。例如，這正是柏拉圖其中一篇對話錄《克拉底魯篇》的主題。那些已持續了數個世紀的爭論往往有其特定的發展規律：它們會沉寂一段時間，然後再度激烈爆發。這個特定議題於1959年在語言學界再度浮上檯面，起因是語言學家諾姆·喬姆斯基對哈佛心理學家B·F·史金納所著《言語行為》一書撰寫了一篇犀利而不失幽默的評論。（Skinner 1957；Chomsky 1959）。這本書聲稱要把語言「解釋」為一套多年來逐漸養成的習慣。根據史金納的觀點，不需要任何複雜的先天機制或心理機制。所需要的一切，只是對外部世界中促使說話者發出聲音的事件進行系統性的觀察。

英文原文

When people start thinking about language, the first question which often occurs to them is this: is language natural to humans ? - in the same way that grunting is natural to pigs, and barking comes naturally to dogs. Or is it just something we happen to have learned? - in the same way that dogs may learn to beg, or elephants may learn to waltz, or humans may learn to play the guitar. Clearly, in one sense, children 'learn' whatever language they are exposed to, be it Chinese, Nootka or English. So no one would deny that 'learning' is very important. But the crucial question is whether children are born with 'blank sheets' in their head as far as language is concerned - or whether humans are 'programmed' with an outline knowledge of the structure of languages in general. This question of whether language is partly due to nature or wholly due to learning or nurture is often referred to as the nature-nurture controversy , and has been discussed for centuries. For example, it was the topic of one of Plato's dialogues, the Cratylus. Controversies which have been going on for literally ages tend to behave in a characteristic fashion. They lie dormant for a while, then break out fiercely. This particular issue resurfaced in linguistics in 1959 when the linguist Noam Chomsky wrote a devastating and witty review of Verbal Behavior, a book by the Harvard psychologist B·F· Skinner (Skinner 1957; Chomsky 1959). This book claimed to 'explain' language as a set of habits gradually built up over the years . According to Skinner, no complicated innate or mental mechanisms are needed. All that is necessary is the systematic observation of the events in the external world which prompt the speaker to utter sounds.

#117 Academics (學術) #060117 原文
中文翻譯

認識學術同仁，尤其是資歷更深的前輩，往往令人望而生畏。講師和研究人員習慣於長時間獨立工作、埋頭苦幹。「公開亮相」和「推銷自己」這樣的想法似乎毫無吸引力。然而，開始建立有助於職涯發展的人脈網絡，其實比你想像的容易得多。你的博士指導教授和口試委員，或者如果你已在職，你的導師，都是很好的起點。他們之所以被選來指導你，是因為他們更有經驗，而且在大多數情況下，他們的研究領域與你的興趣方向相近。向他們請教如何建立自己的人脈聯絡網。此外，如果你能提及一位共同認識的人的名字，與陌生人搭話也會容易得多。

如果你是一位認真考慮學術生涯的研究生，或是一位希望拓展發展的資深學者，你必然會相當定期地出席學術會議。出席的場次沒有所謂的對與錯，有些學者每年只參加一兩場，有些人似乎每個月都要參加一場！學術會議是學者們相互建立人脈的主要方式，因此千萬不要錯過這些機會。如果你正在發表論文，這讓其他人有機會了解你的研究內容，而議程中的非正式環節（例如餐飲休息時間）則能促進交流與進一步的討論。

英文原文

Getting to know fellow academics , especially more senior ones, can be very daunting . Lecturers and researchers are used to spending a lot of time in isolation working independently. The thought of going public and ‘selling yourself' does not seem enticing. However, it is easier than you think to begin to develop your own career-enhancing networks . Your PhD supervisor and examiners or if you are already in post, your mentor, are a great place to start . They will have been chosen to guide you because they are more experienced and in most cases they will work close to your field of interest . Ask their advice for ways of building up your own network of contacts. Also it is easier to approach someone unknown to you if you can mention the name of a mutual acquaintance. If you are a postgraduate who is serious about a career in academia, or a more senior scholar wanting to develop one, you will surely be attending conferences on a fairly regular basis. There is no right or wrong number of these, some scholars stick to one or two a year, others seem to attend one a month! Conferences are the main way that academics network with each other , so do not miss out on these opportunities. If you are presenting a paper it gives others a chance to see what you are working on, and the informal sections of the programmed (such as food and drink breaks) encourage mingling and further discussion.

#118 Frog (青蛙) #060118 原文
中文翻譯

墨西哥恰帕斯州一名礦工發現了一隻保存於琥珀中、距今已有兩千五百萬年歷史的微型樹蛙，
一名研究人員表示。若獲得鑑定確認，這隻保存完好的青蛙將是墨西哥境內首度發現的同類標本，
美國自然歷史博物館生物學家暨館長大衛·格里馬爾迪（David Grimaldi）如此表示，他並未參與此次發現。
包裹著這隻青蛙的琥珀塊不到半英寸長，於2005年由一名礦工在墨西哥南部恰帕斯州挖掘出土，隨後被一位私人收藏家購入，並借給科學家進行研究。
此前已有少數保存完好的青蛙在琥珀塊中被發現——琥珀是由古代樹脂形成的礦石——大多出土於多明尼加共和國。與那些標本類似，在恰帕斯州發現的這隻青蛙似乎屬於克勞加斯托屬（Craugastor），
其後代至今仍棲息於該地區，恰帕斯州自然歷史與生態研究所生物學家赫拉爾多·卡博特（Gerardo Carbot）說道。
卡博特於本週宣布了這一發現。

該科學家表示，根據發現琥珀所在地的地質層位，判斷這隻青蛙生活於約兩千五百萬年前。
卡博特希望從青蛙遺骸中提取樣本，以期找到能夠鑑定具體物種的DNA，
但他懷疑收藏者是否願意讓他對這塊石頭進行鑽取採樣。

英文原文

A miner in the state of Chiapas found a tiny tree frog that has been preserved in amber for 25 million years , a researcher said.If authenticated, the preserved frog would be the first of its kind found in Mexico , according to David Grimaldi, a biologist and curator at the American Museum of Natural History, who was not involved in the find. The chunk of amber containing the frog, less than half an inch long, was uncovered by a miner in Mexico’s southern Chiapas state in 2005 and was bought by a private collector, who loaned it to scientists for study. A few other preserved frogs have been found in chunks of amber — a stone formed by ancient tree sap — mostly in the Dominican Republic. Like those, the frog found in Chiapas appears to be of the genus Craugastor , whose descendants still inhabit the region, said biologist Gerardo Carbot of the Chiapas Natural History and Ecology Institute. Carbot announced the discovery this week. The scientist said the frog lived about 25 million years ago, based on the geological strata where the amber was found. Carbot would like to extract a sample from the frog’s remains in hopes of finding DNA that could identify the particular species but doubts the owner would let him drill into the stone.

#119 Family dinner (家庭晚餐) #060119 原文
中文翻譯

作為一名家庭治療師，我常常有衝動告訴家庭們回家一起吃晚飯，而不是花一個小時和我在一起。20年來在北美、歐洲和澳洲進行的研究支持了我對家庭晚餐的熱情。事實證明，每晚坐下來吃飯對大腦、身體和心靈都大有裨益。而且每晚的晚餐不必是花了三個小時烹調的美食，也不需要用有機芝麻菜和傳家寶歐防風製作。

首先，研究人員發現，對幼兒來說，晚餐時的對話比大聲朗讀更能促進詞彙量的增長。研究人員統計了家庭在晚餐對話中使用的生僻詞彙數量——即那些不在3,000個最常用詞彙列表中的詞。幼兒在餐桌上學到了1,000個生僻詞彙，相比之下，父母大聲朗讀故事書只能讓他們學到143個。擁有大量詞彙的孩子閱讀起步更早、也更輕鬆。年齡較大的孩子同樣能從家庭晚餐中獲得智識上的益處。對學齡兒童來說，規律的用餐時間在預測高學業成績方面，甚至比在學校上課、做作業、參加體育運動或從事藝術活動所花費的時間更具影響力。其他研究人員也報告了一致的關聯，即家庭晚餐頻率與青少年學業表現之間存在顯著關係。

每週與家人共餐5至7次的青少年，在學校獲得優異成績的可能性，是每週與家人共餐不足兩次的青少年的兩倍。

英文原文

As a family therapist, I often have the impulse to tell families to go home and have dinner together rather than spending an hour with me. And 20 years of research in North America, Europe, and Australia back up my enthusiasm for family dinners. It turns out that sitting down for a nightly meal is great for the brain, the body, and the spirit . And that nightly dinner doesn’t have to be a gourmet meal that took three hours to cook, nor does it need to be made with organic arugula and heirloom parsnips. For starters, researchers found that for young children, dinnertime conversation boosts vocabulary even more than being read aloud to. The researchers counted the number of rare words – those not found on a list of 3,000 most common words – that the families used during dinner conversations. Young kids learned 1,000 rare words at the dinner table , compared to only 143 from parents reading storybooks aloud. Kids who have a large vocabulary read earlier and more easily. Older children also reap intellectual benefits from family dinners . For school-age youngsters, regular mealtime is an even more powerful predictor of high achievement scores than time spent in school, doing homework, playing sports or doing art. Other researchers reported a consistent association between family dinner frequency and teen academic performance . Adolescents who ate family meals 5 to 7 times a week were twice as likely to get an A in school as those who ate dinner with their families fewer than two times a week.

#120 Museology (博物學) #060120 原文
中文翻譯

博物學是什麼？簡單來說，它是對博物館的研究，涵蓋其歷史與
基本理念、博物館在歷史發展過程中以各種方式建立
與演進的脈絡、其明示或隱含的目標與政策、以及其教育、政治或社會功能。
從更宏觀的角度來看，這樣的研究也可能涵蓋形形色色的受眾——
參觀者、學者、藝術愛好者、孩童——這些人都是博物館工作人員努力服務的對象，此外還包括相關議題，例如博物館所承擔（或自願履行）的法律義務與責任，乃至對其未來的若干思考。
如此看來，博物學乍看之下似乎是一門極度專業的學科，只與
博物館專業人員有關——他們因職業性質而多少有義務對此感興趣。
然而事實上，博物館的歷史幾乎與人類文明本身一樣悠久，而當今
數量龐大的博物館幾乎涵蓋了人類活動的每一個領域——不僅是藝術、工藝或
科學，還有娛樂、農業、鄉村生活、童年、漁業、古物、汽車：這份清單
無窮無盡——因此博物學是一個廣博的探究領域，幾乎與每個人都息息相關。

英文原文

What is museology? A simple definition might be that it is the study of museums, their history and underlying philosophy , the various ways in which they have, in the course of time, been established and developed, their avowed or unspoken aims and policies, their educative or political or social role. More broadly conceived, such a study might also embrace the bewildering variety of audiences — visitors, scholars, art lovers, children- at whom the efforts of museum staff are supposedly directed, as well as related topics such as the legal duties and responsibilities placed upon (or incurred by) museums, perhaps even some thought as to their future. Seen in this light, museology might appear at first sight a subject so specialized as to concern only museum professionals , who by virtue of their occupation are more or less obliged to take an interest in it. In reality, since museums are almost, if not quite as old as civilization itself, and since the plethora of present-day museums embraces virtually every field of human endeavor - not just art, or craft, or science, but entertainment, agriculture, rural life, childhood, fisheries, antiquities, automobiles: the list is endless- it is a field of enquiry so broad as to be a matter of concern to almost everybody .

#原文

2More broadly conceived, such a study might also embrace the bewildering variety of audiences —
