#121 Read aloud (大聲朗讀) #060121 原文
中文翻譯

大聲朗讀自己的作品或許看起來有點古怪，但這樣做有助於找出文章中最含糊不清的
地方。最有效的做法是以富有戲劇感的方式朗讀，在逗號和句尾處停頓。
如果你在念完一個句子之前就上氣不接下氣，那這個句子可能太長了。你應該能夠用這種方式把文章轉化成演講稿——如果聽起來過於生硬繁瑣，或許可以修改這些段落，直到聽起來流暢自然為止。讀者不太可能
被「用長詞顯得聰明」的想法所矇騙。在句子中堆砌過多
複雜的詞彙，反而可能使其意思完全無法被理解。短詞永遠比長詞好。
為什麼寫文章時要用 erroneous 這個字，而不直接用 wrong？通常，使用較晦澀詞彙的作者是想顯得博學，但反而可能給人裝腔作勢的印象。直白的詞語讓你能夠掌控自己所要表達的內容，這樣的選擇並不幼稚，而是最適合當下情境的用字。當你大聲朗讀自己的文字時，你會發現
句子中的重音落在句尾。因此，以簡短有力的詞語結尾是最有效的方式，
能夠鞏固你的論點。
盡量克制在句尾拖泥帶水、加上一長串附帶子句的衝動。如果你覺得某個子句對句子意思貢獻不大，不妨考慮將它移到句首，或者直接刪掉。
你的句子或許在文法上無懈可擊，但如果語氣拿捏不當，仍然會讓文章讀起來怪異。使用俚語和感嘆詞的口語風格，對於文章而言是過於隨意的語氣。然而，如果你的詞彙
對於所處語境來說過於正式或艱深，文風同樣會顯得突兀。用簡單的語言和文法表達複雜的觀點，
才是真正令人印象深刻的做法。

英文原文

It might seem a little eccentric but reviewing your work by reading it aloud can help to identify the woolliest areas . This works best if you perform your reading in a theatrical way, pausing at the commas and ends of sentences. If you run out of breath during a sentence, it is probably too long. You ought to be able to convert your writing into a speech in this way if it sounds too stilted and convoluted, perhaps you could rework these parts until they sound fluid. It is unlikely that your reader will be fooled by the idea that long words make you sound clever. Cluttering a sentence with too many complicated words can prevent its meaning from being understood at all . A short word is always preferable to a long one. Why should anyone choose the word erroneous over the word wrong in an essay? Usually, writers who employ more obscure words are trying to sound impressive but can appear pretentious. Direct words enable you to control what you are saying, and are not necessarily babyish, but the most appropriate ones for the job. When you read your writing aloud, you will notice that the key stress comes at the end of your sentence. It is , therefore, most effective to end with a short and emphatic word to secure our point . Try to resist the impulse to waffle at the end of your sentence by trailing off into qualifying clauses. It might be worth relocating the clause to the beginning of the sentence or losing it altogether if you feel that it adds little to its meaning. Your sentences might be the most grammatically perfect in the world, but still, cause your writing to sound wrong if you have misjudged its tone. A colloquial style, which uses slang and exclamations, is an inappropriately chatty tone for an essay. However, style can be equally jarring if your vocabulary is too formal or ambitious for its context. It is much more impressive to make complicated points using simple language and grammar.

2fooled by the idea that long words make you sound clever. Cluttering a sentence with too many complicated words can prevent its meaning from being understood at all . A short word is always
3key stress comes at the end of your sentence. It is , therefore, most effective to end with a short and emphatic word to secure our point . Try to resist the impulse to waffle at the end of your sentence by
4too formal or ambitious for its context. It is much more impressive to make complicated points using simple language and grammar.
#122 Armed police in NSW (新州警察) #060122 原文
中文翻譯

武裝警察已進駐新州學校，以降低犯罪率並對學生進行教育。共有40名學校聯絡警察（SLP）被分配至全州各地的公立及私立中學。主辦方表示，這些於上週開始履職的警員將在警方與學生之間建立正向關係。然而，家長團體警告，在警民關係已趨緊張的社區中，讓武裝警察在學校工作可能帶來潛在風險。

學校聯絡警察的職責包括舉辦犯罪預防工作坊，就商店行竊、妨礙公眾行為、塗鴉以及毒品與酒精等議題與學生進行討論。他們也可為校長提供建議。其中一名學校聯絡警察、警員本·珀維斯於上週開始在悉尼內城區域服務，服務範圍涵蓋亞歷山德里亞公園社區學校高年級校區。他此前擔任岩石區的犯罪預防警員，現在管轄範圍擴及岩石區、雷德芬及國王十字等地區的27所學校。珀維斯警員表示，這個全職職位將讓他致力於更廣泛的犯罪預防工作。「我不是保安，」他說，「我不是去學校巡邏的。我們希望改善警方與在校學生的關係，促進正向互動。我們到學校來，是為了給他們知識，讓他們能提升自身的安全意識。」

家長團體對該計畫作出正面回應，但表示此舉可能引發各種社區反應。「這是一件好事，也是一個創新的想法，可能帶來一些正面效益，」天主教學校家長委員會執行幹事表示。

英文原文

Armed police have been brought into NSW schools to reduce crime rates and educate students . The 40 School Liaison Police (SLP) officers have been allocated to public and private high schools across the state. Organizers say the officers, who began work last week, will build positive relationships between police and students. But parent groups warned of potential dangers of armed police working at schools in communities where police relations were already under strain. Among their duties, the SLPs will conduct crime prevention workshops, talking to students about issues including shoplifting, offensive behavior, graffiti and drugs and alcohol. They can also advise school principals . One SLP, Constable Ben Purvis, began work in the inner Sydney region last week, including at Alexandria Park Community School's senior campus. Previously stationed as a crime prevention officer at The Rocks, he now has 27 schools under his jurisdiction in areas including The Rocks, Redfern and Kings Cross. Constable Purvis said the full time position would see him working on the broader issues of crime prevention. "I am not a security guard," he said. "I am not there to patrol the school. We want to improve relationships between police and schoolchildren, to have positive interaction. We are coming to the school and giving them knowledge to improve their own safety." Parents' groups responded to the program positively, but said it may spark a range of community reactions . "It is a good thing and an innovative idea and there could be some positive benefits," Council of Catholic School Parents executive officer.

#123 Crop rotation (輪作) #060123 原文
中文翻譯

透過良好的輪作制度，尤其是加上任何你能取得的肥料，在一塊土地上連續耕種 2 至 3 年並獲得良好收成是有可能的。然而，若你希望長期持續耕作，終究還是必須讓土地休息。讓一塊土地休養一段時間，稱為「讓田地休耕」，這樣做有幾個原因。

讓一塊田地或土地休耕，意思是在至少一年內不在上面種植任何新作物、不進行收割，也不讓任何牲畜在土地上放牧。有時一塊田地會休耕兩年、三年甚至四年，但許多農場的傳統慣例是每 2 至 3 年讓田地休耕一次。

這段休耕期能讓土地補充許多養分。各種草類或地被植物（如三葉草）的根系有機會擴展生長，進一步強化土壤並防止水土流失。

在休耕期間，土壤中存在許多有益的植物菌群和微小生物，包括藍藻菌。這些微生物在根部層面持續活動，穩定地改善土壤品質，使你在一兩年後回來時，能夠重新開始種植糧食作物或經濟作物。

英文原文

With a good system of crop rotation , and especially with the addition of any sort of fertilizer you may be able to come up with, it’s possible to grow crops on a plot of land for upwards of 2 – 3 years at a time with good results. Ultimately, though, you must let the land rest if you hope to continue farming there in the long-run. Allowing a plot of land to rest for a period of time is known as letting the field go fallow , and there are several reasons for this. Allowing a field or plot to lie fallow means that you don’t grow anything new on it, don’t harvest anything and don’t graze any animals on the land for at least a year. Sometimes a field will lay fallow for two, three or even four years, but the traditional standard on many farms was to let a field lie fallow once every 2 – 3 years. This fallow period allows the land to replenish many of its nutrients . The root networks of various grasses or groundcovers (like clover) have a chance to expand and grow, which further strengthens the soil and protects it from erosion. During the fallow period, there are many beneficial flora and micro-fauna , including cyanobacteria, which live in the soil. These microorganisms continue to be active at the root level, steadily improving the quality of the soil so that when you come back in a year or two, you can begin planting food or cash crops anew.

2there in the long-run. Allowing a plot of land to rest for a period of time is known as letting the field go fallow , and there are several reasons for this.
3This fallow period allows the land to replenish many of its nutrients . The root networks of various

#124 Malaysia travel (馬來西亞旅遊) #060124 原文
中文翻譯

馬來西亞是東南亞最令人愉快、最輕鬆愜意的旅遊國家之一。除了閃耀的21世紀玻璃高樓外，這裡還擁有該地區最壯麗的海灘、山脈
與國家公園。馬來西亞也正在推出有史以來規模最大的旅遊宣傳活動，致力於
吸引今年2000萬名遊客前來造訪。2005年（最後一個擁有完整統計數據的年份）共有超過1600萬名遊客到訪。在來自西方的88.5萬名旅客中，有24萬人來自英國，26.5萬人來自澳大利亞，15萬人來自美國。

任何旅遊行程都必須從首都吉隆坡開始，在這裡你將看到石油雙峰塔——曾經是世界最高建築，如今位居第二高的寶座。這兩座各88層樓的塔樓高聳入雲，達452公尺（1,480英尺），並由一座位於第41層的空中廊橋相連。同樣值得一遊的是中央市場——這棟戰前建築曾是城市的主要濕貨市場，現已蛻變為藝術與文化中心。石灰岩神廟黑風洞位於市區以北15公里（9英里）處，擁有高達100公尺（328英尺）的岩洞天花板，並設有精美的印度教神祠，包括一尊高43公尺（141英尺）的金色印度神明雕像。遊客必須攀登272級陡峭的台階才能抵達洞窟。在婆羅洲島上的沙巴州，你會發現小巧的蘑菇形仙本那島就坐落於沙巴外海，被評為全球前五大潛水勝地之一。仙本那是馬來西亞唯一的海洋島嶼，從西里伯斯海700公尺（2,300英尺）深的海底拔地而起。

你還可以攀登東南亞最高峰神山，參觀西必洛紅毛猩猩保育中心，體驗激流泛舟，並一睹奇特的長鼻猴——這種靈長類動物只生活在婆羅洲，擁有碩大下垂的鼻子、標誌性的圓滾肚腩，以及獨特的鳴叫
聲。在馬來西亞期間，不妨考慮前往馬六甲一遊。在其全盛時期，這個南部州屬曾是強大的馬來蘇丹國，也是該地區蓬勃發展的貿易港口。面向馬六甲海峽，這個歷史古州如今遍布迷人的華人街道、古董店、古老廟宇，以及歐洲殖民強權留下的印記。另一個有趣的目的地是檳城，被稱為「東方之珠」。這座位於馬來西亞西北海岸外的島嶼，以豐富的華人文化遺產、美食與美麗的海灘聞名於世。

英文原文

Malaysia is one of the most pleasant, hassle-free countries to visit in Southeast Asia . Aside from its gleaming 21st century glass towers, it boasts some of the most superb beaches, mountains and national parks in the region. Malaysia is also launching its biggest-ever tourism campaign in effort to lure 20 million visitors here this year . More than 16 million tourists visited in 2005, the last year for which complete statistics were available. Of the 885,000 travelers from the West, 240,000 were from the United Kingdom, 265,000 from Australia and 150,000 from the US. Any tourist itinerary would have to begin in the capital, Kuala Lumpur , where you will find the Petronas Twin Towers, which once comprised the world's tallest buildings and now hold the title of second- tallest. Both the 88-story towers soar 452 meters (1,480 feet) high and are connected by a sky-bridge on the 41st floor. Also, worth visiting is the Central Market , a pre-war building that was the main wet market for the city, and has now been transformed into an arts and cultural center. The limestone temple Batu Caves , located 15 kilometers (9 miles) north of the city, have a 100-meter-high (328-foot- high) ceiling and feature ornate Hindu shrines, including a 43-meter-tall (141-foot-tall) gold-painted statue of a Hindu deity. To reach the caves, visitors have to climb a steep flight of 272 steps. In Sabah state on Borneo island, you'll find the small mushroom-shaped Sipadan island, off the coast of Sabah, rated as one of the top five diving sites in the world. Sipadan is the only oceanic island in Malaysia, rising from a 700-meter (2,300-foot) abyss in the Celebes Sea. You can also climb Mount Kinabalu , the tallest peak in Southeast Asia, visit the Sepilok Orang Utan Sanctuary, go white-water rafting and catch a glimpse of the bizarre Proboscis monkey, a primate found only in Borneo with a huge pendulous nose, a characteristic pot belly and strange honking sounds. While you're in Malaysia, consider a trip to Malacca . In its heyday, this southern state was a powerful Malay sultanate and a booming trading port in the region. Facing the Straits of Malacca, this historical state is now a place of intriguing Chinese streets, antique shops, old temples and reminders of European colonial powers. Another interesting destination is Penang , known as the "Pearl of the Orient.'' This island off the northwest coast of Malaysia boasts of a rich Chinese cultural heritage, good food and beautiful beaches.

#125 School bullying (校園霸淩) #060125 原文
中文翻譯

由於感到南尤克里德市學生的失序行為日益增加，校園資源警察（SRO）審查了有關轉介至校長室的相關數據。他發現高中每年有數千件霸淩轉介案，而初中最近的霸淩轉介案也增加了30%。警察數據顯示，在過去10年中，課後時間有關騷擾、霸淩和攻擊行為的青少年投訴增加了90%。

校園資源警察與一名社工及大學研究員密切合作。他們組建了一個應對規劃小組，由多方利益相關者組成，旨在回應初步分析中確認的各個問題領域。環境方面的改變包括調整課程時間表，以及加強教師對問題熱點區域的監督。輔導員和社工為教師開設了衝突調解與霸淩預防培訓課程。家長教育方面則包括寄送含有霸淩相關資訊的郵件、說明新的學校政策，以及討論在家中可採取哪些措施來應對問題。

最後，學生教育方面包括班主任與學生的課堂討論，以及由校園資源警察主持的全校集會。校園資源警察也在一個主要熱點區域旁開設了一個分站。俄亥俄州教育廳出資開設了一個新的培訓中心，為有特殊需求的學生提供非傳統的輔導環境。

各項應對措施的成效顯著。學校停學人數下降了40%。走廊的霸淩事件減少了60%，健身房區域的霸淩事件更減少了80%。後續調查顯示，學生對霸淩的態度有了正向轉變，且更多學生相信當問題發生時，教師會採取行動。教師表示培訓課程很有幫助，他們也更願意將霸淩視為嚴肅議題加以討論。家長反應正面，並要求在未來的郵件中提供更多相關資訊。整體結果顯示，學校環境不僅更加安全，及早介入也正在幫助高風險學生在學業上取得成功（南尤克里德（俄亥俄州）警察局，2001年）。

英文原文

Spurred by the sense that disorderly behavior among students in South Euclid was increasing, the school resource officer (SRO) reviewed data regarding referrals to the principal's office. He found that the high school reported thousands of referrals a year for bullying and that the junior high school had recently experienced a 30 percent increase in bullying referrals. Police data showed that juvenile complaints about disturbances, bullying, and assaults after school hours had increased 90 percent in the past 10 years. The SRO worked in close collaboration with a social worker and the university researcher . They coordinated a Response Planning Team comprising many stakeholders that was intended to respond to each of the areas identified in the initial analysis. Environmental changes included modifying the school schedule and increasing teacher supervision of hotspots. Counsellors and social workers conducted teacher training courses in conflict resolution and bullying prevention. Parent education included mailings with information about bullying, an explanation of the new school policy, and a discussion about what could be done at home to address the problems. Finally, student education included classroom discussions between homeroom teachers and students, as well as assemblies conducted by the SRO. The SRO also opened a substation next to a primary hotspot. The Ohio Department of Education contributed by opening a new training center to provide a non-traditional setting for specialized help . The results from the various responses were dramatic. School suspensions decreased 40 percent. Bullying incidents dropped 60 percent in the hallways and 80 percent in the gym area. Follow- up surveys indicated that there were positive attitudinal changes among students about bullying and that more students felt confident that teachers would take action when a problem arose. Teachers indicated that training sessions were helpful and that they were more likely to talk about bullying as a serious issue. Parents responded positively, asking for more information about the problem in future mailings. The overall results suggest that the school environments were not only safer; but that early intervention was helping at-risk students succeed in school (South Euclid (Ohio) Police Department, 2001).

#126 Sochi Olympics (索契冬奧會) #060126 原文
中文翻譯

全球主要體育賽事——從2014年索契冬奧會到挪威峽灣年度快艇賽——正致力於抵銷其碳足跡，作為全球氣候網絡的一部分，聯合國環境規劃署（UNEP）今日表示。

聯合國環境規劃署執行主任阿基姆·施泰納表示，這些體育賽事是加入該網絡的最新成員，對於激勵全球進一步採取環境行動尤為重要。

「無論是在田徑場上還是在冰雪之中，體育賽事都能在數千名參賽者和全球數十億名觀眾心中點燃追求卓越的精神，」施泰納先生說。

「因此，令人振奮的是，這種對卓越的熱情日益涵蓋環境表現，體育組織在每一場賽事中不斷提高標準，」他補充道。

2014年索契冬季奧運會暨殘奧會的主辦方表示，賽事將在黑海海岸與白雪皚皚的高加索山脈之間的獨特自然環境中舉行，他們將投入約17.5億美元用於節能與可再生能源。

這筆投資將用於改善交通基礎設施、抵銷電力使用、航空旅行及地面交通所產生的溫室氣體排放、索契國家公園的植樹造林以及城市綠化帶的建設。

英文原文

Major athletic events around the globe – from the 2014 Sochi Olympics to an annual powerboat race in Norwegian fjords – are striving to neutralize their carbon footprint as part of a world- wide climate network , the United Nations Environment Programme (UNEP) said today. The sporting events are the latest participants to join the network, and are particularly important for inspiring further global action on the environment , said Achim Steiner, UNEP Executive Director. "Whether carried out on track and field or on ice and snow, sporting events ignite the spirit of achievement in thousands of competitors and billions of spectators worldwide," Mr· Steiner said. "It is, therefore, heartening that this passion for excellence increasingly encompasses environmental performance, with sporting organizations raising the bar ever higher at each and every tournament," he added. Organizers of the 2014 Sochi Olympic and Paralympic Winter Games – to be held in a unique natural setting between the shores of the Black Sea and the soaring snow-capped Caucasus Mountains – say they will put an estimated $1·75 billion into energy conservation and renewable energy . That investment will be dedicated to improving transport infrastructure, offsetting greenhouse gas emissions from the use of electricity, air travel and ground transportation, the reforestation of Sochi National Park and the development of green belts in the city.

#127 Humans and animals (人和動物) #060127 原文
中文翻譯

所有非人類動物都受到大自然透過自然選擇賦予牠們的工具所約束。牠們無法追求真理；只是單純吸收資訊，並以對自身生存有利的方式行動。演化已大致預先篩選了牠們所需要的世界知識種類。沒有任何動物能夠提出與其眼前處境或演化設計的需求無關的問題，或產生此類困惑。當海狸建造水壩時，牠不會問自己為何這樣做，或是否有更好的方式。當燕子南飛時，牠不會好奇非洲為何較熱，或若繼續往更南方飛會發生什麼事。

人類確實會問自己這些以及許多其他種類的問題——這些問題在演化需求與目標的脈絡下毫不相干，甚至幾乎毫無意義。人類的獨特之處在於我們有能力超越自然賦予我們的目標——例如尋找食物、棲身之所或伴侶的需求——進而建立由人類自身創造的目標。

英文原文

All non-human animals are constrained by the tools that nature has bequeathed them through natural selection . They are not capable of striving towards truth; they simply absorb information, and behave in ways useful for their survival. The kinds of knowledge they require of the world have been largely pre-selected by evolution . No animal is capable of asking questions or generating problems that are irrelevant to its immediate circumstances or its evolutionarily designed needs. When a beaver builds a dam, it doesn't ask itself why it does so or whether there is a better way of doing it. When a swallow flies south, it doesn't wonder why it is hotter in Africa or what would happen if it flew still further south. Humans do ask themselves these and many other kinds of questions, questions that have no relevance , indeed make little sense, in the context of evolved needs and goals . What marks out humans is our capacity to go beyond our naturally defined goals such as the need to find food, shelter or a mate and to establish human created goals.

#128 Australian food (澳大利亞飲食） #060128 原文
中文翻譯

澳大利亞在周期性地追尋烹飪身份認同時，自然而然地將目光投向本土食材——那些原產於這片土地的食物。正如Stephanie Alexander所指出的，使用本土食材無疑能使一道菜肴具備澳大利亞的資格。
同樣地，有人毫無保留地聲稱，「獨特的澳大利亞飲食文化只能建立在這個國家原產的食物之上」，儘管如Craw所言，將澳大利亞原生食物作為國家象徵，更多依賴的是它們與「自然」及地理起源的關聯，而非日常使用的普遍性。

撇開「國菜必然以本國原產食材為基礎」這一前提缺乏充分依據不談——畢竟，義大利的美食身份與非本土的番茄緊密相連，泰國亦是如此，與非本土的辣椒密不可分——現實是，澳大利亞人並未大量食用本土原生食物。

例外的是來自海洋、河流和湖泊的魚類、甲殼類和貝類，其中大多數無疑是這個國家所獨有的。儘管如今人們做出了勇敢而善意的努力，致力於推廣和鼓勵食用本土資源，但叢林食物的採集或生產數量並不足以成為澳大利亞人日常飲食的標準組成部分，且這些食物普遍難以取得。 原生食物對當今澳大利亞身份認同的意義，甚至不及羊肉和百香果——這兩者最初都是舶來品，如今已在此地落地生根。

英文原文

In its periodic quest for culinary identity, Australia automatically looks to its indigenous ingredients, the foods that are native to this country. There can be little doubt that using an indigenous product must qualify a dish as Australian notes Stephanie Alexander. Similarly, and without qualification, states that ‘a uniquely Australian food culture can only be based upon foods indigenous to this country’ , although, as Craw remarks, proposing Australian native foods as national symbols relies more upon their association with 'nature' and geographic origin than on common usage. Notwithstanding the lack of justification for the premise that national dishes are, of necessity, founded on ingredients native to the country—after all, Italy's gastronomic identity is tied to the non- indigenous tomato, Thailand to then on-indigenous chili—the reality is that Australians do not eat indigenous foods in significant quantities . The exceptions are fish, crustaceans and shellfish from oceans, rivers and lakes, most of which are unarguably unique to this country. Despite valiant and well-intentioned efforts today at promoting and encouraging the consumption of native resources, bush foods are not harvested or produced in sufficient quantities for them to be a standard component of Australian diets, nor are they generally accessible . Indigenous foods are less relevant to Australian identity today than lamb and passionfruit, both initially imported and now naturalized .

#129 Software engineer (軟件工程師) #060129 原文
中文翻譯

考慮當前情況：與美國的同行一樣，印度的工程師和技術人員
具備提供電腦程式設計和創新新技術的能力。
印度程式設計師和高科技工程師的薪資只有美國同行的四分之一；因此，印度能夠以比美國更低的美元成本完成這兩項工作，
印度在這兩方面都具有絕對優勢。 換言之，它生產一單位程式設計所需的美元成本低於美國，
生產一單位技術創新所需的美元成本同樣低於美國。
這是否意味著美國不僅會失去程式設計工作，連創新技術工作也會一併流失？
這是否意味著，若美國與印度展開國際貿易，我們的生活水準將會下降？

大衛·李嘉圖對這兩個問題的回答都是否定的——正如我們今日的看法。儘管印度在兩項活動中均可能具有絕對優勢，但這一事實與決定印度或美國將生產什麼並不相關。印度在程式設計方面具有比較優勢，部分原因在於
這類活動所需的實體資本較少。反面來看，美國在技術創新方面具有比較優勢，部分原因在於在美國相對容易取得資本，
以推動此類長期專案。其結果是，印度程式設計師將愈來愈多地承擔過去由美國程式設計師所從事的工作。
相對地，美國企業將轉向愈來愈多的創新活動。

英文原文

Consider the current situation: like their counterparts in the United States, engineers and technicians in India have the capacity to provide both computer programming and innovative new technologies . Indian programmers and high-tech engineers earn one-quarter of what their counterparts earn in the United States; Consequently, India is able to do both jobs at a lower dollar cost than the United States: India has absolute advantage in both . In other words, it can produce a unit of programming for fewer dollars than the Unites States, and it can also produce a unit of technology innovation for fewer dollars . Does that mean that the United States will lose not only programming jobs but innovative technology job, too? Does that mean that our standard of living will fall if the United States and India engage in the international trade? David Ricardo would have answered no to both questions - as we do today. While India may have an absolute advantage in both activities, that fact is irrelevant in determining what India or the United States will produce. India has a comparative advantage in doing programming in part because of such activity requires little physical capital. The flip side is that the United States has a comparative advantage in technology innovation partly because it is relatively easy to obtain capital in this country to undertake such long-run projects. The result is that Indian programmers will do more and more of what U·S· programmers have been doing in the past . In contrast, American firms will shift to more and more innovation .

#130 Invisibility Cloak (隱形鬥篷) #060130 原文
中文翻譯

根據研究人員的說法，隱形鬥篷錯覺源於一種信念：我們在社交觀察上遠比周遭的人敏銳。這意味著，儘管我們盡可能地觀察並揣測他人，我們卻往往認為周遭的人沒有那麼警覺。
這種錯覺之所以產生，是因為我們完全清楚自己對他人的印象與推測，卻對那些人在想什麼毫無所知——除非他們主動告訴我們，而這種事除了在特殊情況下，幾乎不會發生。
要更好地理解這一現象，有必要參考阿莫斯·特沃斯基與丹尼爾·卡尼曼在認知偏誤領域的開創性研究。當人們在社交場合對他人做出判斷時，往往依賴特定的偏誤，例如可得性捷思法——也就是說，我們會對腦中容易浮現的想法賦予更大的意義。這就是為何我們認為關於他人的想法比關於無生命物體的想法更為重要。因此，當我們環顧四周時，往往會將注意力集中在所見的人以及他們正在做的事情上——這也是為什麼觀察路人會讓人如此著迷。
讓我們覺得自己相對不被他人注意的原因之一，在於人們觀察他人時往往盡量保持低調。正因為其他人沒有把他們的觀察分享給我們，我們很容易就以為他們沒有我們那麼善於觀察。當然，人們或許會與身旁的人分享他們觀察路人的所見所聞，但大多數情況下，只有足夠值得一提的事才會被拿出來討論。對我們大多數人來說，所看到的一切往往極為私密，不會與他人分享。

英文原文

According to researchers, the invisibility cloak illusion stems from the belief that we are much more socially observant than the people around us . This means that, while we watch and wonder about other people as much as possible, we often think that people around us are less aware . This illusion occurs because, while we are fully aware of our own impressions and speculations about other people, we have no idea about what those other people are thinking unless they choose to share with us , something that rarely happens except in exceptional circumstances. To better understand what is happening, it is important to consider the groundbreaking research by Amos Tversky and Daniel Kahneman on cognitive biases. When people make judgments about other people in social situations, they often depend on specific biases such as the availability heuristic, i·e·, that we attach more significance to thoughts that come to mind easily. This is why we consider thoughts about other people as being more important than thoughts about inanimate objects. And so, as we look around us, we tend to focus our thoughts on the people we see and what they happen to be doing. Which is why people-watching can be so addictive. What adds to the sense that we are relatively invisible to others is that people tend to be as discreet as possible about their people-watching . Just because other people aren't sharing their observations with us, it's easy to pretend that they are not as observant as we are . Of course, people may share their people-watching observations with anyone they happen to be with but, for the most part, that only applies to something remarkable enough to comment on. For most of us, what we are seeing tends to be extremely private and not to be shared with others.

#131 Pay your child (付錢給小孩的好處) #060131 原文
中文翻譯

許多曾就零用錢主題撰文的人表示，付錢讓孩子做家事並不是個好主意。這些工作是家庭生活的正常一部分。

然而，付錢讓孩子做額外的家務可能是有益的，甚至能讓他們了解生意是如何運作的。零用錢給了孩子一個機會，去體驗金錢能為他們帶來什麼。他們可以以禮物或捐助善款的形式分享它。

他們可以用它購買自己想要的東西，或者儲存起來，甚至加以投資。儲蓄幫助孩子理解，要達成昂貴的目標需要犧牲：你必須節省開支，並為未來做計劃。要求孩子將部分零用錢存起來，也能為他們日後的儲蓄與投資習慣打開大門。

許多銀行提供服務，幫助兒童和青少年學習個人理財。儲蓄帳戶是了解複利威力的絕佳途徑。複利的運作方式是利滾利。

舉例來說，以二％的利率投資一美元，兩年後第一年將賺得兩分錢。第二年，這筆錢將以一美元零兩分為本金計算二％的利息，以此類推。這看起來似乎不多，但隨著時間累積，總額會相當可觀。

英文原文

Many people who have written on the subject of allowances say it is not a good idea to pay your child for work around the home . These jobs are a normal part of family life. Paying children to do extra work around the house, however, can be useful. It can even provide an understanding of how a business works . Allowances give children a chance to experience the things they can do with money . They can share it in the form of gifts or giving to a good cause. They can spend it by buying things they want. Or they can save and maybe even invest it. Saving helps children understand that costly goals require sacrifice: you have to cut costs and plan for the future. Requiring children to save part of their allowance can also open the door to future saving and investing. Many banks offer services to help children and teenagers learn about personal finance. A savings account is an excellent way to learn about the power of compound interest. Compounding works by paying interest on interest. So, for example, one dollar invested at two percent interest for two years will earn two cents in the first year. The second year, the money will earn two percent of one dollar and two cents, and so on. That may not seem like a lot. But over time it adds up.

#132 Continental Drift (大陸漂移) #060132 原文
中文翻譯

根據大陸漂移學說，在大部分的地質歷史時期，世界是由單一一塊大陸所組成的。這塊大陸最終分裂並向四方漂移，形成了我們今日所見的七大洲。大陸漂移的第一個完整理論是由德國氣象學家阿爾弗雷德·韋格納於1912年提出的。該假說主張，大陸由較輕的岩石構成，漂浮在較重的地殼物質之上——類似於冰山漂浮在水面上的方式。韋格納認為，各大陸的相對位置並非固定不變，而是緩慢移動的——速率約為每世紀一碼。根據普遍被接受的板塊構造理論，科學家認為地球表面被分割成若干不斷移動的板塊，平均厚度約為50英里。這些板塊在更炎熱、更深層、流動性更強的地帶之上相對移動，平均速率可達每年數英寸。世界上大多數活火山位於移動板塊的邊界上或其附近，被稱為板塊邊界火山。

太平洋盆地的周邊地區包含多個板塊的邊界，散布著許多活火山，形成了所謂的「火環」。火環提供了板塊邊界火山的絕佳範例，包括聖海倫斯火山。

然而，部分活火山並不與板塊邊界相關聯，其中許多所謂的板塊內火山在某些海洋板塊的內部形成大致呈線狀的火山鏈。夏威夷群島或許是板塊內火山鏈最典型的範例，它是由向西北方移動的太平洋板塊經過一個推測中的「熱點」所形成的，這個熱點啟動了岩漿生成與火山形成的過程。

英文原文

According to the theory of continental drift, the world was made up of a single continent through most of geologic time. That continent eventually separated and drifted apart, forming into the seven continents we have today. The first comprehensive theory of continental drift was suggested by the German meteorologist Alfred Wegener in 1912. The hypothesis asserts that the continents consist of lighter rocks that rest on heavier crustal material—similar to the manner in which icebergs float on water. Wegener contended that the relative positions of the continents are not rigidly fixed but are slowly moving—at a rate of about one yard per century. According to the generally accepted plate-tectonics theory , scientists believe that Earth's surface is broken into a number of shifting slabs or plates , which average about 50 miles in thickness. These plates move relative to one another above a hotter, deeper, more mobile zone at average rates as great as a few inches per year. Most of the world's active volcanoes are located along or near the boundaries between shifting plates and are called plate-boundary volcanoes. The peripheral areas of the Pacific Ocean Basin , containing the boundaries of several plates, are dotted with many active volcanoes that form the so-called Ring of Fire. The Ring provides excellent examples of plate-boundary volcanoes, including Mount St· Helens. However, some active volcanoes are not associated with plate boundaries , and many of these so-called intra-plate volcanoes form roughly linear chains in the interior of some oceanic plates. The Hawaiian Islands provide perhaps the best example of an intra-plate volcanic chain, developed by the northwest- moving Pacific plate passing over an inferred "hot spot" that initiates the magma-generation and volcano-formation process.

2accepted plate-tectonics theory , scientists believe that Earth's surface is broken into a number of shifting slabs or plates , which average about 50 miles in thickness. These plates move relative to one
3The peripheral areas of the Pacific Ocean Basin , containing the boundaries of several plates, are dotted with many active volcanoes that form the so-called Ring of Fire. The Ring provides excellent examples
4However, some active volcanoes are not associated with plate boundaries , and many of these so-called
#133 Straw as building material(稻草房) #060133 原文
中文翻譯

許多技術曾經承諾具備這些特質，但真正具有商業可行性的卻寥寥無幾。目前所欠缺的，是能夠證明這些技術耐久、真正對環境有益，且適合投保的性能數據。在過去13年間，我們的建築與土木工程學院一直主導稻草作為低環境衝擊建材的研究。這項研究工作涵蓋了獨特稻草包板材的開發，以及科學監測與測試，如今已取得關鍵的業界認證。BM TRADA 的 Q-Mark 認證保障了稻草建築的能源效率、防火安全、耐久性與抗候性，這意味著開發商與購屋者現在可以為稻草住宅和建築申請保險與房貸。

新建住宅中創新的稻草牆體，提供了現行英國建築法規要求兩倍以上的隔熱效能。根據對利茲一處住宅稻草包開發案的監測，預計可節省高達90%的燃料費用。這些牆體採用 ModCell 技術建造；預製板材由木結構框架填充稻草包或大麻纖維，再以透氣石灰基系統或通風木材、磚面覆層進行抹面。這項技術結合了目前所有現行建築系統中最低的碳足跡，以及最佳的運營二氧化碳排放表現。事實上，作為一種農業副產品，稻草在生長過程中能吸收二氧化碳，因此稻草建築可以達到碳負值。

英文原文

Many technologies have promised these qualities, but few have been commercially viable. What's been lacking is the performance data needed to demonstrate that these technologies are durable, genuinely environmentally beneficial, and suitable to be insured. Over the past 13 years, our Department of Architecture & Civil Engineering has led on research into straw as a low-impact building material . This work, which has included developing a unique straw bale panel as well as scientific monitoring and testing, has now culminated in crucial industry certifications . The BM TRADA’s Q-Mark certification guarantees a straw building’s energy efficiency, fire safety, durability and weather-resilience and means that developers and homebuyers can now get insurance and mortgages for straw homes and buildings. The innovative straw walls in the new houses provide two times more insulation than required by current UK building regulations . Based on monitoring a residential straw-bale development in Leeds, fuel bill reductions up to 90% can be expected . The walls have been built using ModCell technology; prefabricated panels consisting of a wooden structural frame infilled with straw bales or hemp and rendered with either a breathable lime-based system or ventilated timber or brick cladding. This technology combines the lowest carbon footprint and the best operational CO² performance of any system of construction currently available . In fact, as an agricultural co-product, straw buildings can be carbon negative as straw absorbs CO² when it grows.

#134 Electric Cars(電車） #060134 原文
中文翻譯

雖然我們往往認為電動車是完全現代的產物，但事實上它們是最早出現的機動車輛之一。

在二十世紀初，電動車實際上比內燃機汽車更受歡迎，因為乘坐起來更為舒適。然而，隨著以汽油為燃料的汽車日益普及，電動車逐漸式微。

情況演變至電動車僅被用於某些特定用途，例如作為堆高機、救護車以及城市配送車輛。雖然電力在道路車輛上的使用有所衰退，但它作為火車動力來源的重要性卻穩步提升。例如，瑞士便迅速發展出電氣化鐵路系統，這無疑是受到該國本身缺乏煤炭與石油資源這一事實的推動。如今，以電力驅動道路車輛的想法重新引起了廣泛關注。這是為什麼呢？無庸置疑，經濟因素具有相當重要的地位。石油成本急劇上漲，形成了強烈的財務誘因，促使人們尋求替代方案。然而，環境方面的動機同樣不可忽視。汽車廢氣排放在很大程度上被認為是造成臭氧層破壞，以及隨之而來的極地氣溫上升等問題的主要原因之一。不願讓情況繼續惡化的意願，也正在推動著有效電動交通工具的設計研究。

英文原文

Although we tend to think of electric cars as being something completely modern, they were in fact some of the earliest types of motorized vehicle . At the beginning of the twentieth century electric cars were actually more popular than cars with an internal combustion engine as they were more comfortable to ride in. However, as cars fueled by petrol increased in importance, electric cars declined . The situation became such that electric vehicles were only used for certain specific purposes, as fork- lift trucks, ambulances and urban delivery vehicles, for example. Although electricity declined in use in road vehicles, it steadily grew in importance as a means of powering trains . Switzerland, for example, was quick to develop an electrifed train system, encouraged in this no doubt by the fact that it had no coal or oil resources of its own. Nowadays there is renewed interest in electricity as a means of powering road vehicles. Why is this the case? Well, undoubtedly economic reasons are of considerable importance . The cost of oil has risen so sharply that there is a strong fnancial imperative to look for an alternative. However, there are also environmental motivations . Emissions from cars are blamed in large part for -among other things - the destruction of the ozone layer and the resultant rise in temperatures in the polar regions. A desire not to let things get any worse is also encouraging research into designing effective electric transport.

#135 Postive Mindset(積極心態） #060135 原文
中文翻譯

研究顯示，當人們以積極的心態工作時，幾乎各個層面的表現——
生產力、創造力、投入程度——都會有所提升。然而，幸福感或許是最常被誤解的
績效驅動因素。首先，大多數人認為成功先於幸福。「等我升職了，我就會快樂，」他們這樣想。或者，「等我達到業績目標，我就會感覺很好。」但由於成功是個移動的目標——每當你達到目標，你又會把它再次提高——因成功而來的幸福感是短暫的。事實上，情況恰恰相反：培養積極心態的人在面對挑戰時表現得更好。我將這稱為「幸福優勢」——當大腦處於積極狀態時，每一項商業成果都會顯示出改善。

我在擔任研究員和講師的過程中，於48個國家觀察到了這種效應，研究主題正是員工幸福感與成功之間的關聯。而且我並不孤單：在一項涵蓋225項學術研究的元分析中，研究人員桑雅·柳波莫斯基、蘿拉·金和艾德·迪納發現了生活滿意度與成功商業成果之間存在方向性因果關係的有力證據。

另一個常見的誤解是，我們的基因、我們的環境，或兩者的結合，決定了我們有多快樂。誠然，這兩個因素都有影響。但一個人對幸福感的整體感受，其可塑性之高令人驚訝。你所培養的習慣、你與同事互動的方式、你看待壓力的態度——這一切都可以被管理，從而提升你的幸福感和成功的機會。

英文原文

Research shows that when people work with a positive mind-set, performance on nearly every level - productivity, creativity, engagement - improves . Yet happiness is perhaps the most misunderstood driver of performance. For one, most people believe that success precedes happiness . “Once I get a promotion, I'll be happy," they think. Or, “Once I hit my sales target, I'll feel great”. But because success is a moving target - as soon as you hit your target, you raise it again, the happiness that results from success is fleeting. In fact, it works the other way around : people who cultivate a positive mind- set perform better in the face of challenge. I call this the "happiness advantage”- every business outcome shows improvement when the brain is positive. I've observed this effect in my role as a researcher and lecturer in 48 countries on the connection between emplovee happiness and success. And I'm not alone: in a meta-analysis of 225 academic studies, researchers Sonja Lyubomirsky, Laura King, and Ed Diener found strong evidence of directional causality between life satisfaction and successful business outcomes. Another common misconception is that our genetics, our environment, or a combination of the two determines how happy we are . To be sure, both factors have an impact. But one's general sense of well- being is surprisingly malleable . The habits you cultivate, the way you interact with coworkers, how you think about stress - all these can be managed to increase your happiness and your chances of success.

#136 New Women(新女性) #060136 原文
中文翻譯

「新女性」的概念在社會與文化變革時期興起於英國與北美。這一理念由一位名叫莎拉的作家大力推廣，她撰寫了一部在評論界引發廣泛爭論的著作。她的作品探討了中產階級女性角色與期望的轉變，聚焦於經濟獨立、就業機會以及婚姻的本質。莎拉的論述強調保護並提升女性社會地位的必要性，揭示了她們在男性主導的社會結構中所面臨的種種挑戰。儘管她的觀點引發了褒貶不一的回應，有人支持推動性別平等，也有人批評或抗拒這樣的改變，但她這部著作所產生的影響是不可否認的。它促進了有關女性權利、自主性與社會角色的更廣泛討論。莎拉的倡導是一場更大運動的組成部分，這場運動致力於重新定義女性的位置，不僅在家庭領域，也延伸至公共與職業生活。

儘管遭遇阻力，且她的願景在當時未能完全實現，「新女性」的概念仍留下了深遠的印記，並已被後世銘記為女性運動史上的重要里程碑。它代表著社會對性別不平等日益增長的覺醒，並為日後的改革與女性主義思潮奠定了基礎。

英文原文

The concept of the "New Woman" emerged in Britain and North America during a time of social and cultural transformation . This idea was notably advanced by a writer named Sarah, who authored a book that sparked signifcant debate among commentators. Her work explored the shifting roles and expectations of middle-class women , focusing on financial independence, employment opportunities, and the nature of marriage. Sarah's arguments emphasized the need to protect and uplift women's status in society, highlighting the challenges they faced in a male-dominated structure. Although her ideas received mixed responses, with some embracing the push for gender equality while others criticized or resisted the change, the impact of her book was undeniable . It contributed to broader discussions about women's rights, autonomy, and social roles. Sarah's advocacy was part of a larger movement that sought to redefine the place of women not only in the domestic sphere but also in public and professional life. Despite the resistance and the fact that her vision wasn't fully realized at the time, the notion of the "New Woman" left a lasting impression and has since been commemorated as an important milestone in the history of women's movements . It represented a growing awareness of gender inequality and laid the groundwork for future reforms and feminist thought .

#137 Independent Workforce(獨立勞動力) #060137 原文
中文翻譯

朝九晚五地為單一雇主工作，與當今相當大比例的勞動力的謀生方式已大相徑庭。數百萬人整合多元收入來源，以獨立方式工作，而非受僱於結構化的固定薪資職位。這一現象並非新生事物，然而在官方統計數據中卻從未被妥善衡量——由此產生的資料缺口，使外界無法清晰掌握勞動市場中大量的活動實況。

為了更深入了解獨立勞動力，以及是什麼驅動了參與其中的人們，麥肯錫全球研究院對歐洲和美國約 8,000 名受訪者進行了調查。我們詢問了他們過去 12 個月的收入情況，涵蓋主要工作及其他任何創收活動，並了解他們的職業滿意度與未來工作的期望。

由此產生的報告《獨立工作：選擇、必要性與零工經濟》發現，歐洲和美國多達 1.62 億人，即勞動年齡人口的 20% 至 30%，從事某種形式的獨立工作。儘管人口結構多元，獨立工作者大致可分為四類：自由工作者，主動選擇獨立工作並以此為主要收入來源；兼差族，出於個人選擇以獨立工作賺取額外收入；不情願者，以獨立工作維持主要生計，但更希望擁有傳統工作；以及財務困難者，出於生活所迫從事額外的獨立工作。

英文原文

Working nine to five for a single employer bears little resemblance to the way a substantial share of the workforce makes a living today. Millions of people assemble various income streams and work independently, rather than in structured payroll jobs. This is hardly a new phenomenon , yet it has never been well measured in official statistics—and the resulting data gaps prevent a clear view of a large share of labor-market activity. To better understand the independent workforce and what motivates the people who participate in it, the McKinsey Global Institute surveyed some 8,000 respondents across Europe and the US. We asked about their income in the past 12 months, encompassing primary work, as well as any other income- generating activities, and about their professional satisfaction and aspirations for work in the future. The resulting report, Independent work: Choice, necessity, and the gig economy, finds that up to 162 million people in Europe and the US, or 20 to 30 percent of the working-age population, engage in some form of independent work . While demographically diverse, independent workers largely fit into four segments: free agents , who actively choose independent work and derive their primary income from it; casual earners , who use independent work for supplemental income and do so by choice; reluctants , who make their primary living from independent work but would prefer traditional jobs; and the financially strapped , who do supplemental independent work out of necessity.

紅字句（原文）
#原文

2The resulting report, Independent work: Choice, necessity, and the gig economy, finds that up to 162 million people in Europe and the US, or 20 to 30 percent of the working-age population, engage in some form of independent work . #138 The National Oceanography Centre(國家海洋學中心) #060138 原文
中文翻譯

國家海洋學中心（NOC）正在研究開採深海礦產資源的潛在風險與效益，其中部分礦產對低碳技術至關重要，同時也運用海洋機器人評估這些潛在深海採礦活動對環境的影響。NOC主導了一次乘坐RRS詹姆斯·庫克號進行的遠征，發現一座水下火山的地殼中蘊藏了足量的稀有元素碲，若全部用於生產太陽能光伏板，可提供英國年電力需求的三分之二。此外，NOC還主導了一項國際研究，證明深海結核採礦將對深海生物造成持久損害，影響時間至少長達數十年。這些結核是馬鈴薯大小的岩石，含有高濃度的金屬，包括銅、錳和鎳。它們在海床上經過數百萬年的時間極緩慢地生長。雖然目前尚無商業開採作業，但已有許多計畫正在籌備中。NOC執行董事愛德華·希爾教授表示：「到2050年，地球將有九十億人口，人們的目光日益轉向海洋，尤其是深海，以尋求食物、清潔能源及戰略性礦產。NOC正就開發海洋資源所涉及的諸多面向與觀點開展研究。這項研究旨在以可靠的科學證據為未來的決策提供依據，因為人們正日益轉向海洋，以應對社會面臨的若干重大挑戰。」

英文原文

The National Oceanography Centre(NOC) is engaged in research into the potential risks and benefits of exploiting deep-sea mineral resources, some of which are essential for low-carbon technology, as well as using ocean robots to estimate the environmental impact of these potential deep-sea mining activities. The NOC has led an expedition on the RRS James Cook that found enough of the scarce element Tellurium present in the crust of a submerged volcano that, if it were all to be used in the production of solar PV panels, could provide 2/3rds of the UK's annual electricity supply . In addition, the NOC also led an international study demonstrating deep-sea nodule mining will cause long-lasting damage to deep-sea life, lasting at least for decades .These nodules are potato-sized rocks containing high levels of metals, including copper, manganese and nickel. They grow very slowly on the sea-bed, over millions of years. Although no commercial operations exist to extract these resources, many are planned. Professor Edward Hill, Executive Director at the NOC commented,"By 2050 there will be nine billion people on earth and attention is increasingly turning to the ocean, particularly the deep ocean, for food, clean supplies of energy and strategic minerals. The NOC is undertaking research related to many aspects and perspectives involved in exploiting ocean resources . This research is aimed at informing with sound scientific evidence the decisions that will need to be taken in the future, as people increasingly turn to the oceans to address some of society's greatest challenges ."

#139 Immune System(免疫系統) #060139 原文
中文翻譯

什麼是免疫系統？

免疫系統是由不同器官、細胞和蛋白質所組成的複雜網絡，它們共同協作運作。
免疫系統主要分為兩部分：先天性免疫系統——與生俱來；以及後天性免疫系統——在身體接觸微生物或微生物所釋放的化學物質後逐漸發展而成。這兩套免疫系統相輔相成，共同運作。

先天性免疫系統

這是孩子身體的快速反應系統，當發現入侵者時，它是最先做出反應的。先天性免疫系統由皮膚、眼角膜，以及覆蓋呼吸道、消化道和泌尿生殖道的黏膜所構成。這些組織共同形成物理屏障，保護孩子的身體免受有害病菌、寄生蟲（如蠕蟲）或異常細胞（如癌細胞）的侵害。先天性免疫系統是遺傳而來的，從孩子出生的那一刻起便開始運作。當系統偵測到入侵者時，便會立即採取行動——免疫細胞會將入侵者包圍並覆蓋，再由稱為吞噬細胞的免疫細胞將其消滅於內部。

後天性免疫系統

後天性免疫系統在先天性免疫系統的協助下，會製造特殊蛋白質（稱為抗體）來保護身體對抗特定入侵者。這些抗體由稱為B淋巴球的細胞在身體接觸入侵者後產生。抗體會持續留存在孩子體內。抗體的形成可能需要數天時間，但在首次接觸後，免疫系統便會記住該入侵者，並在下次入侵時加以防禦。後天性免疫系統會隨著孩子的成長而不斷變化。接種疫苗能訓練孩子的免疫系統產生抗體，使其免受有害疾病的侵害。

英文原文

What is the Immune System? The immune system is a complex network of different organs, cells, and proteins that work together . There are 2 main parts of the immune system: the innate immune system - you are born with this, and the adaptive immune system - you develop this when your body is exposed to microbes or chemicals released by microbes. These two immune systems work together. The Innate Immune System This is your child's rapid response system. It is the first to respond when it finds an invader. It is made up of the skin, the eye's cornea, and the mucous membrane that lines the respiratory, gastrointestinal, and genitourinary tracts. These all create physical barriers to help protect your child's body. They protect against harmful germs, parasites (such as worms), or cells (such as cancer). The innate immune system is inherited. It is active from the moment your child is born. When this system recognizes an invader, it goes into action right away. The cells of this immune system surround and cover the invader. The invader is killed inside the immune system cells (called phagocytes). The Acquired Immune System The acquired immune system, with help from the innate system, makes special proteins (called antibodies) to protect your body from a specific invader . These antibodies are developed by cells called B lymphocytes after the body has been exposed to the invader. The antibodies stay in your child's body. It can take several days for antibodies to form. But after the first exposure, the immune system will recognize the invader and defend against it . The acquired immune system changes during your child's life. Immunizations train your child's immune system to make antibodies to protect them from harmful diseases.

2The Innate Immune System

#140 Bank Overdraft(銀行透支) #060140 原文
中文翻譯

銀行以活期帳戶透支的形式向企業提供短期融資。透支的優點在於其靈活性。當企業的資金需求因季節性因素而增加時，企業可以持續開立支票，並看著透支額度不斷攀升。當商品和服務售出、現金開始流入時，企業應能看著透支額度再度下降。以這種模式運作的企業中，最典型的例子便是農業。農夫利用透支來支付耕作農業的種子採購費用，或支應畜牧農業冬季的飼料費用，以及作物或牲畜生長成熟期間的開支。透支在作物或牲畜售出時得以償還。透支的主要缺點在於它須按要求即時償還。遭逢惡劣天氣導致作物歉收的農夫，深知無力償還透支的困境。依賴透支融資會加重企業管理者的憂慮。另一個缺點是透支所需支付的利息是浮動的。當利率上升時，透支的成本也隨之增加。此外，對於小型企業而言，普遍存在一種抱怨，認為被收取的利率相較於大型企業所能獲得的利率偏高。銀行方面的回應是，所收取的利率反映了相對風險，而根據其經驗，小型企業的風險確實較高。

英文原文

Banks provide short-term finance to companies in the form of an overdraft on a current account . The advantage of an overdraft is its flexibility . When the cash needs of the company increase with seasonal factors, the company can continue to write cheques and watch the overdraft increase. When the goods and services are sold and cash begins to flow in, the company should be able to watch the overdraft decrease again. The most obvious example of a business which operates in this pattern is farming. The farmer uses the overdraft to finance the acquisition of seed for arable farming, or feed through the winter for stock farming and to cover the period when the crops or animals are growing and maturing. The overdraft is reducedwhen the crops or the animals are sold. The main disadvantage of an overdraft is that it is repayable on demand . The farmer whose crop fails because of bad weather knows the problem of being unable to repay the overdraft. Having overdraft financing increases the worries of those who manage the company. The other disadvantage is that the interest payable on overdrafts is variable . When interest rates increase, the cost of the overdraft increases. Furthermore, for small companies there are often complaints that the rate of interest charged is high compared with that available to larger companies . The banks answer that the rates charged reflect relative risk and it is their experience that small companies are more risky.

3those who manage the company. The other disadvantage is that the interest payable on overdrafts is variable . When interest rates increase, the cost of the overdraft increases. #141 Wright Brothers (B) (萊特兄弟-B版) #060141 原文
中文翻譯

1905年的飛行季結束後，萊特兄弟聯繫了美國戰爭部，以及英國、法國、德國和俄國的政府與個人，提出出售飛行機器。
他們一再遭到拒絕——政府官僚認為他們是瘋子；
其他人則認為，如果兩個自行車修理工能造出成功的飛機，他們自己也辦得到。
但萊特兄弟堅持不懈，1907年底，美國陸軍通信兵部隊提出了購買一架飛機的需求。
幾個月後的1908年初，一個法國商人財團也同意購買另一架。美國陸軍和法國方面都要求飛機能夠搭載一名乘客。萊特兄弟迅速對1905年的飛行者號進行改裝，增設了雙人座位並換上更強力的引擎。他們秘密地在北卡羅來納州的小鷹鎮進行測試——這是幾年來他們首次重返那裡。隨後，兄弟倆暫時分開行動——威爾伯前往法國，奧維爾則前往維吉尼亞州。

1908至1909年間，威爾伯在歐洲展示萊特飛機，奧維爾則在維吉尼亞州的麥爾堡進行飛行。飛行一切順利，直到奧維爾的螺旋槳脫落導致墜機，他本人腿部骨折，乘客托馬斯·塞爾弗里奇中尉不幸罹難。奧維爾養傷期間，威爾伯在法國持續飛行，屢破紀錄。奧維爾與妹妹凱特最終赴法與威爾伯會合，三人一同回到代頓，受到盛大的歸國歡迎儀式。此後，奧維爾與威爾伯帶著新型軍用飛行者號重返麥爾堡，完成了美國陸軍的驗收測試。數月後，威爾伯
在紐約港超過百萬名觀眾面前飛行——這是他在祖國的首次公開飛行。所有這些飛行壯舉震驚並深深吸引了全世界。萊特兄弟成為二十世紀第一批偉大的名人。

英文原文

After the 1905 flying season, the Wrights contacted the United States War Department , as well as governments and individuals in England, France, Germany, and Russia, offering to sell a flying machine. They were turned down time and time again -- government bureaucrats thought they were crackpots; others thought that if two bicycle mechanics could build a successful airplane, they could do it themselves. But the Wright persisted, and in late 1907, the US Army Signal Corps asked for an aircraft . Just a few months later, in early 1908, a French syndicate of businessmen agreed to purchase another. Both the US Army and the French asked for an airplane capable of carrying a passenger. The Wright brothers hastily adapted their 1905 Flyer with two seats and a more powerful engine. They tested these modifications in secret, back at Kitty Hawk, North Carolina for the first time in several years. Then the brothers parted temporarily -- Wilbur to France and Orville to Virginia. In 1908 and 1909, Wilbur demonstrated Wright aircraft in Europe, and Orville flew in Fort Meyer, Virginia. The flights went well until Orville lost a propeller and crashed, breaking his leg and killing his passenger Lt Thomas Selfridge. While Orville recuperated, Wilbur kept flying in France, breaking record after record. Orville and his sister Kate eventually joined Wilbur in France, and the three returned home to Dayton to an elaborate homecoming celebration. Together, Orville and Wilbur returned to Fort Meyer with a new Military Flyer and completed the US Army trials. A few months later, Wilbur flew before over a million spectators in New York Harbor — his first public flight in his native land. All of these flights stunned and captivated the world. The Wright Brothers became the first great celebrities of the twentieth century .

#原文

2themselves. But the Wright persisted, and in late 1907, the US Army Signal Corps asked for an aircraft .
3before over a million spectators in New York Harbor — his first public flight in his native land. All of these flights stunned and captivated the world. The Wright Brothers became the first great celebrities of the twentieth century .
#142 Education Technology (教育技術) #060142 原文
中文翻譯

1953年，BF·斯金納走進了女兒的數學課堂。這位哈佛心理學家發現，每個學生都以相同的方式、相同的速度學習相同的內容。幾天後，他製造出了第一台「教學機器」，讓孩子們能夠按照自己的節奏作答。 到1960年代中期，類似的裝置已由挨家挨戶的推銷員兜售。然而不出幾年，人們對它的熱情便逐漸消退。

自此，教育科技（edtech）不斷重複著熱潮與泡沫破滅的循環，儘管電腦已徹底改變了生活中幾乎所有其他領域。 原因之一是教師及其工會的保守態度，但另一個原因在於，教育科技激發思維潛能的可能性始終未能得到證實。

然而今天，斯金納的繼承者們正迫使懷疑論者重新審視這一問題（詳見文章）。在馬克·祖克柏、比爾·蓋茨等科技億萬富翁的支持下，世界各地的學校正借助新型軟體來「個人化」學習。 這或許能幫助數億身陷沉悶課堂的孩子——但前提是，教育科技的擁護者必須抵制住重拾那些有害學習理念的誘惑。 要想成功，教育科技必須服務於教學，而非本末倒置。

現行的學校教育模式起源於18世紀的普魯士。 迄今為止，其他替代方案尚未能以同等效率教育如此多的孩子。課堂、按年齡分級的年級制度、標準化課程與固定課表，對於全球近15億在校學童中的絕大多數而言，依然是教育的常態。

英文原文

In 1953 BF Skinner visited his daughter's maths class. The Harvard psychologist found every pupil learning the same topic in the same way at the same speed . A few days later he built his first "teaching machine" , which let children tackle questions at their own pace. By the mid-1960s similar gizmos were being flogged by door-to-door salesmen. Within a few years, though, enthusiasm for them had fizzled out. Since then education technology (edtech) has repeated the cycle of hype and flop , even as computers have reshaped almost every other part of life. One reason is the conservatism of teachers and their unions. But another is that the brain-stretching potential of edtech has remained unproven . Today, however, Skinner’s heirs are forcing the sceptics to think again (see article). Backed by billionaire techies such as Mark Zuckerberg and Bill Gates, schools around the world are using new software to "personalize" learning . This could help hundreds of millions of children stuck in dismal classes—but only if edtech boosters can resist the temptation to revive harmful ideas about how children learn. To succeed, edtech must be at the service of teaching, not the other way around. The conventional model of schooling emerged in Prussia in the 18th century. Alternatives have so far failed to teach as many children as efficiently. Classrooms, hierarchical year-groups, standardized curriculums and fixed timetables are still the norm for most of the world’s nearly one point five billion schoolchildren .

#143 Wright Brothers (C)(萊特兄弟-C版) #060143 原文
中文翻譯

1892年，兄弟倆開設了一家自行車銷售與維修店，並於1896年開始小規模生產自行車。他們研發了自家的自潤式自行車輪轂，並在店內安置了多台輕型機床。印刷店與自行車業務所獲得的利潤，最終成為萊特兄弟在1899年至1905年間進行航空實驗的資金來源。此外，設計並製造以木材、金屬線與金屬管構成的輕量精密機械，這段經驗正是建造飛行機器的絕佳準備。

在晚年，萊特兄弟追憶起他們對飛行的著迷，源於父親在家人居住愛荷華州期間，從旅途中帶回的一架小型直升機玩具。十年後，他們讀到了德國滑翔機先驅奧托·利林塔爾的研究記述。然而，真正開啟他們對飛行產生認真興趣的，是1896年8月利林塔爾在滑翔機墜毀事故中罹難的新聞報導。到了1899年，兄弟倆已讀遍當地圖書館的相關館藏，並致函史密森尼學會，請求推薦更多航空學讀物。次年，他們去函自我介紹，結識了奧克塔夫·沙努特——一位傑出的土木工程師及航空權威，在1900至1905年的關鍵歲月裡，他始終是兄弟倆的知心摯友。

英文原文

In 1892 the brothers opened a bicycle sales and repair shop , and they began to build bicycles on a small scale in 1896. They developed their own self-oiling bicycle wheel hub and installed a number of light machine tools in the shop. Profits from the print shop and the bicycle operation eventually were to fund the Wright brothers’ aeronautical experiments from 1899 to 1905. In addition, the experience of designing and building lightweight, precision machines of wood, wire, and metal tubing was ideal preparation for the construction of flying machines . In later years the Wrights dated their fascination with flight to a small helicopter toy that their father had brought home from his travels when the family was living in Iowa. A decade later, they had read accounts of the work of the German glider pioneer Otto Lilienthal. But it was news reports of Lilienthal’s death in a glider crash in August 1896 that marked the beginning of their serious interest in flight. By 1899 the brothers had exhausted the resources of the local library and had written to the Smithsonian Institution for suggestions as to further reading in aeronautics. The following year they wrote to introduce themselves to Octave Chanute, a leading civil engineer and an authority on aviation who would remain a confidant of the brothers during the critical years from 1900 to 1905.

#144 Pre-service teacher (實習教師) #060144 大意
中文翻譯

每門個別的內容領域課程都有各自的課程大綱，著重說明與該內容領域相關的特定技術與教學法。這些技術是在教學法與技術課程講師多次會議後確定的。在確認最適合的技術後，教學法與技術課程講師共同制定課程大綱，並設計橫跨兩門課程的專題計畫。

因此，學生在技術課程中學習特定技術，並將其融入教學法課程中的實習教學經驗。

在與一位教學法領域教師合作的研究中，技術課程講師發現，雖然職前教師知道如何操作技術，但他們無法將其有效地融入日常教學計畫，也無法設想學生能夠開發出何種類型的專題計畫。這些發現促使技術課程講師為每個技術課程單元（即各內容領域）開發技術專題與教學法的示範模型。

舉例而言，在自然科學組別中，有一個示範專題旨在說明學生如何運用概念圖建構對雲的理解。這個專題輔以講師示範在自然科學課堂中運用概念圖進行有效教學的實踐。其目標是引導職前教師不僅專注於課程中最終技術專題的開發，更鼓勵他們思考如何在未來的課堂中成功整合技術。

這些示範案例被置於線上，讓職前教師在為技術課程開發自己的專題時，能夠隨時取用。

英文原文

Each individual content-area course has a separate syllabus that highlights the specific technologies and pedagogy relevant to the content area. The technologies were selected after numerous meetings between methods and technology course instructors. After identifying the most appropriate technology, methods and technology course instructors co-develop their syllabi with projects spanning the two courses. Therefore, students learn about a specific technology in the technology course, and they integrate it in their practice teaching experiences within their methods course. In a research collaboration with a methods area faculty member, the technology course instructor found that although pre-service teachers know how to operate technology, they could not integrate it effectively within daily lesson plans and they were not able to envision the type of projects their students could develop . These findings influenced the technology course instructor to develop exemplary models of technology projects and pedagogy for each technology course section (ie content areas) For example, a project was modeled to illustrate how students construct understanding of clouds using concept mapping within the science cohort. This project was supplemented by the instructor modeling effective teaching practices using concept mapping in the science classroom. The goal was to move the pre-service teachers from focusing not only on the development of a final technology project in the course but encouraging them to think about successful integration in their future classrooms. These examples were placed online so the pre-service teachers had access to them at all times in the development of their own projects for the technology course .

2found that although pre-service teachers know how to operate technology, they could not integrate it effectively within daily lesson plans and they were not able to envision the type of projects their students could develop . #147 Development of Africa (非洲的發展 2) #060147 大意
中文翻譯

非洲是一個擁有豐富天然資源的大陸，且這些資源大多尚未開發。若能妥善開發這些資源，必將帶來重大改變。因此，對非洲負面形象的一概而論是不公平的。
非洲並非一個同質化的國家，非洲共有50個國家。
勤勞的非洲人正努力應對糧食、貧困與疾病等問題，但這需要國際社會的支持。
非洲是極具吸引力的商業之地，但需要外界協助。
非洲人有能力識別自身的需求，但需要國際組織與社會各界的共同支持。
非洲許多國家仍處於戰亂之中。
非洲是一片文化多元、多姿多彩的土地，是觀光客、考古學家等人士的天堂。

英文原文

Africa is a continent with vast natural resources, and the resources are mainly unexploited. If the resources are exploited properly, it will. Thus, the generalization of negative image of Africa is unfair. Africa is not a homogeneous country. There are 50 countries in Africa. Hardworking Africans are struggling to address food, poverty and disease issues, but it requires international support. Africa is an attractive place for business but needs assistance. Africans are capable to identify their own needs, but require concerted support from international organizations and communities. Wars are ongoing in many countries in Africa. Africa is a place rich in culture and diversity. It's a heaven for tourists, archeologists, etc.

#148 Electric car 2 (電車2) #060148 原文
中文翻譯

電動車絕非新鮮事物。早在1890年，美國人便已打造出高效能的「電動馬車」——威廉·莫里森在迪莫因製造了一輛，時速可達14英里，續航長達13小時。早在1899年，電動計程車、電車與公共馬車已普遍出現在各大城市，電動車與蒸汽車的銷量更超過燃油馬車。1900年至1915年間，超過60家美國企業投入電動車生產，其中包括安德魯·萊克公司（1896－1901年），該公司提供多種款式與型號。1901年，該公司的電動賽車「萊克魚雷」以時速57英里跑完一英里，創下紀錄。另一家公司沃克·貝克公司（1899－1914年）則打造了一輛時速超過75英里的電動賽車，並率先在賽車上配備乘客安全帶。

儘管電動車乾淨、安靜且操作簡便，但其缺點與現在一樣——續航里程有限、充電時間冗長。1915年後，隨著以內燃機驅動、以廉價汽油為燃料的汽車逐漸走紅，電動車便淡出了流行。近年來，隨著人們對二氧化碳排放所引發的全球暖化問題日益關注，科學家開始重新考慮以電力作為車輛燃料。然而，現今的電動車儘管效率尚可，卻需要頻繁補充電力，且充電過程遠非即時可完成。其造價亦十分高昂，因為正常使用下，價值2,000美元的鉛酸電池在短短幾年內便會耗盡。諷刺的是，電動車對減少二氧化碳排放幾乎毫無貢獻，因為美國大部分電力仍來自燃煤與其他化石燃料。要獲得消費者的青睞，未來的汽車必須在電動車的優勢與消費者對行駛距離及動力的需求之間取得平衡。

英文原文

Electric cars are by no means new . Americans built efficient "electric carriages" as far back as 1890, when William Morrison built one in Des Moines that could go for 13 hours at 14 miles per hour. As early as 1899, electric taxis, trams, and omnibuses were commonly seen in major cities, and electric and steam-powered cars outsold gasoline buggies. Between 1900 and 1915, more than 60 American companies were building electric vehicles, including the Andrew Riker Company (1896-1901), which offered a wide range of styles and models. In 1901, the company’s electric-powered racer, the Riker Torpedo, set a record run of a mile at 57 miles per hour. Another firm, the Walker Baker Company (1899-1914), created an electric-powered racer that could go over 75 miles per hour, and was the first car to have passenger seat belts. Although electric cars were clean, quiet, and simple to operate, the drawback then, as now, was their limited range and long charging time . After 1915, they fell out of vogue as cars powered by internal combustion engines and fueled with cheap gasoline gained favor. As concerns in recent years have grown about global warming caused by carbon-dioxide emissions, scientists have begun to reconsider electricity as a fuel for vehicles. But today’s electric cars, although electric cars are fairly efficient, they require frequent refueling, and the process is far from instantaneous . They are expensive, too , since normal use causes their US$2,000 lead-acid batteries to wear out in just a few years. And, ironically, electric cars do very little to reduce carbon-dioxide emissions , because most electricity in the US is generated by burning coal and other fossil fuels. To gain consumer acceptance, the car of the future will need to balance the benefits of electric cars with consumer demands for distance and dynamo .

2Although electric cars were clean, quiet, and simple to operate, the drawback then, as now, was their limited range and long charging time . After 1915, they fell out of vogue as cars powered by internal
3electricity as a fuel for vehicles. But today’s electric cars, although electric cars are fairly efficient, they require frequent refueling, and the process is far from instantaneous . And, ironically, electric cars do very little to reduce carbon-dioxide emissions , because most electricity in the US is generated by burning coal and other fossil fuels. To gain consumer acceptance, the car of the future will need to balance the benefits of electric cars with consumer demands for distance and dynamo .
#149 Content-area Course(內容學科課程) #060149 原文
中文翻譯

每門內容學科課程都有獨立的課程大綱，著重說明與該學科領域相關的特定技術
與教學法。這些技術的選定，經過了教學法課程講師與技術課程講師之間的多次會議討論。在確認最適合的
技術後，教學法與技術課程的講師共同制定課程大綱，設計跨越
兩門課程的專題計畫。因此，學生在技術課程中學習特定技術，
並在教學法課程的教學實習中加以整合運用。
在一項與教學法領域教師合作的研究中，技術課程講師
發現，儘管職前教師或許知道如何操作該技術，他們卻不知道
如何在日常教學計畫中有效地整合它，主要原因在於他們無法
構想出學生能夠發展的專題類型（Doering, Hughes, and Huffman, 2002）。
這些研究發現促使技術課程講師為各技術課程科組（即各內容學科）開發示範性的
技術專題與教學法範本。
例如，一個 InspirationTM 專題被作為示範，說明學生如何在科學科組中透過概念圖來建構對雲的理解。這個專題輔以講師在科學課堂中示範有效教學實踐的概念圖運用。其目標是引導職前教師不僅專注於
課程中最終技術專題的完成，更鼓勵他們思考如何
在未來的課堂中成功整合技術。這些範例被放置於線上，使職前教師在為技術課程開發自己的專題時，能隨時取得參考。

英文原文

Each individual content-area course has a separate syllabus that highlights the specific technologies and pedagogy that is relevant to the content area. The technologies were selected after numerous meetings between methods and technology course instructors. After identifying the most appropriate technology, the methods and technology course instructors co-develop their syllabi with projects that span the two courses . Therefore, students learn about a specific technology in the technology course and they integrate it in their practice teaching experiences within their methods course. In a research collaboration with a methods area faculty member, the technology course instructor found that although preservice teachers may know how to operate the technology, they do not know how to integrate it effectively within their daily lessons plans, mainly citing that they were not able to envision the type of projects their students could develop (Doering, Hughes, and Huffman, 2002). These findings influenced the technology course instructor to develop exemplary models of technology projects and pedagogy for each of the technology course sections (ie, content areas). For example, an InspirationTM project was modeled to illustrate how students could construct an understanding of clouds using concept mapping within the science cohort. This project was supplemented by the instructor modeling effective teaching practices using concept mapping in the science classroom. The goal was to move the preservice teachers from focusing not only on the development of a final technology project in the course, but encouraging them to think about successful integration in their future classrooms . These examples were placed online so the preservice teachers had access to them at all times in the development of their own projects for the technology course.

#150 New Women 2（新女性） #060150 原文
中文翻譯

1890年代，英國與北美媒體掀起了一場聲勢浩大的輿論風潮，既有為「新女性」辯護的聲音，也有大肆抨擊的言論。部分評論者將這場風潮的起點精確地定在1894年3月，彼時英國小說家莎拉·格蘭德在《北美評論》上首次以此詞標示這類女性。格蘭德盛讚新女性終於「解決了問題，為自己宣示了『家是女人的領域』這一觀念的錯謬所在」，並開出了解方。另一些評論者則認為，這個詞語是從數十年來持續升溫的辯論中逐漸浮現並凝結成形的，辯論的核心是中產階級女性的地位、她們獨立自主的空間、接受中等及高等教育的意涵，以及婚姻在法律、財務、社會與心理層面加諸她們的種種束縛。

後一種解讀更具啟發性，因為它容許我們在更長的時間跨度內考察更廣泛的文獻——不僅包括小說與戲劇，也涵蓋當時人們所熟知的「女性問題」這一議題上的政治與社會論著，而這一議題也吸引了形形色色的倡議組織參與其中。儘管英國國家體制與政治結構有利於單一議題的運動，這些運動卻往往彼此關聯——儘管各自的首要訴求不盡相同——且在當時人眼中被統稱為「婦女運動」。

英文原文

In the 1890s there was a positive media feeding frenzy in Britain and in North America both defending and attacking the ‘New Woman’ . Some commentators have dated the beginning of this very precisely , from March 1894, when the British novelist Sarah Grand first used the label in an article in the North American Review. Grand hailed the New Woman as one who has at last ‘solved the problem and proclaimed for herself what was wrong with Home is the Woman’s Sphere’, and prescribed the remedy. Other commentators have seen the term growing out of and crystallising a steadily swelling debate over several decades about the position of women of the middle classes, their scope for independence, the implications of access to secondary and higher education, and the legal, financial, social and psychological constraints imposed upon them by marriage. The latter is a more fruitful reading, allowing as it does a consideration of a wider literature over a longer period , not only fiction and drama but also political and social writing on the subject contemporaries came to know as the ‘Woman Question’, and which attracted a range of campaigning organisations. Although the structure of the English state and political system favoured single-issue campaigns, those campaigns were often associated , even though their primary targets differed, and they were collectively known to contemporaries as ‘the women’s movement’ .

#151 Wright brothers (懷特兄弟) #060151 原文
中文翻譯

1903年，來自俄亥俄州代頓市的懷特兄弟——威爾伯與奧維爾——成為史上第一批駕駛重於空氣的動力操控飛行器升空的人，這架飛機被稱為「懷特飛行者號」。這一切並非一蹴而就，兄弟倆從童年起便斷斷續續地鑽研飛行的概念。他們是兩位具有機械天賦的年輕人，深受前人努力的啟發。

1878年，兄弟倆的父親米爾頓·懷特帶回了一個以橡皮筋驅動的玩具直升機。這個玩具由法國航空實驗家阿方斯·佩諾設計，並未如預期般直接落地，而是「飛越整個房間，撞上天花板，在那裡振翅片刻，最後才緩緩落到地板上。」儘管這個易碎的玩具很快就壞了，威爾伯與奧維爾卻從未忘記它。他們甚至嘗試自己動手製作玩具直升機。多年後，奧維爾將這個童年玩具視為點燃他們飛行夢想的起點。

兄弟倆一生中嘗試過各種謀生事業，但直到1892年，他們成立了懷特自行車公司販售自行車，才終於找到一門成功的生意，同時也為其他計畫留有餘裕的時間。隨著生意日漸興隆，兄弟倆還開設了修車店，後來更開始自行製造自行車。

儘管生意蒸蒸日上，兩兄弟內心卻始終躁動不安。1896年發生的兩件大事讓他們的精力有了新的方向：著名滑翔機實驗家奧托·李林塔爾在一次飛行事故中罹難，以及塞繆爾·蘭利成功完成無人動力模型的試飛。這兩人的創意與才智深深觸動了懷特兄弟。幸運的是，自行車生意為這項新興趣提供了資金來源，因為與航空領域的其他人不同，懷特兄弟從未接受過任何人的資助。此外，自行車的修繕與製造也磨練了兄弟倆的機械技能。在建造飛行器的過程中，威爾伯與奧維爾常常沿用修理自行車所用的設備與工具。他們在店鋪後間進行了許多科學實驗，而第一架成功飛行的飛機所使用的大部分零件，也正是在那裡製造完成的。

英文原文

In 1903, Wilbur and Orville Wright , two brothers from Dayton, OH, became the first people to fly a heavier than air, power controlled machine , known as the Wright Flyer. This did not simply happen overnight. The brothers had been tinkering with the idea of flight of f and on since childhood . They were mechanically inclined young men who were inspired by the efforts of others. In 1878, the brothers’ father , Milton Wright, brought home a rubber band powered toy helicopter. Designed by French aeronautical experimenter Alphonse Pénaud, this toy did not simply fall to the ground as expected. Rather, it "flew across the room till it struck the ceilingwhere it fluttered awhile, and finally sank to the floor." Though the fragile toy soon broke, Wilbur and Orville never forgot it. They even attempted to build their own toy helicopters. In later years, Orville accredited this childhood toy as being the object that sparked their interest in flight. Throughout their lives, the brothers were involved in a variety of ventures to make money. But it wasn’ t until 1892 , when they formed the Wright Cycle Company to sell bicycles, that they found a successful business that also allowed them spare time for other projects . With the business doing rather well, the brothers also opened a repair shop and later began to manufacture bicycles. Though the business was going well, the brothers were restless. Their energies were focused by two events of 1896 ; the death of Otto Lilienthal, the celebrated glider experimenter, in a flying accident, and the successful unmanned launching of powered models by Samuel Langley. The creativity and ingenuity of these two men were well and truly captured. Fortunately, the bicycle business provided the funds for this new interest, for unlike others in aviation, the Wrights were never financed by anyone. Furthermore, the repair and manufacture of bicycles sharpened the brothers' mechanical skills . In their construction of flying machines, Wilbur and Orville often used the same equipment and tools used in repairing bicycles. They conducted many of their scientific experiments in the backroom of their shop and most of the parts used in the first successful airplane were built there .

#152 Summer Vacation (暑假) #060152 大意
中文翻譯

幾個世紀以來，九月到六月的學年制度一直是標準，這給現代教育工作者留下了一個問題：如何善用七月和八月。

學生們被告知，暑假是農村社會遺留下來的傳統。在農村地區，學校放假是為了讓學生能夠下田工作——但這些假期是在春季和秋季。冬季和夏季反而是上學的時間。

但暑假標誌著人們對休息價值的一種自覺認可，而非農業勞動週期的遺跡。這種假期最初在城市中實施，因為學校建築品質低劣——加上夏季的酷熱——引發了教育學者和家長對學生身體健康的擔憂。

英文原文

For centuries, a September-to-June school year has been the standard, which leaves a question for modern educators to resolve about how to make use of July and August. Students have been told that the summer break is a tradition born in rural society. In rural areas, school let out so students could work in the fields--but those breaks came in the spring and fall. School was in session in winter and summer. But summer vacation marked a conscious recognition of the value of rest, not a vestige of the farm labor cycle. Such a vacation initially took effect in cities, because the poor quality of school buildings--and the heat of summer--fueled concerns of educational scholars and parents about the physical health of students.

#153 Bertand Russell (伯納德·羅素) #060153 原文
中文翻譯

身為哲學家、數學家、教育家、社會評論家及政治運動者，伯特蘭·羅素著作等身，撰寫了逾七十本著作及數以千計的文章與書信，涵蓋各式各樣的主題。羅素於 1950 年榮獲諾貝爾文學獎，他文筆優雅，是史上最傑出的邏輯學家之一，亦是致力改善人類生活的一股砥礪力量。 他可說是二十世紀最偉大的哲學家，也是自亞里斯多德以來最偉大的邏輯學家。

分析哲學是二十世紀的主流哲學，其存在所歸功於羅素的貢獻，遠超過任何其他哲學家。羅素與懷海德（A.N. Whitehead）共同建立的邏輯體系，奠基於戴德金、康托爾、弗雷格及皮亞諾的早期研究，使邏輯學得以掙脫亞里斯多德學派的束縛。他也是那個世紀最具影響力的公共知識分子之一，並於 1950 年榮獲諾貝爾文學獎，以表彰「他文體多樣、意義深遠的著作，在其中他捍衛人道主義理想與思想自由」。 羅素對他所處時代的眾多社會與政治爭議都積極投入，往往懷抱強烈的熱情。 例如，他支持婦女參政運動、宗教與道德上的自由思想及世界政府；他反對第一次世界大戰與越戰、民族主義以及政治迫害。 他於 1918 年因反戰立場入獄，並於 1961 年因反核武立場再度身陷囹圄。

他結過四次婚，育有三名子女。他與朵拉·羅素（Dora Russell）共同創辦了實驗性的燈塔山學校（Beacon Hill School）。他所認識或共事過的人，涵蓋十九世紀末至二十世紀哲學、數學、科學、文學及政治各領域中許多最傑出的人物。

英文原文

As a philosopher, mathematician, educator, social critic and political activist,Bertrand Russell authored over 70 books and thousands of essays and letters addressing a myriad of topics. Awarded the Nobel Prize in Literature in 1950, Russell was a fine literary stylist, one of the foremost logicians ever, and a gadfly for improving the lives of men and women . He was arguably the greatest philosopher of the 20th century and the greatest logician since Aristotle . Analytic philosophy, the dominant philosophy of the twentieth century, owes its existence more to Russell than to any other philosopher. And the system of logic developed by Russell and AN Whitehead, based on earlier work by Dedekind, Cantor, Frege, and Peano, broke logic out of its Aristotelian straitjacket. He was also one of the century's leading public intellectuals and won the Nobel Prize for Literature in 1950 "in recognition of his varied and significant writings in which he champions humanitarian ideals and freedom of thought . "Russell was involved, often passionately, in numerous social and political controversies of his time . For example, he supported suffragists, free thought in religion and morals, and world government; he opposed World War I and the Vietnam War, nationalism, and political persecution. He was jailed in 1918 for anti-war views and in 1961 for his anti- nuclear weapons stance. He was married 4 times and had 3 children. With Dora Russell, he founded the experimental Beacon Hill School. He knew or worked with many of the most prominent figures in late 19th and 20th century philosophy, mathematics, science, literature, and politics .

2Aristotelian straitjacket. #154 Volcanic Eruption Prediction (火山噴發預測) #060154 大意
中文翻譯

- 關於火山噴發的相關數據，例如 49%、52%……
- 預測火山噴發需要多個事件的累積，單一事件並不足夠。示範模型有助於輔助預測。
- 然而，每座火山各有不同，因此預測的可靠性取決於各火山本身的特性。
- 部分噴發在事前毫無預兆。以某次噴發為例，預測工作需要對火山進行長期研究。
- 居住在火山附近的居民可以將自己的發現提供給科學家參考。

英文原文

#155 Volcanic Eruption Prediction 2 (火山噴發預測2) #060155 原文
中文翻譯

一般而言，沒有任何單一事件可用於預測火山噴發，因此通常需要同時監測多種事件，綜合評估後才能經常準確預測噴發。然而，每座火山的行為各有不同，在找出個別火山的規律之前，預測的可靠性參差不齊。此外，火山有時會在毫無前兆的情況下突然噴發。
1980年5月18日聖海倫斯火山發生災難性噴發後，火山口內開始形成一個熔岩穹丘。此穹丘的生長斷斷續續，有時也會從穹丘處發生小規模噴發。經過數年持續監測，科學家現在已能以越來越高的精確度預測此穹丘的噴發。
右側圖表展示了一個具體例子。在1982年3月19日噴發前的數週內，地震能量釋放量增加、穹丘膨脹量增加、地面傾斜度增加，且二氧化硫排放量也在事件發生前持續上升。
請注意，如此例所示的噴發預測，唯有在對火山進行持續不斷的監測下才有可能實現。
監測是一項耗費大量資源的工作，並非所有活躍或潛在活躍的火山都受到監測。
儘管如此，若居住在火山周邊的民眾能夠留意一些前兆現象，他們或許能將所觀察到的異常事件告知科學家，使科學家得以開始定期監測，從而協助預防即將發生的災難。

英文原文

In general, no single event can be used to predict a volcanic eruption, and thus many events are usually monitored so that taken in total, an eruption can often be predicted . Still, each volcano behaves somewhat differently, and until patterns are recognized for an individual volcano, predictions vary in their reliability . Furthermore, sometimes a volcano can erupt with no precursor events at all . After the catastrophic eruption of Mount St Helens on May 18, 1980, a volcanic dome began to grow in the crater. Growth of this dome occurred sporadically, and sometimes small eruptions occurred from the dome. After several years of dedicated monitoring, scientists are now able to predict with increasing accuracy eruptions from this dome. An example is shown in the graphs to the right. In the weeks prior to an eruption on March 19, 1982, the amount of seismic energy released increased, the amount dome expansion increased, tilt increased, and SO₂ emissions increased prior to the event. Note that eruption predictions such as in this example are only possible if constant monitoring of a volcano takes place . Monitoring is an expensive endeavor, and not all active or potentially active volcanoes are monitored . Still, if people living around volcanoes are aware of some of the precursor phenomena that occur, they may be able to communicate their findings of anomalous events to scientists who can begin monitoring on a regular basis and help prevent a pending disaster .

紅字句（原文）
#原文
1In general, no single event can be used to predict a volcanic eruption, and thus many events are usually monitored so that taken in total, an eruption can often be predicted . Still, each volcano behaves somewhat differently, and until patterns are recognized for an individual volcano, predictions vary in their reliability . Furthermore, sometimes a volcano can erupt with no precursor events at all .
2Note that eruption predictions such as in this example are only possible if constant monitoring of a volcano takes place . Monitoring is an expensive endeavor, and not all active or potentially active volcanoes are monitored . Still, if people living around volcanoes are aware of some of the precursor phenomena that occur, they may be able to communicate their findings of anomalous events to scientists who can begin monitoring on a regular basis and help prevent a pending disaster .
#156 Computers and Human Brains (計算機與人腦) #060156 大意
中文翻譯

部分認知科學家嘗試利用電腦來模擬人腦，因為他們認為電腦與人腦具有相似之處。例如，電腦能夠儲存與提取資訊，而人腦則能夠記憶與回憶資訊。然而，部分科學家認為兩者存在差異，因為人腦能夠產生情緒，而電腦的處理速度則比人腦更快。因此，利用電腦來模擬人腦並不切實際。

英文原文

Some cognitive scientists are trying to use computers to mimic human brains because they think computers and human brains are similar. For example, computers can store and retrieve information, and human brains can remember and recall information. However, some scientists argue that these two are different because the human brain can generate emotions, whereas computers process faster than human brains do. Therefore, it is not realistic to use computers to mimic human brains.

#157 Energy Demand (能源需求) #060157 原文
中文翻譯

隨著全球人口持續增長，地球資源所承受的壓力也日益加劇。我們面臨的核心挑戰，是如何滿足支撐這一增長所需的急劇攀升的能源需求。這不僅僅是維持電力供應的問題，更關乎驅動我們現代生活每一個層面的能源需求。
隨著人口增長，對各類資源的需求也持續上升，這在各個領域引發了一連串複雜的連鎖反應。

各種替代資源、原材料、造紙用木材，當然還有能源，預計需求都將大幅增加。這股需求浪潮是可以理解的——更多的人需要更多的住房、消費品與包裝材料，而這一切都需要大量的原材料與生產所需的能源。

然而，壓力並不僅限於可再生資源領域。需求的增長同樣出現在非可再生資源領域，例如金屬。這些金屬是建築、科技與基礎設施不可或缺的材料，但其供應量是有限的。此外，我們對化石燃料的依賴依然根深柢固。汽油、柴油與原油的需求也極為龐大，以應對製造塑膠以及驅動全球運輸網絡運送這些商品所產生的巨大需求。

這種相互交織的需求帶來了一個關鍵的兩難困境。一方面，我們需要這些資源來維持並提升生活水準；另一方面，資源的開採與消耗卻帶來了嚴重的環境後果。

這正是為何走向可持續發展的道路至關重要。人們應當確保自然界仍能良好運作，以保障未來的福祉，因為全球人口仍在持續增長。

英文原文

As our global population continues to expand, the pressure on our planet's resources intensifies. A central challenge we face is how to meet the skyrocketing energy demand required to support this growth . This isn't just about keeping the lights on; it's about powering every facet of our modern lives. With the population growth, the demand for resources has been growing as well. This creates a complex chain reaction across various sectors. There is an expected increase in demand for various alternative resources, raw materials, timber for paper using, and of course, energy. This surge is understandable. More people need more homes, consumer goods, and packaging, all of which require vast amounts of materials and the energy to produce them. However, the strain is not limited to renewable resources. The increase in demand also happens in the non-renewable resource field, such as metal. These metals are essential for construction, technology, and infrastructure, but their supply is finite. Furthermore, our reliance on fossil fuels remains deeply entrenched . The demand for petrol, diesel and crude oil is also huge to cope with the demand for manufacturing plastics and for powering the global transportation network that moves these goods around the world. This interconnected demand presents a critical dilemma . On one hand, we need these resources to maintain and improve living standards. On the other, their extraction and consumption have significant environmental consequences. This is why a sustainable path forward is crucial . People should ensure the natural world can still work well to ensure future well-being because the world population rises.

#158 Urbanization and Sustainability (城市化與可持續發展) #060158 原文
中文翻譯

城市化一直是現代時代的決定性趨勢，全球超過一半的人口現居住在城市中。城市提供了眾多優勢，包括獲得更好的就業機會、醫療保健、教育及文化設施。城市地區人口與資源的集中推動了經濟增長與創新，使城市成為發展的引擎。此外，城市通常充當多元文化的熔爐，促進社會融合與思想交流。

然而，居住在城市也帶來了若干挑戰。城市地區經常深受交通擁擠、污染及高生活成本等問題的困擾。密集的人口可能對基礎設施和公共服務造成壓力，導致住房不足和醫療設施匱乏等問題。此外，城市通常以懸殊的不平等為特徵，不同社區之間在財富和資源獲取方面存在顯著差距。城市化的快速步伐可能加劇這些問題，因為城市難以應對不斷增長的人口。可持續性是城市生活另一個關鍵的隱憂，高能耗與廢棄物的大量產生助長了環境惡化與氣候變遷。

為應對這些挑戰，城市規劃者和政策制定者日益致力於打造可持續、宜居的城市。這涉及推廣公共交通、綠色空間、可再生能源及高效的廢棄物管理系統。透過採取這些措施，城市可以在降低環境影響的同時提升居民的生活品質。歸根究柢，城市雖提供了眾多益處，但也需要審慎的規劃與管理，以確保城市持續成為充滿活力、包容共融且永續發展的居住之地。

英文原文

Urbanization has been a defining trend of the modern era , with more than half of the world's population now living in cities. Cities offer numerous advantages, including access to better job opportunities, healthcare, education, and cultural amenities . The concentration of people and resources in urban areas drives economic growth and innovation, making cities engines of development. Additionally, cities often serve as melting pots of diverse cultures, fostering social integration and the exchange of ideas. However, living in cities also presents several challenges . Urban areas are frequently plagued by issues such as traffic congestion, pollution, and high living costs . The dense population can strain infrastructure and public services, leading to problems like inadequate housing and healthcare facilities. Furthermore, cities are often characterized by stark inequalities , with significant disparities in wealth and access to resources between different neighborhoods. The rapid pace of urbanization can exacerbate these issues, as cities struggle to accommodate the growing population. Sustainability is another critical concern for urban living. High energy consumption and waste generation contribute to environmental degradation and climate change. To address these challenges, urban planners and policymakers are increasingly focusing on creating sustainable, livable cities . This involves promoting public transportation, green spaces, renewable energy sources, and efficient waste management systems. By adopting such measures, cities can enhance the quality of life for their residents while minimizing their environmental impact. Ultimately, while cities offer numerous benefits, they also require careful planning and management to ensure that they remain vibrant, inclusive, and sustainable places to live.

#159 The San (南非土著） #060159 原文
中文翻譯

桑人（San），南非南部民族，由數個群體組成，總人口逾八萬五千人。他們身材普遍矮小，膚色呈黃褐色，顴骨明顯突出。白人曾稱桑人為「布希曼人」（Bushmen），但此稱謂現已被視為帶有貶義。儘管許多人如今受僱於白人移民，仍有約半數人過著遊牧生活，在卡拉哈里半沙漠等荒僻地帶以狩獵和採集野生食物為生；卡拉哈里半沙漠橫跨今日的波札那、納米比亞與南非三國。他們的社會單位是小型狩獵群體，較大規模的組織則鬆散且具臨時性質。草屋、洞穴與岩石掩蔽處是他們的居所，他們僅攜帶力所能及之物，以塗毒箭頭獵殺野獸，並以鴕鳥蛋殼盛水運送。桑人擁有豐富的民間傳說，擅長繪畫，並使用一種極為複雜的語言，以點擊音為其特色，與科伊科伊人（Khoikhoi）的語言相近。數千年來，桑人居住於南部及中部非洲，但在十五世紀葡萄牙人抵達之時，他們已被迫遷入南部非洲內陸。十八至十九世紀間，他們抵抗荷蘭移民對其土地的侵佔，然而至一八六二年，這場抵抗已遭到徹底鎮壓。

英文原文

San, people of southern Africa , consisting of several groups and numbering over 85,000 in all. They are generally short instature; their skin is yellowish brown in color; and they feature prominent cheekbones. The San have been calledBushmen by whites in South Africa, but the term is now considered derogatory . Aithough many now work for white settlers, about half are still nomadic hunters and gatherers of wild food in desolate areas like the Kalahari semi-desert, which stretches between today's Nation States of Botswana, Namibia and SouthAfrica. Their social unit is the small hunting band; larger organizations are loose and temporary. Grass Huts, caves androck shelters are used as dwellings , They possess only what they can carry, using poisoned arrow heads to fell game andtransporting water in ostrich-eggshells. The San have a rich folklore , are skilled in drawing, and have a remarkablycomplex language characterized by the use of click sounds, related to that of the Khoikhoi. For thousands of years the San lived in southern and central Africa , but by the time of the Portuguese arrival in the 15thcent., they had already been forced into the interior of southern Africa. In the 18th and 19th cent., they resisted the encroachment on their lands of Dutch settlers, but by 1862 that resistance had been crushed.
