#160 Authority (權威) #060160 原文
中文翻譯

在對正式組織最早期的研究之一中，韋伯區分了三種權威類型：傳統型、魅力型與法理型。這些權威類型以下屬認為正當的控制形式為基礎，並涉及下屬對上級權力的接受。這三種權威類型對應不同類型的組織。

在傳統型組織中，權威由習俗以及對統治自然權利的長久信念所賦予正當性，或由傳統（「正統」）程序所持有。例子包括教宗、國王或女王，或家長式雇主的權威。

在魅力型組織中，權威由對領導者個人特質的信仰所賦予正當性；權威建立在領導者的人格力量與感召力之上。溫斯頓·邱吉爾可作為一個例子。

對某種常規、程序與制度，以及經濟支援的現實需求，意味著若要使運動持續下去，就必須加以組織化。當魅力型領導者即將離世時，若找不到「正統」繼承人，整個運動可能隨之瓦解。這一過程往往使魅力型組織轉變為傳統型組織或官僚型組織。

在官僚型組織中，權威建立在對正式規則與程序之法律的接受，以及非人格化原則之上。其法理型權威源自於在組織中的層級位置，而非個人特質。

例子包括武裝部隊，以及政府部長或學院校長的權威。

法理型權威的概念對我們最具參考價值，因為大多數商業組織，尤其是大型組織，往往傾向採取官僚型結構，儘管在程度上存在差異。官僚制度，就其適用於組織某些結構特徵而言，是最主要的正式組織類型。

英文原文

In one of the earliest studies of formal organizations, Weber distinguished three types of authority: traditional, charismatic and legal-rational . These types of authority are based on the form of control regarded as legitimate by subordinates and their acceptance of the power of superiors. The three types of authority relate to different types of organizations . In traditional organizations, authority is legitimized by custom and a longstanding belief in the natural right to rule, or is possessed by traditional (“proper”) procedure . Examples would be the authority of the Pope, kings or queens or a paternalistic employer. In charismatic organizations, authority is legitimised by belief in the personal qualities of the leader ; authority is based on the leader's strength of personality and inspiration.Winston Churchill might be quoted as an example. The practical need for some routine, for procedures and systems and for economic support means that if the movement is to continue it must become organized.On the impending demise of the charismatic leader the movement might collapse unless a “legitimate” heir is found.This process tends to transform a charismatic organization into either a traditional organization or a bureaucratic organisation. In bureaucratic organizations, authority is based on the acceptance of the law of formal rules and procedures , and on impersonal principles.There is a legal-rational authority which stems from hierarchical position in the organization and not from personality. Examples are the armed forces and the authority of government ministers or a college principal. The concept of legal-rational authority is of most interest to us because most business organizations, particularly large-scale ones, tend to be of the bureaucratic type of structure , although there are variations in degree.Bureaucracy, as applying to certain structural features of organization, is the most dominant type of formal organization.

紅字句（原文）
#原文
1In one of the earliest studies of formal organizations, Weber distinguished three types of authority: traditional, charismatic and legal-rational . These types of authority are based on the form of control regarded as legitimate by subordinates and their acceptance of the power of superiors. The three types of authority relate to different types of organizations . In traditional organizations, authority is legitimized by custom and a longstanding belief in the natural right to rule, or is possessed by traditional (“proper”) procedure . Examples would be the authority of
2In charismatic organizations, authority is legitimised by belief in the personal qualities of the leader ;
3In bureaucratic organizations, authority is based on the acceptance of the law of formal rules and procedures , and on impersonal principles.There is a legal-rational authority which stems from

#161 Wright Brothers (懷特兄弟「確認版」) #060161 原文
中文翻譯

1903年，來自俄亥俄州代頓市的懷特兄弟——威爾伯與奧維爾——成為史上第一批駕駛
重於空氣、動力可控機器飛行的人，該機器即著名的「萊特飛行者號」。這一成就並非一蹴可幾，
兄弟倆自幼便斷斷續續地鑽研飛行的概念。他們是天生具有機械天賦的年輕人，並從他人的努力中汲取靈感。

1878年，兄弟倆的父親米爾頓·懷特帶回家一個由橡皮筋驅動的玩具
直升機。這個玩具由法國航空實驗者阿爾方斯·佩諾設計，並未如預期般直接落地，
而是「飛越整個房間，直到撞上天花板，在那裡顫動了一會兒，最終才落到地板上。」這個易碎的玩具很快就損壞了，但威爾伯和奧維爾始終
未曾忘懷。他們甚至嘗試自製玩具直升機。多年後，奧維爾將這個
童年玩具視為點燃他們飛行夢想的起點。

兄弟倆一生涉足各種事業以維持生計，但直到1892年他們創辦懷特自行車公司販售自行車，才
找到一門既成功又能讓他們有餘暇追求其他興趣的事業。隨著生意蒸蒸日上，
兄弟倆也開設了一間維修店，後來更開始自行製造自行車。

儘管生意順遂，兄弟倆內心卻始終躁動不安。1896年的兩件大事將他們的精力重新聚焦：其一是著名滑翔機實驗家奧托·李林塔爾在一次飛行事故中喪生，
其二是塞繆爾·蘭利成功發射無人動力模型飛機。這兩位先驅的創造力與
獨創性深深俘獲了他們的心。幸運的是，自行車生意為這項新興趣提供了資金，因為與其他航空先驅不同，懷特兄弟從未接受過
任何外部資助。

此外，自行車的維修與製造也磨練了兄弟倆的機械技能。在建造飛行機器的過程中，
威爾伯和奧維爾常常使用與修理自行車相同的設備和工具。他們在店鋪後室進行了許多科學實驗，而第一架成功飛行的飛機所使用的大多數零件，也正是在那裡製造完成的。

英文原文

In 1903, Wilbur and Orville Wright, two brothers from Dayton, OH, became the first people to fly a heavier-than-air, power-controlled machine, known as the Wright Flyer. This did not simply happen overnight. The brothers had been tinkering with the idea of flight off and on since childhood. They were mechanically inclined young men who were inspired by the efforts of others. In 1878, the brothers’ father, Milton Wright, brought home a rubber-band-powered toy helicopter. Designed by French aeronautical experimenter Alphonse Pénaud, this toy did not simply fall to the ground as expected. Rather, it “flew across the room till it struck the ceiling, where it fluttered awhile, and finally sank to the floor.” Though the fragile toy soon broke, Wilbur and Orville never forgot it. They even attempted to build their own toy helicopters. In later years, Orville accredited this childhood toy as being the object that sparked their interest in flight. Throughout their lives, the brothers were involved in a variety of ventures to make money. But it wasn’t until 1892, when they formed the Wright Cycle Company to sell bicycles, that they found a successful business that also allowed them spare time for other projects. With the business doing rather well, the brothers also opened a repair shop and later began to manufacture bicycles. Though the business was going well, the brothers were restless. Their energies were focused by two events of 1896; the death of Otto Lilienthal, the celebrated glider experimenter, in a flying accident, and the successful unmanned launching of powered models by Samuel Langley. The creativity and ingenuity of these two men were well and truly captured. Fortunately, the bicycle business provided the funds for this new interest, for unlike others in aviation, the Wrights were never financed by anyone. Furthermore, the repair and manufacture of bicycles sharpened the brothers’ mechanical skills. In their construction of flying machines, Wilbur and Orville often used the same equipment and tools used in repairing bicycles. They conducted many of their scientific experiments in the back room of their shop, and most of the parts used in the first successful airplane were built there.

#164 Job Replaced by Automation(工作被自動化取代) #060164 大意
中文翻譯

在過去100年裡，自動化的發展持續引發外界對失業問題的擔憂。

雖然許多例行性和重複性的工作確實已被機器輕易取代，但並非所有職位都同樣脆弱。

例如，需要複雜決策、創造力和人類判斷力的角色——例如執行長——至今仍難以被自動化取代。

儘管經歷了數十年的技術進步與廣泛的焦慮，人類並未被自動化完全取代。

相反地，技術往往改變了工作的本質，在淘汰部分職業的同時，也創造了新的職位與產業。

英文原文

- Over the last 100 years, the development of automation has consistently raised concerns about job losses. - While it is true that many routine and repetitive jobs have been easily replaced by machines, not all positions are equally vulnerable. - For instance, roles that require complex decision-making, creativity, and human judgment—such as that of a CEO—remain difficult to automate. - Despite decades of technological advancement and widespread anxiety, humans have not been completely replaced by automation. - Instead, technology has often transformed the nature of work, creating new roles and industries while rendering others obsolete.

#165 Drone Delivery(無人機配送) #060165 大意
中文翻譯

華盛頓大學運輸工程師的一項全新研究發現，在某些情況下，與卡車配送相比，使用無人機配送包裹可減少二氧化碳排放。

研究人員發現，當無人機不需要飛行很遠的距離抵達目的地，或配送路線收件人較少時，無人機往往比卡車具有二氧化碳排放優勢。

卡車單次能運載大量貨物，當配送路線有多個停靠點或距離中央倉庫較遠時，卡車反而是更環保的選擇。

對於小型輕量的包裹，無人機的表現尤為出色。

然而，隨著包裹重量增加，碳排放效益會隨之下降，因為無人機需要消耗額外能源才能攜帶更重的貨物保持飛行。

英文原文

-Delivering packages with drones will reduce CO2 emissions in certain circumstances as compared to truck deliveries, a brand new study from University of Washington transportation engineers finds. - Researchers found that drones tend to have CO2 emission advantages over trucks when the drones do not have to fly very far to their destinations or when a delivery route has few recipients. - Trucks, which can carry many goods in a single trip, become a more climate-friendly option when a delivery route has several stops or is far from a central warehouse. - For small and light-weight packages, drones perform particularly well. - However, the carbon benefits decline as the weight of a package increases because drones require extra energy to stay airborne with heavier loads.

#167 Aggressive Behavior(侵略行爲) #060167 大意
中文翻譯

侵略行為通常被分為兩大類：敵意性（反應性）攻擊與目標導向性（主動性）攻擊。

敵意性攻擊是對感知威脅的防禦反應，而目標導向性攻擊則是為達成特定目的而預謀的行為。

此類攻擊行為通常與「侵略行動是實現個人目標的有效手段」這一信念密切相關。

攻擊行為深受外部因素的影響，包括文化與社會規範。

在法律執行薄弱、犯罪率高或社會結構鬆散的社會中，暴力行為往往更為普遍。

當社會體系無法有效管理衝突時，個人可能訴諸「自助式」暴力，並變得更具攻擊性以保護自身。

英文原文

- Aggressive behavior is commonly classified into two main types: hostile (reactive) aggression and goal-oriented (proactive) aggression. - Hostile aggression is a defensive response to a perceived threat, while goal-oriented aggression is planned behavior intended to achieve a specific objective. - Such aggression is often linked to the belief that aggressive actions are an effective way to achieve personal goals. - Aggression is strongly influenced by external factors, including cultural and social norms. - In societies with weak legal enforcement, high crime rates, or loose social structures, violence tends to be more common. - When social systems fail to manage conflicts effectively, individuals may resort to “self-help” violence and become more aggressive to protect themselves.

- 這份最新報告聚焦於研究人員對學術圖書館的使用方式，有助於培養並鼓勵館員深入理解實務工作。
- 報告的研究結果在一場由研究人員、圖書館員及館員共同參與的工作坊中進行討論，與會者一致認為學術圖書館仍有進一步改善的空間。
- 圖書館正從單純提供資源，轉型為研究過程中的積極協作者，尤其在數位典藏、資料管理與開放取用等領域更是如此。
- 圖書館員工需要更積極主動地參與研究工作，並更深入理解研究人員的專業「語言」。
- 研究人員的需求與部分圖書館所提供的服務之間，仍存在相當大的落差，尤其在支援專業研究資料方面更為明顯。
- 報告同時強調培育二十一世紀學術館員的重要性，包括強化資料科學、開放研究及夥伴關係建立等方面的能力。

英文原文

- The RLUK (Research Libraries UK) released a report examining the role of research libraries in producing scholarly research and emphasizing that library staff should act as partners and leaders rather than merely service providers. - The recent report focuses on researchers' use of academic library, helping to develop and encourage librarians to understand practice. - The report’s findings were discussed in a workshop involving researchers, librarians, and library staff, where participants argued that academic libraries still need further improvement. - Libraries are shifting from simply providing resources to becoming active collaborators in research, especially in areas such as digital curation, data management, and open access. - Library staff need to focus more on proactive engagement in research and better understanding the professional “language” of researchers. - There remains a significant gap between researchers’ needs and the services provided by some libraries, particularly in supporting specialized research materials. - The report also stresses the importance of developing 21st-century academic librarians by strengthening skills in data science, open research, and partnership building.

#169 Computers and Human Brains （計算機與人腦） #060169 大意
中文翻譯

一些認知科學家嘗試用計算機來模擬人腦，因為他們認為兩者具有某些相似之處。

例如，計算機能夠存儲和檢索信息，而人腦則能夠記憶和回憶信息。

然而，一些科學家認為，計算機和人腦在本質上是不同的。

人腦能夠產生情感，而計算機處理信息的速度則比人腦更快。

因此，用計算機來完全模擬人腦是不切實際的。

英文原文

- Some cognitive scientists try to use computers to mimic human brains because they believe the two share certain similarities. - For example, computers can store and retrieve information, while human brains can remember and recall information. - However, some scientists argue that computers and human brains are fundamentally different. - The human brain can generate emotions, whereas computers can process information faster than human brains. - Therefore, it is unrealistic to use computers to fully mimic human brains.

#170 Differences in Intelligence(智力差異) #060170 原文
中文翻譯

人們在通常所稱的「智力」方面存在很大的差異，這些差異不僅體現在學業表現上，也體現在日常能力中，例如理解詞彙、閱讀地圖、遵從指示或記憶資訊。
這些差異十分普遍，以至於人們往往視之為理所當然。
過去普遍認為，環境因素——例如學習經歷、父母影響以及學校的語言訓練——是認知能力差異的主要來源。
然而，現代心理學已採取一種更為平衡的觀點，認為先天與後天在認知發展中相互作用。
遺傳學研究顯示，遺傳在塑造智力與認知功能方面扮演著重要角色。
這些研究結果並非否定環境的影響，而是指出基因差異會影響個體學習的難易程度。

英文原文

People differ greatly in what is commonly called intelligence, and these differences appear not only in school but also in everyday abilities such as understanding words, reading maps, following directions, or remembering information. These variations are so common that they are often taken for granted. It was once widely believed that environmental factors, such as learning experiences, parental influence, and language training in schools, were the main sources of differences in cognitive abilities. However, modern psychology has adopted a more balanced view in which both nature and nurture interact in cognitive development . Studies in genetics show that heredity plays an important role in shaping intelligence and cognitive functions . Rather than rejecting environmental influences, these findings suggest that genetic differences affect how easily individuals learn.

紅字句（原文）
#原文
1People differ greatly in what is commonly called intelligence, and these differences appear not only in school but also in everyday abilities such as understanding words, reading maps, following directions, or remembering information.
2However, modern psychology has adopted a more balanced view in which both nature and nurture interact in cognitive development . Studies in genetics show that heredity plays an important role in shaping intelligence and cognitive functions .

#173 Product Life Cycle(産品生命周期) #060173 原文
中文翻譯

產品生命週期有四個定義非常明確的階段，每個階段都有其各自的特徵，對於試圖管理特定產品生命週期的企業來說意義各不相同。導入
階段——這個階段對於推出新產品的公司來說可能是花費最高的一個階段。
該產品的市場規模較小，這意味著銷售量偏低，儘管銷售量會持續增長。另一方面，研發、消費者測試等方面的成本，以及
產品上市所需的行銷費用可能非常高，尤其是在競爭激烈的行業中更是如此。
成長階段——成長階段的典型特徵是銷售額與利潤的強勁增長，
由於公司可以開始在生產上享受規模經濟的效益，利潤率以及整體利潤總額都會隨之提升。這使得企業得以投入更多
資金於推廣活動，以充分發揮這一成長階段的潛力。成熟階段——在
成熟階段，產品已建立穩固的市場地位，製造商的目標轉為維持其所建立的
市場份額。這對大多數產品而言可能是競爭最為激烈的時期，
企業需要審慎地投資於所採取的任何行銷活動。他們還需要考慮對產品進行任何改良，或對生產流程加以改進，以獲取
競爭優勢。衰退階段——最終，某項產品的市場將開始萎縮，
這就是所謂的衰退階段。這種萎縮可能源於市場趨於飽和（即所有會購買該產品的消費者都已完成購買），或是因為消費者正在轉向另一種類型的產品。雖然這種衰退或許難以避免，但企業仍有可能透過轉向成本更低的生產方式及進入更廉價的市場，來繼續獲取一定利潤。

英文原文

The product life cycle has 4 very clearly defined stages , each with its characteristics that mean different things for businesses that are trying to manage the life cycle of their particular products. Introduction Stage - This stage of the cycle could be the most expensive for a company launching a new product. The size of the market for the product is small, which means sales are low, although they will be increasing . On the other hand, the cost of things like research and development, consumer testing, and the marketing needed to launch the product can be very high, especially if it's a competitive sector. Growth Stage - The growth stage is typically characterized by strong growth in sales and profits , and because the company can start to benefit from economies of scale in production, the profit margins, as well as the overall amount of profit, will increase. This makes it possible for businesses to invest more money in promotional activity to maximize the potential of this growth stage. Maturity Stage - During the maturity stage, the product is established and the aim for the manufacturer is now to maintain the market share they have built up . This is probably the most competitive time for most products and businesses need to invest wisely in any marketing they undertake. They also need to consider any product modifications or improvements to the production process which might give them a competitive advantage. Decline Stage - Eventually, the market for a product will start to shrink , and this is what's known as the decline stage. This shrinkage could be due to the market becoming saturated (i.e. all the customers who will buy the product have already purchased it), or because the consumers are switching to a different type of product. While this decline may be inevitable, it may still be possible for companies to make some profit by switching to less-expensive production methods and cheaper markets.

#174 Fallacy (謬論） #060174 大意
中文翻譯

談到謬論時，有一個重要的例外需要注意：雖然許多謬論因為推理不當而明顯具有誤導性，但有些則不那麼明顯——它們涉及一些乍看之下似乎毫不相關的事物，但實際上可能存在關聯。從本質上說，這個例外凸顯了辨識謬論的複雜性。謬論在日常生活中十分常見。舉例而言，當甲打電話給乙卻發現電話不通時，一個典型的謬論是：甲草率地得出乙在刻意迴避自己的結論，卻忽略了電池沒電、訊號不良或技術故障等其他可能性。謬論也可以在心理層面觀察到，因為我們與生俱來的偏見和認知捷徑，往往在不知不覺中使我們產生有缺陷的推理。我們常常傾向於快速下結論，而非仔細思考，這便很容易滋生謬論。

英文原文

When talking about fallacy, one important exception to note is this: while many fallacies are clearly misleading because of bad reasoning, some are less obviousthey involve things that seem unrelated at first, but might actually be connected . Essentially, this exception highlights the complexity of identifying it. Fallacy is common in daily life . For example, when Person A calls Person B and finds the phone not working, a typical fallacy iss A hastily concluding B is avoiding them, ignoring possibilities like a dead battery, poor signal,or technical issues. Fallacy also can be observed at the psychological level , as our inherent biases and cognitive shortcuts often lead us to makeflawed reasoning without noticing it. We often tend to draw quick conclusions instead of thinking carefully, which easily gives rise to fallacies.

Essentially, this exception highlights the complexity of identifying it. Fallacy is common in daily life . For example, when Person A calls Person B and finds the
2like a dead battery, poor signal,or technical issues. Fallacy also can be observed at the psychological level , as our inherent biases and cognitive shortcuts often lead us to makeflawed reasoning without
#175 Public Speaking (公共演講) #060175 原文
中文翻譯

許多不安全感、恐懼和疑慮，都源自於對某件事缺乏理解或缺乏認識。你對一個情境了解得越多、知道得越多，你就會越自在，你的害羞也就越無法左右你。

以公開演講為例。這是一項讓大多數人嚇得半死的活動，但原因只是大多數人對它所知甚少。如果你做一些研究和調查，你會了解到，對公開演講感到恐懼是完全正常的，而且幾乎每一個人都和你有著同樣的恐懼與不安。當你進一步追問自己為何如此恐懼時，你會發現自己害怕被評判，或被嘲笑。從那裡出發，你可以去閱讀和學習那些擅長公開演講的人——學習他們的訣竅和策略。

這樣一來，你就會因為對這個主題有了豐富的知識而做好更充分的準備。因此，你的自信心將遠比以前更高，這或許能讓你在加入像 Toastmasters 這樣的社團時，鼓起勇氣嘗試公開演講。隨著你不斷練習，你自然會變得更加自信。

這個原則適用於任何你感到不安的領域。盡可能地閱讀和研究相關主題。這將有助於提升你的自信，讓你敢於嘗試這項活動，看看自己是否能夠做得更好。而那最初敢於行動的自信，正是你啟動一切、克服害羞所需要的全部。

英文原文

Many insecurities, fears, and doubts stem from lack of understanding or lack of knowledge about something. The more you understand and know about a situation, the more comfortable you will be and thus the less power your shyness will have over you . Let’s take for example the subject of public speaking. This is an activity that terrifies most people half to death, but only because most people don’t have much knowledge about it. If you do some research and investigation, you’ll come to learn that it’s perfectly natural to be terrified of public speaking, and that almost every single person has the same fears and insecurities that you do. When you take it further and ask yourself why you are so terrified of this, you’ll come to learn that you are scared of being judged, or of being laughed at. From there, you can go and read and learn about people who are good at public speaking —learn their tips and strategies. This way you are much more prepared because your knowledge on the subject is vast. As a result of this, your confidence will already be much higher than before , which might allow you to attempt public speaking when you join a club like Toastmasters. As you practice more, you will naturally become even more confident. This rule applies to any area where you feel insecure . Read and research as much about the topic as possible. This will help increase your confidence enough to give the activity a try to see if you might be able to become better at it. And that initial confidence to take action is all you need to get the ball rolling and overcome your shyness.

2When you take it further and ask yourself why you are so terrified of this, you’ll come to learn that you are scared of being judged, or of being laughed at. From there, you can go and read and learn about people who are good at public speaking —learn their tips and strategies.
3this, your confidence will already be much higher than before , which might allow you to attempt public
4This rule applies to any area where you feel insecure . Read and research as much about the topic as
#176 Life-long learning(終身學習) #060176 大意
中文翻譯

學習過程中常伴隨著令人感到羞愧的時刻，例如努力跟上他人的學習進度卻力不從心、即使經過反覆講解仍無法理解關鍵概念，或是無法將所學知識實際應用於實踐中。
然而，這並不意味著我們應該放棄終身學習——導師能夠提供專業指導，幫助我們克服困難並建立自信；朋友能在我們感到沮喪時給予情感支持與鼓勵；夥伴則能與我們攜手並進，互相交流想法、共同成長——這一切都能幫助我們堅持終身學習。

英文原文

Learning often comes with moments that make people feel humiliated, such as struggling to keep up with others’ learning progress, failing to understand key concepts even after repeated explanations, or being unable to apply what they have learned in practice. However, this does not mean we should give up on life-long learning—mentors can offer professional guidance to help us overcome difficulties and build confidence, friends can provide emotional support and encouragement when we feel frustrated, and partners can work with us hand in hand, exchanging ideas and making progress together, all of which can assist us in adhering to life-long learning.

#177 Triangulation (叁角驗證) #060177 原文
中文翻譯

儘管多方法研究正經歷一股普及熱潮，我們仍有理由擔憂：多方法應用是否真的比單一方法研究產出了更有根據、更具說服力的推論。這些疑慮源自「三角驗證」框架——它被視為多方法社會科學研究的原型設計。簡單來說，三角驗證設計是用兩種不同方法提出同一個因果推論問題，並檢驗是否得出相同的實質結論。其比喻來自幾何技術：從兩個不同的觀測點測量視角，藉此估算距離。

三角驗證在社會科學中存在重大缺陷。其中一個廣為人知且被廣泛討論的缺陷是：當兩種方法產生不同結論時，應該如何解讀？不幸的是，面對這種結果，在智識上合理的應對方式幾乎是無窮無盡的。例如，學者可以合理地得出以下結論：兩項結論皆正確，只是捕捉到了研究現象的不同面向；其中一種方法在分析上存在根本性的局限；兩種方法的差異本身就是對各自假設可信度的反證；結果反映的是兩種方法在研究範圍或適用對象上的差異；或者，未能完成三角驗證只是讓推論停留在不確定的狀態。數十年來關於三角驗證的著述中，至今仍未出現任何確定性的指引，說明在一項研究中面對多種方法結論相左時應如何回應。

英文原文

While multi-method research is experiencing a surge of popuarity, there are reasons to worry about whether multi-method applications are producing more grounded, justified, and persuasive inferences than single-method studies . These concerns arise from the 'triangulation' framework as prototypical research design for multi-method social science. Simply put, triangulation designs involve asking the same causal inference question using two different methods, checking same substantive conclusions. The metaphor is to the geometric technique of estimating distance by measuring the angle of sight toward an object from two different vantage points. Triangulation in social sciences has major flaws . One is well-known and widely discussed: what conclusion should be drawn when the two methods produce different findings? Unfortunately, theist of intellectually plausible responses to such an outcome is all but unbounded . For example,a scholar could reasonably conclude that both findings are correct but capture different aspects of the phenomenon of interest; that one method or the other displayed fundamental limitations in the analysis; that the divergence provides evidence against the credibility of the assumptions involved in both methods; that the outcome involves a contrast in terms of scope or relevant populations for the two methods; or that the failure to triangulate simply leaves the inference in a state of uncertainty. In decades of writing about triangulation, no definitive guidancehas yet emerged about how to respond to divergent findings between the multiple methods in a study .

紅字句（原文）
#原文
1While multi-method research is experiencing a surge of popuarity, there are reasons to worry about whether multi-method applications are producing more grounded, justified, and persuasive inferences than single-method studies . These concerns arise from the 'triangulation' framework as prototypical
2Triangulation in social sciences has major flaws . One is well-known and widely discussed: what conclusion should be drawn when the two methods produce different findings? Unfortunately, theist of intellectually plausible responses to such an outcome is all but unbounded .
3in a state of uncertainty. In decades of writing about triangulation, no definitive guidancehas yet emerged about how to respond to divergent findings between the multiple methods in a study .
#178 On the Origin of Species (物種起源) #060178 原文
中文翻譯

1837年，達爾文在28歲時於其中一本筆記本中寫下「物種變化」，這是他演化思想最早的文字紀錄。
在此之前，他曾乘坐小獵犬號環遊世界五年，在南美洲、大洋洲等地觀察到大量物種並非一成不變的跡象。
回到英格蘭後，他在另一本筆記本中寫下「cuidado」（西班牙語，意為「小心」），意識到演化論是一種激進而危險的觀點，當時尚無充分的證據可以公諸於世。
此後二十年間，達爾文持續積累大量資料，並首先在小範圍的科學家圈子中提出他的觀點。
直到1859年《物種起源》出版，他的思想才得以傳達給廣大讀者，引發了巨大轟動。
第一版1,250冊在出版當天即告售罄，一年內發行量達到4,250冊，在獲得科學界讚譽的同時，也遭到宗教界和保守勢力的強烈批評。
時至今日，《物種起源》仍是人類歷史上最重要的著作之一，也是少數在出版逾150年後依然具有科學價值的作品之一。
達爾文深知自己的研究不過是一個開端。
他在書中寫道：「在遙遠的未來，我看見一片廣闊的天地，等待著更為重要的研究去探索。」

英文原文

In 1837, at the age of 28, Darwin wrote “species change” in one of his notebooks, which was the earliest record of his evolutionary ideas . Prior to this, he had sailed around the world for 5 years on the HMS Beagle, observing numerous signs that species were not fixed in South America, Oceania, and other places. After returning to England, he wrote “cuidado” (meaning “be careful” in Spanish) in another notebook, realizing that the theory of evolution was a radical and dangerous view, and that there was insufficient evidence to make it public at that time. Over the next 20 years, Darwin continuously accumulated a vast amount of data and first presented his views to a small circle of scientists. It was not until 1859, when On the Origin of Species was published, that his ideas became accessible to the general readership, causing a great sensation . The first edition of 1,250 copies sold out on the day of publication, and the circulation reached 4,250 copies within a year, receiving both praise from the scientific community and fierce criticism from the religious community and conservative forces . To this day, On the Origin of Species remains one of the most important works in human history, and one of the few works that still has scientific value more than 150 years after its publication . Darwin was well aware that his work was only the beginning . He wrote in the book: “In the distant future, I see open fields for far more important research.”

紅字句（原文）
#原文
1In 1837, at the age of 28, Darwin wrote “species change” in one of his notebooks, which was the earliest record of his evolutionary ideas .
2It was not until 1859, when On the Origin of Species was published, that his ideas became accessible to the general readership, causing a great sensation . The first edition of 1,250 copies sold out on the day of publication, and the circulation reached 4,250 copies within a year, receiving both praise from the scientific community and fierce criticism from the religious community and conservative forces . To this day, On the Origin of Species remains one of the most important works in human history, and one of the few works that still has scientific value more than 150 years after its publication . Darwin was well aware that his work was only the beginning .
#179 Changing Commuting (通勤變化) #060179 原文
中文翻譯

西雅圖一直是美國成長最快速的城市之一，這在很大程度上歸因於亞馬遜雇用了 35,000 名員工。
然而，這種成長在帶來經濟效益的同時，也衍生了城市治理的難題，尤其是就業機會的增加吸引了更多人口湧入城市，對住房、基礎設施與交通運輸造成了更大的壓力。
因此，交通擁堵日益惡化，成為西雅圖快速擴張所帶來的最顯著挑戰之一。
然而，問題不僅在於車輛數量，還在於人們選擇通勤的方式。
部分受到該地區大型雇主及職場模式轉變的影響，單人駕車的比例呈現下降趨勢，而其他通勤方式則出現了顯著的變化。
在調查中，搭乘公車和火車的比例從 46% 下降至 22%，而步行、騎車、自行開車及居家辦公則在日常出行中各自佔據了不同的比重。
儘管這些統計數據有助於說明人們如何穿越西雅圖擁擠的市中心，但它們可能並不完整，因為並未單獨統計 Uber 等叫車服務的使用情況。

英文原文

Seattle has been one of the fastest-growing cities in the US, due largely to Amazon hiring 35,000 employees . But while that growth has brought economic benefits, it has also created civic headaches, especially as rising employment has drawn more people into the city and placed greater pressure on housing, infrastructure and transportation . As a result, traffic congestion has worsened, becoming one of the most obvious challenges associated with Seattle's rapid expansion . The problem, however, is not only the number of cars, but also the way people choose to commute. Thanks in part to the region's largest employers and changing workplace patterns, solo driving has followed a downward trend, while other forms of commuting have shifted sharply . In the survey, buses and trains decreased from 46% to 22%, while walking, cycling, driving and working from home accounted for changing shares of daily travel. Although these statistics help explain how people move through Seattle's crowded downtown, they may be incomplete because they do not separately count ride-hailing services such as Uber.

紅字句（原文）
#原文
1Seattle has been one of the fastest-growing cities in the US, due largely to Amazon hiring 35,000 employees . But while that growth has brought economic benefits, it has also created civic headaches, especially as rising employment has drawn more people into the city and placed greater pressure on housing, infrastructure and transportation . As a result, traffic congestion has worsened, becoming one of the most obvious challenges associated with Seattle's rapid expansion .
2Thanks in part to the region's largest employers and changing workplace patterns, solo driving has followed a downward trend, while other forms of commuting have shifted sharply .
